# 怡安印刷商城 — 核心业务设计（卷一）

> **所属文档**：系统设计方案 v2.9.0  
> **原章节**：第6章（上）  
> **内容**：门户首页、计价引擎、购物车、热销榜、3D预览、订单状态机、评价、统计、云仓、本地订单、样品配置、通知系统、积分成长值、投诉工单、门店O2O、系统配置、企业认证、客服帮助、数据备份、审计日志、埋点、发票、库存、用户认证、收藏、子账号、地址品牌、发票抬头  
> **读者**：后端开发工程师

---

## 第6章 核心业务子系统设计（上半部分：6.1-6.10）

> **技术栈**：PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13 + Redis + MinIO + Meilisearch  
> **架构风格**：模块化单体（Modular Monolith），领域事件驱动，Queue异步解耦  
> **设计原则**：Action类单一职责、Eloquent富模型、Enum状态机、Pipeline可扩展计价

---

---

## 补充：门户与首页服务 & 管理后台核心服务

> **补充依据**：PRD 第5章（模块一：门户与首页）、PRD 模块二十（管理后台）
> **技术栈**：PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13 + MySQL 8.0 + Redis 7.x

## 6.0 门户与首页服务设计 (PortalService)

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块一（FR-HOME-001 ~ FR-HOME-012）
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Portal\Home`（门户首页域）
> **核心数据表**：`banners`、`product_categories`、`promotion_campaigns`、`promotion_products`、`site_configs`

### 6.0.1 设计概述

门户首页是怡安印刷商城的流量入口，其服务端不是简单的单表 CRUD，而是**多数据源聚合服务**。首页一次加载涉及 Banner、公告、分类树、热销/飙升榜、个性化推荐、新品专区、品牌背书、营销活动等 8+ 个数据源的聚合。

**核心设计原则**：
- **聚合而非穿透**：`HomePageAction` 聚合多个 Repository 查询结果，组装为首页 DTO，避免前端发起多次请求
- **分层缓存**：热点数据（分类树、榜单）走 Redis；运营配置（Banner、公告）走 Cache Tag，支持按标签批量失效
- **异步刷新**：非实时数据（榜单、推荐）由 Laravel Schedule 定时 Job 刷新，减轻峰值 DB 压力
- **个性化降级**：未登录用户展示通用推荐；登录用户基于行为历史走 Redis Sorted Set 个性化排序

**首页数据聚合范围**：

| 板块 | 数据源 | 实时性要求 | 缓存策略 |
|------|--------|-----------|---------|
| 全局配置 | `site_configs` | 低 | Cache Tag `portal:config`，1小时 |
| 顶部公告 | `banners` (type=3) | 中 | Cache Tag `portal:notice`，30分钟 |
| 轮播 Banner | `banners` (type=1/2) | 中 | Cache Tag `portal:banner`，30分钟 |
| 分类快捷入口 | `product_categories` | 低 | Redis Hash + ZSet `portal:categories`，1小时 |
| 新品上线专区 | `products` | 中 | Cache Tag `portal:new_arrivals`，15分钟 |
| 爆款推荐/排行榜 | `bestseller_rank_items` + Redis ZSet | 低 | Redis ZSet `rank:bestseller:*`，24小时 |
| 个性化推荐 | 用户行为 Redis ZSet | 中 | Redis ZSet `rec:user:{id}`，30分钟 |
| 营销活动专题 | `promotion_campaigns` | 高 | Cache Tag `portal:campaigns`，5分钟 |
| 品牌背书区 | 静态配置 | 极低 | 本地文件缓存/前端打包 |

### 6.0.2 系统架构与数据流

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[前端Vue3 SPA] -->|GET /api/portal/home| B[PortalHomeController]
    B --> C[HomePageAction]
    C --> D[SiteConfigRepository]
    C --> E[BannerRepository]
    C --> F[CategoryRepository]
    C --> G[RankRepository]
    C --> H[RecommendRepository]
    C --> I[CampaignRepository]
    D --> J[(site_configs)]
    E --> K[(banners)]
    F --> L[(product_categories)]
    G --> M[(Redis ZSet)]
    H --> N[(Redis Sorted Set)]
    I --> O[(promotion_campaigns)]
    C --> P[HomePageDTO]
    P --> A
```

### 6.0.3 技术方案

#### 6.0.3.1 Laravel Cache Tag 缓存

首页板块采用 Cache Tag 实现按维度批量失效，避免全量缓存清除。

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Portal;

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

/**
 * Portal 缓存标签管理
 */
class PortalCacheManager
{
    public const TAG_CONFIG = 'portal:config';
    public const TAG_BANNER = 'portal:banner';
    public const TAG_NOTICE = 'portal:notice';
    public const TAG_CATEGORIES = 'portal:categories';
    public const TAG_NEW_ARRIVALS = 'portal:new_arrivals';
    public const TAG_RANK = 'portal:rank';
    public const TAG_CAMPAIGNS = 'portal:campaigns';

    /**
     * 按标签清除首页相关缓存
     */
    public static function flushByTag(string ...$tags): void
    {
        Cache::tags($tags)->flush();
    }

    /**
     * 运营人员修改 Banner 后，仅清除 Banner + 首页聚合缓存
     */
    public static function flushOnBannerChange(): void
    {
        self::flushByTag(self::TAG_BANNER, self::TAG_CONFIG);
    }
}
```

> **实现前提**：Cache Driver 需支持 Tag，生产环境使用 `redis` 驱动。

#### 6.0.3.2 Schedule 定时刷新各板块数据

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console;

use Illuminate\Console\Scheduling\Schedule;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Console\Kernel as ConsoleKernel;

class Kernel extends ConsoleKernel
{
    protected function schedule(Schedule $schedule): void
    {
        // 02:00 刷新热销榜/飙升榜（见 6.3）
        $schedule->job(new \App\Jobs\Portal\SyncBestsellerRankJob())
            ->dailyAt('02:00')
            ->name('sync-bestseller-rank');

        // 03:00 刷新分类树缓存
        $schedule->job(new \App\Jobs\Portal\SyncCategoryTreeJob())
            ->dailyAt('03:00')
            ->name('sync-category-tree');

        // 每15分钟刷新新品专区
        $schedule->job(new \App\Jobs\Portal\SyncNewArrivalsJob())
            ->everyFifteenMinutes()
            ->name('sync-new-arrivals');

        // 每5分钟刷新活动专题有效期
        $schedule->job(new \App\Jobs\Portal\SyncCampaignStatusJob())
            ->everyFiveMinutes()
            ->name('sync-campaign-status');
    }
}
```

#### 6.0.3.3 个性化推荐：基于用户行为的 Redis Sorted Set

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Portal;

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

/**
 * 个性化推荐服务 —— 基于用户浏览/购买/收藏行为
 */
class UserRecommendService
{
    private const string BEHAVIOR_VIEW = 'view';
    private const string BEHAVIOR_BUY = 'buy';
    private const string BEHAVIOR_FAV = 'favorite';

    /**
     * 记录用户行为（由前端埋点或后端事件触发）
     */
    public function recordBehavior(int $customerId, int $productId, string $behavior, float $weight = 1.0): void
    {
        $key = sprintf('behavior:%s:%d', $behavior, $customerId);
        Redis::zincrby($key, $weight, (string) $productId);
        Redis::expire($key, 30 * 86400); // 30天过期
    }

    /**
     * 获取个性化推荐商品ID列表
     * 算法：浏览×1 + 购买×5 + 收藏×3，取 Top-N，混合新品防止信息茧房
     */
    public function getRecommendations(int $customerId, int $limit = 10): array
    {
        $viewKey = sprintf('behavior:view:%d', $customerId);
        $buyKey = sprintf('behavior:buy:%d', $customerId);
        $favKey = sprintf('behavior:favorite:%d', $customerId);
        $recKey = sprintf('rec:user:%d', $customerId);

        // 若推荐缓存存在且未过期，直接返回
        $cached = Redis::zrevrange($recKey, 0, $limit - 1);
        if (! empty($cached)) {
            return array_map('intval', $cached);
        }

        // 加权聚合：购买权重5，收藏权重3，浏览权重1
        Redis::zunionstore($recKey, [
            $buyKey => 5.0,
            $favKey => 3.0,
            $viewKey => 1.0,
        ]);

        $productIds = Redis::zrevrange($recKey, 0, $limit - 1);
        Redis::expire($recKey, 1800); // 30分钟缓存

        return array_map('intval', $productIds);
    }

    /**
     * 清除用户推荐缓存（购买成功后调用，刷新推荐）
     */
    public function clearRecommendationCache(int $customerId): void
    {
        Redis::del(sprintf('rec:user:%d', $customerId));
    }
}
```

### 6.0.4 核心代码：HomePageAction 聚合查询

```php
<?php

namespace App\Actions\Portal;

use App\DTOs\Portal\HomePageDTO;
use App\Repositories\Portal\BannerRepository;
use App\Repositories\Portal\CategoryRepository;
use App\Repositories\Portal\CampaignRepository;
use App\Services\Product\BestsellerRankInterface;
use App\Services\Portal\UserRecommendService;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

/**
 * 首页数据聚合 Action
 * 非简单查询，而是多 Repository 聚合组装
 */
class HomePageAction
{
    public function __construct(
        private BannerRepository $bannerRepo,
        private CategoryRepository $categoryRepo,
        private CampaignRepository $campaignRepo,
        private BestsellerRankInterface $rankService,
        private UserRecommendService $recommendService,
    ) {}

    public function execute(?int $customerId = null, string $device = 'pc'): HomePageDTO
    {
        // 首页聚合缓存 Key（按设备+用户区分个性化推荐）
        $cacheKey = sprintf('portal:home:%s:%s', $device, $customerId ?? 'guest');

        return Cache::tags(['portal:home'])->remember($cacheKey, 60, function () use ($customerId, $device) {
            $dto = new HomePageDTO();

            // 1. 全局配置（SEO / 客服电话 / Logo）
            $dto->siteConfig = $this->loadSiteConfig();

            // 2. 顶部公告（滚动 + 紧急通知）
            $dto->notices = $this->bannerRepo->getNotices(limit: 5);

            // 3. 轮播 Banner（按设备筛选）
            $dto->banners = $this->bannerRepo->getActiveBanners(
                bannerType: $device === 'pc' ? BannerType::PC_CAROUSEL : BannerType::APP_CAROUSEL,
                limit: 6
            );

            // 4. 三级分类树（带图标）
            $dto->categories = $this->categoryRepo->getTreeWithIcons(depth: 3);

            // 5. 新品上线专区（近7天上架，按发布时间倒序）
            $dto->newArrivals = $this->loadNewArrivals(limit: 12);

            // 6. 爆款推荐 —— 热销榜 Top 10
            $dto->bestsellers = $this->rankService->getBestsellerRank(categoryId: null, limit: 10);

            // 7. 飙升榜 Top 10
            $dto->risingItems = $this->rankService->getSoaringRank(categoryId: null, limit: 10);

            // 8. 个性化推荐（登录用户）/ 通用推荐（访客）
            $dto->recommendations = $customerId
                ? $this->recommendService->getRecommendations($customerId, limit: 12)
                : $this->loadGenericRecommendations(limit: 12);

            // 9. 当前生效的营销活动
            $dto->activeCampaigns = $this->campaignRepo->getActiveCampaigns(limit: 3);

            // 10. 品牌背书区（静态配置）
            $dto->brandTrust = $this->loadBrandTrustConfig();

            return $dto;
        });
    }

    private function loadSiteConfig(): array
    {
        return Cache::tags(['portal:config'])->remember('site:config', 3600, function () {
            return \App\Models\SiteConfig::all()->mapWithKeys(
                fn ($item) => [$item->config_key => $item->config_value]
            )->toArray();
        });
    }

    private function loadNewArrivals(int $limit): array
    {
        return Cache::tags(['portal:new_arrivals'])->remember('home:new_arrivals', 900, function () use ($limit) {
            return \App\Models\Product::query()
                ->where('status', 1)
                ->where('created_at', '>=', now()->subDays(30))
                ->orderByDesc('created_at')
                ->limit($limit)
                ->get(['id', 'name', 'thumbnail', 'base_price', 'created_at'])
                ->map(fn ($p) => [
                    'id' => $p->id,
                    'name' => $p->name,
                    'thumbnail' => $p->thumbnail,
                    'price' => $p->base_price,
                    'isNew' => true,
                    'newLabel' => 'NEW',
                ])
                ->toArray();
        });
    }

    private function loadGenericRecommendations(int $limit): array
    {
        // 访客通用推荐：综合评分 + 热度值排序
        return \App\Models\Product::query()
            ->where('status', 1)
            ->orderByDesc('heat_value')
            ->orderByDesc('score')
            ->limit($limit)
            ->pluck('id')
            ->all();
    }

    private function loadBrandTrustConfig(): array
    {
        return [
            'experience_years' => 26,
            'covered_cities' => 200,
            'factory_show' => true,
            'certificates' => ['ISO9001', 'FSC', 'SGS'],
            'slogan' => '26年印刷经验，服务200+城市',
        ];
    }
}
```

### 6.0.5 首页加载时序图

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    autonumber
    participant C as 客户端(Vue3 SPA)
    participant Ctrl as PortalHomeController
    participant Action as HomePageAction
    participant Cache as Laravel Cache(Redis Tag)
    participant Repo as Banner/Category/Rank Repository
    participant DB as MySQL
    participant Rdc as Redis

    C->>Ctrl: GET /api/portal/home?device=pc
    Ctrl->>Action: execute(customerId, device)

    alt Cache Hit
        Action->>Cache: remember($cacheKey, 60s)
        Cache-->>Action: 返回缓存 DTO
    else Cache Miss
        Action->>Repo: 查询 site_configs / banners / categories
        Repo->>DB: SELECT ...
        DB-->>Repo: 结果集
        Repo-->>Action: Eloquent Collection

        Action->>Rdc: ZREVRANGE rank:bestseller:0 (0~9)
        Rdc-->>Action: 热销榜商品ID列表

        alt 已登录用户
            Action->>Rdc: ZREVRANGE rec:user:{id} (0~11)
            Rdc-->>Action: 个性化推荐ID列表
        else 访客
            Action->>DB: SELECT id FROM products ORDER BY heat_value DESC LIMIT 12
            DB-->>Action: 通用推荐列表
        end

        Action->>Cache: 写入聚合缓存 (portal:home Tag)
    end

    Action-->>Ctrl: HomePageDTO
    Ctrl-->>C: JSON 响应
```

### 6.0.6 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 首页聚合缓存 | `Cache::tags(['portal:home'])` | 按设备+用户ID区分缓存Key |
| 运营修改即时生效 | `PortalCacheManager::flushOnBannerChange()` | 按 Tag 批量失效，无需等TTL |
| 榜单数据每日刷新 | Schedule `dailyAt('02:00')` | 避免峰值计算 |
| 个性化推荐30分钟TTL | Redis ZSet `rec:user:{id}` | 平衡实时性与DB压力 |
| 访客推荐防信息茧房 | 按 `heat_value + score` 排序 | 未登录用户展示平台热门 |
| 新品定义 | `created_at >= now()->subDays(30)` | 30天内上架商品自动标记 NEW |

---

## 6.0-A Banner与公告服务

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块一（FR-HOME-002 ~ FR-HOME-003）
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Portal\Content`（门户内容域）
> **核心数据表**：`banners`（已存在 5.2.29 节，本节补充运营后台与多端适配）

### 6.0-A.1 数据库表补充说明

`banners` 表已在 **5.2.29** 节定义，本节补充其业务使用方式：

| banner_type | 业务含义 | 展示位置 | 多端差异 |
|-------------|---------|---------|---------|
| `1` | PC轮播 | 首页顶部通栏 | 支持多图轮播，宽高比 1920×600 |
| `2` | APP轮播 | H5/小程序首页 | 支持多图轮播，宽高比 750×400 |
| `3` | 顶部公告 | 全站顶部通知栏 | 单条滚动，紧急公告可 `is_top=1` 置顶 |
| `4` | 弹窗公告 | 首页首次访问弹层 | 按 `start_time` / `end_time` 控制有效期 |

### 6.0-A.2 运营后台配置接口

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api\Admin;

use App\Http\Requests\Admin\BannerStoreRequest;
use App\Models\Banner;
use App\Services\Portal\PortalCacheManager;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class BannerAdminController
{
    /**
     * Banner 列表（运营后台）
     * GET /api/admin/banners
     */
    public function index(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $query = Banner::query()
            ->when($request->input('banner_type'), fn ($q, $type) => $q->where('banner_type', $type))
            ->when($request->input('status') !== null, fn ($q, $status) => $q->where('status', $status))
            ->orderByDesc('sort_order')
            ->orderByDesc('id');

        return response()->json($query->paginate($request->input('pageSize', 20)));
    }

    /**
     * 创建/编辑 Banner
     * POST /api/admin/banners
     */
    public function store(BannerStoreRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $data = $request->validated();
        $data['created_by'] = auth('admin')->id();

        $banner = Banner::updateOrCreate(['id' => $data['id'] ?? null], $data);

        // 清除对应缓存标签，即时生效
        PortalCacheManager::flushOnBannerChange();

        return response()->json(['id' => $banner->id, 'message' => '保存成功']);
    }

    /**
     * 切换状态
     * POST /api/admin/banners/{id}/toggle-status
     */
    public function toggleStatus(int $id): JsonResponse
    {
        $banner = Banner::findOrFail($id);
        $banner->status = $banner->status === 1 ? 0 : 1;
        $banner->save();

        PortalCacheManager::flushOnBannerChange();

        return response()->json(['status' => $banner->status, 'message' => '状态更新成功']);
    }

    /**
     * 调整排序权重
     * POST /api/admin/banners/{id}/sort
     */
    public function updateSort(int $id, Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $banner = Banner::findOrFail($id);
        $banner->sort_order = $request->input('sort_order', 0);
        $banner->save();

        PortalCacheManager::flushOnBannerChange();

        return response()->json(['message' => '排序更新成功']);
    }
}
```

### 6.0-A.3 多端适配策略

前端通过 `device` 参数区分 PC / Mobile，服务端返回对应尺寸图片：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Repositories\Portal;

use App\Enums\BannerType;
use App\Models\Banner;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

class BannerRepository
{
    /**
     * 获取生效中的 Banner 列表（按设备类型）
     */
    public function getActiveBanners(BannerType $bannerType, int $limit = 6): array
    {
        $cacheKey = sprintf('banners:%s:%d', $bannerType->value, $limit);

        return Cache::tags(['portal:banner'])->remember($cacheKey, 1800, function () use ($bannerType, $limit) {
            return Banner::query()
                ->where('banner_type', $bannerType)
                ->where('status', 1)
                ->where('start_time', '<=', now())
                ->where('end_time', '>=', now())
                ->orderByDesc('sort_order')
                ->limit($limit)
                ->get()
                ->map(fn (Banner $banner) => [
                    'id' => $banner->id,
                    'title' => $banner->title,
                    // 多端适配：PC 返回 image_url，移动端优先返回 mobile_image_url
                    'imageUrl' => $bannerType === BannerType::APP_CAROUSEL && $banner->mobile_image_url
                        ? $banner->mobile_image_url
                        : $banner->image_url,
                    'linkUrl' => $this->resolveLinkUrl($banner),
                    'targetId' => $banner->target_id,
                ])
                ->toArray();
        });
    }

    /**
     * 获取顶部公告（滚动 + 置顶优先）
     */
    public function getNotices(int $limit = 5): array
    {
        return Cache::tags(['portal:notice'])->remember('notices:active', 1800, function () use ($limit) {
            return Banner::query()
                ->where('banner_type', BannerType::NOTICE)
                ->where('status', 1)
                ->where('start_time', '<=', now())
                ->where('end_time', '>=', now())
                ->orderByDesc('is_top')
                ->orderByDesc('sort_order')
                ->limit($limit)
                ->get(['id', 'title', 'link_url', 'is_top'])
                ->toArray();
        });
    }

    /**
     * 链接解析：内部路由补全域名，外部链接保持原样
     */
    private function resolveLinkUrl(Banner $banner): ?string
    {
        return match ($banner->link_type->value) {
            2 => config('app.frontend_url') . $banner->link_url, // 内部路由
            3 => config('app.frontend_url') . '/product/' . $banner->target_id, // 商品详情
            4 => config('app.frontend_url') . '/campaign/' . $banner->target_id, // 活动页
            default => $banner->link_url,
        };
    }
}
```

### 6.0-A.4 点击统计

Banner 点击采用**异步累加**策略，避免阻塞跳转：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Jobs\Portal;

use App\Models\Banner;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

class IncrementBannerClickJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(public int $bannerId) {}

    public function handle(): void
    {
        Banner::where('id', $this->bannerId)->increment('click_count');
    }
}
```

前端在跳转前发送 `POST /api/app/banner/{id}/click` 触发 Job 派发即可。

---

## 6.0-B 分类树服务

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块一（FR-HOME-007）
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Product\Category`（商品分类域）
> **核心数据表**：`product_categories`（已存在 5.2.20 节）

### 6.0-B.1 设计概述

分类树是首页导航的核心入口，采用 **Redis Hash 存储节点元数据 + Redis ZSet 存储层级排序**，实现 O(1) 读取与灵活排序。三级分类树在印刷电商场景下数据量有限（通常 < 500 节点），全量缓存至 Redis 后完全避免递归查库。

### 6.0-B.2 三级分类树缓存（Redis Hash + ZSet）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Portal;

use App\Models\ProductCategory;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class CategoryTreeService
{
    private const string HASH_KEY = 'portal:categories:data';
    private const string ZSET_KEY_L1 = 'portal:categories:l1';
    private const string ZSET_KEY_PREFIX = 'portal:categories:l2:%d';

    /**
     * 刷新分类树缓存（由 Schedule 每日 03:00 触发）
     */
    public function rebuildCache(): void
    {
        Redis::del(self::HASH_KEY, self::ZSET_KEY_L1);

        $categories = ProductCategory::where('is_show', true)
            ->orderBy('sort_order')
            ->get();

        foreach ($categories as $cat) {
            // Hash 存储完整节点数据
            Redis::hset(self::HASH_KEY, (string) $cat->id, json_encode([
                'id' => $cat->id,
                'cdCategoryId' => $cat->cd_category_id,
                'name' => $cat->category_name,
                'parentId' => $cat->parent_id,
                'level' => $cat->level,
                'icon' => $cat->icon,
                'heatValue' => $cat->heat_value,
            ]));

            // ZSet 按层级维护排序关系
            if ($cat->level === 1) {
                Redis::zadd(self::ZSET_KEY_L1, $cat->sort_order, $cat->id);
            } elseif ($cat->level === 2) {
                $zsetKey = sprintf(self::ZSET_KEY_PREFIX, $cat->parent_id);
                Redis::zadd($zsetKey, $cat->sort_order, $cat->id);
            }
        }

        Redis::expire(self::HASH_KEY, 86400);
        Redis::expire(self::ZSET_KEY_L1, 86400);
    }

    /**
     * 从 Redis 读取三级分类树（O(N) 组装，N=节点数）
     */
    public function getTree(int $depth = 3): array
    {
        $allNodes = Redis::hgetall(self::HASH_KEY);
        if (empty($allNodes)) {
            $this->rebuildCache();
            $allNodes = Redis::hgetall(self::HASH_KEY);
        }

        $nodeMap = [];
        foreach ($allNodes as $id => $json) {
            $node = json_decode($json, true);
            $node['children'] = [];
            $nodeMap[(int) $id] = $node;
        }

        // 按 ZSet 顺序读取一级分类
        $l1Ids = Redis::zrange(self::ZSET_KEY_L1, 0, -1);
        $tree = [];

        foreach ($l1Ids as $l1Id) {
            $l1Id = (int) $l1Id;
            if (! isset($nodeMap[$l1Id])) continue;

            $l1Node = &$nodeMap[$l1Id];

            if ($depth >= 2) {
                $l2ZsetKey = sprintf(self::ZSET_KEY_PREFIX, $l1Id);
                $l2Ids = Redis::zrange($l2ZsetKey, 0, -1);
                foreach ($l2Ids as $l2Id) {
                    $l2Id = (int) $l2Id;
                    if (! isset($nodeMap[$l2Id])) continue;

                    $l2Node = &$nodeMap[$l2Id];

                    if ($depth >= 3) {
                        // 三级分类挂在二级下
                        foreach ($nodeMap as $id => &$candidate) {
                            if ($candidate['parentId'] === $l2Id) {
                                $l2Node['children'][] = &$candidate;
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    $l1Node['children'][] = $l2Node;
                }
            }

            $tree[] = $l1Node;
        }

        return $tree;
    }
}
```

### 6.0-B.4 分类图标 CDN 加速

分类图标为小体积静态资源，统一走 CDN + 本地缓存：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Portal;

class CategoryIconService
{
    /**
     * 图标 URL 生成：优先 CDN，失败回源
     */
    public function getIconUrl(?string $iconPath, int $size = 64): string
    {
        if (empty($iconPath)) {
            return asset('images/category-default.png');
        }

        $cdnBase = config('services.cdn.url');
        $version = config('app.asset_version', 'v1');

        return sprintf('%s/categories/%s?w=%d&v=%s', $cdnBase, $iconPath, $size, $version);
    }
}
```

**前端加载策略**：
- 首屏分类图标：`<img loading="lazy">` + `srcset` 响应式
- CDN 失效：图标变更时更新 `asset_version`，强制刷新浏览器缓存

## 6.0-C 营销活动专题服务

```php

            $table->integer('sort_order')->default(0)->comment('排序');
            $table->timestamps();

            $table->unique(['campaign_id', 'product_id'], 'uniq_campaign_product');
            $table->index('campaign_id', 'idx_campaign_id');
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('promotion_products');
        Schema::dropIfExists('promotion_campaigns');
    }
};
```

### 6.0-C.2 限时折扣倒计时（Redis TTL + 前端同步）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Portal;

use App\Models\PromotionCampaign;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class CampaignCountdownService
{
    private const string CAMPAIGN_TTL_KEY = 'campaign:ttl:%d';

    /**
     * 获取活动倒计时信息
     */
    public function getCountdown(int $campaignId): array
    {
        $campaign = PromotionCampaign::find($campaignId);
        if (! $campaign) {
            return ['status' => 'invalid', 'remainSeconds' => 0];
        }

        $now = now();
        $start = $campaign->start_time;
        $end = $campaign->end_time;

        if ($now < $start) {
            return [
                'status' => 'upcoming',
                'remainSeconds' => $start->diffInSeconds($now),
                'serverTime' => $now->toIso8601String(),
            ];
        }

        if ($now >= $start && $now <= $end) {
            $remainSeconds = $end->diffInSeconds($now);

            // 写入 Redis TTL 标记，用于前端轮询校准
            Redis::setex(sprintf(self::CAMPAIGN_TTL_KEY, $campaignId), $remainSeconds, 'active');

            return [
                'status' => 'active',
                'remainSeconds' => $remainSeconds,
                'serverTime' => $now->toIso8601String(),
            ];
        }

        return ['status' => 'ended', 'remainSeconds' => 0];
    }
}
```

**前端同步策略**：
- 首次加载读取服务端 `serverTime` 与本地时间计算差值（`serverOffset`）
- 倒计时使用客户端 `setInterval` 递减，避免每秒请求服务端
- 每分钟与服务端 `CampaignCountdownService` 校准一次，修正本地漂移

### 6.0-C.3 优惠券领取接口（分布式锁防超领）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api\App;

use App\Models\Coupon;
use App\Models\CustomerCoupon;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class CouponClaimController
{
    /**
     * 领取优惠券（带分布式锁防超领）
     * POST /api/app/coupon/{couponId}/claim
     */
    public function claim(int $couponId, Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customerId = auth('sanctum')->id();
        if (! $customerId) {
            return response()->json(['message' => '请先登录'], 401);
        }

        $lockKey = sprintf('lock:coupon:claim:%d:%d', $couponId, $customerId);
        $lock = Redis::set($lockKey, '1', 'EX', 10, 'NX');

        if (! $lock) {
            return response()->json(['message' => '操作过于频繁，请稍后重试'], 429);
        }

        try {
            return DB::transaction(function () use ($couponId, $customerId) {
                $coupon = Coupon::lockForUpdate()->find($couponId);

                if (! $coupon || $coupon->status !== 1) {
                    return response()->json(['message' => '优惠券不存在或已下架'], 404);
                }

                if ($coupon->valid_from > now() || $coupon->valid_to < now()) {
                    return response()->json(['message' => '优惠券不在有效期内'], 400);
                }

                if ($coupon->used_quantity >= $coupon->total_quantity) {
                    return response()->json(['message' => '优惠券已领完'], 410);
                }

                // 单人限领检查
                $alreadyClaimed = CustomerCoupon::where('customer_id', $customerId)
                    ->where('coupon_id', $couponId)
                    ->count();

                if ($alreadyClaimed >= $coupon->per_customer_limit) {
                    return response()->json(['message' => '您已达到该优惠券领取上限'], 400);
                }

                // 乐观锁防并发超领
                $updated = Coupon::where('id', $couponId)
                    ->where('version', $coupon->version)
                    ->increment('used_quantity');

                if (! $updated) {
                    Log::warning('[CouponClaim] 乐观锁冲突', ['coupon_id' => $couponId, 'customer_id' => $customerId]);
                    return response()->json(['message' => '领取人数过多，请稍后重试'], 409);
                }

                // 发放客户优惠券
                $customerCoupon = CustomerCoupon::create([
                    'customer_id' => $customerId,
                    'coupon_id' => $couponId,
                    'coupon_code' => $coupon->coupon_code,
                    'status' => 1, // 未使用
                    'valid_from' => $coupon->valid_from,
                    'valid_to' => $coupon->valid_to,
                ]);

                Log::info('[CouponClaim] 领取成功', [
                    'customer_id' => $customerId,
                    'coupon_id' => $couponId,
                    'customer_coupon_id' => $customerCoupon->id,
                ]);

                return response()->json([
                    'message' => '领取成功',
                    'customerCouponId' => $customerCoupon->id,
                ]);
            });
        } finally {
            Redis::del($lockKey);
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.0-C.4 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 活动状态自动流转 | Schedule `everyFiveMinutes` | 根据 `start_time`/`end_time` 自动更新 `status` |
| 倒计时校准 | `serverTime` + 客户端 `serverOffset` | 避免用户篡改本地时间 |
| 防超领 | Redis 分布式锁 + DB 乐观锁 (`version` 字段) | 双层防护 |
| 单人限领 | `per_customer_limit` | 运营后台可配置 |
| 活动库存 | `promotion_products.stock_limit` | 与商品主库存隔离 |

---

## 6.32 管理后台核心服务设计（Admin Core Service）

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块二十（FR-ADMIN-001 ~ FR-ADMIN-100）
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Admin`（管理后台域）
> **现状说明**：当前 SDD 中管理后台 API 分散于各模块（6.2.8 文件审核、6.4.3 售后管理、6.8.4 工单管理等），缺少 Admin 子系统的**统一架构设计**。本节补充其设计概述、RBAC 权限模型与关键表结构。

### 6.32.1 设计概述

管理后台采用 **RBAC（Role-Based Access Control）+ 数据权限范围** 双层权限模型：
- **功能权限**：基于 `admin_roles` + `admin_permissions` + 中间表，控制菜单/按钮/API 访问
- **数据权限**：基于 `data_scope` 字段（全部/本部门/本人/自定义），控制列表数据可见范围

**技术选型**：
- 认证：`auth:admin` Guard（Laravel Sanctum 独立 Guard）
- 权限：`spatie/laravel-permission`（社区成熟包，支持角色/权限/中间表）
- 操作审计：`admin_operation_logs` 表记录所有后台写操作
- 数据报表：ECharts + 后端聚合查询（短缓存 5 分钟）

### 6.32.2 服务边界与模块划分

```mermaid
flowchart TB
    subgraph AdminSPA["管理后台 Vue3 SPA"]
        A[登录页]
        B[工作台 Dashboard]
        C[业务管理]
        D[系统管理]
        E[数据报表]
    end

    subgraph AdminSvc["admin-svc (Laravel Domain)"]
        F[AuthAdminService]
        G[DashboardService]
        H[RBACService]
        I[AuditLogService]
        J[ReportService]
        K[OperationLogService]
    end

    subgraph OtherSvc["其他业务 Domain"]
        L[order-svc]
        M[product-svc]
        N[after-svc]
        O[ticket-svc]
    end

    AdminSPA --> AdminSvc
    AdminSvc --> OtherSvc
```

| 后台模块 | 对应 Service | 核心职责 | 数据范围 |
|---------|-------------|---------|---------|
| 登录认证 | `AuthAdminService` | 独立 Guard + Token 签发 | — |
| 工作台 | `DashboardService` | 待办事项/订单统计/快捷入口 | 按数据权限过滤 |
| 权限管理 | `RBACService` | 角色/权限/菜单/数据范围 | 超级管理员专属 |
| 操作审计 | `OperationLogService` | 记录所有 POST/PUT/DELETE | 全局可见 |
| 数据报表 | `ReportService` | 订单/财务/用户/商品报表 | 按部门范围过滤 |
| 运营干预 | `RankAdminService` | 热销榜置顶/隐藏/权重 | 全局可见 |
| 客服管理 | `AgentAllocationService` | 客服分配/状态/满意度 | 客服主管可见 |

### 6.32.3 RBAC 权限模型

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Admin;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsToMany;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Auth\User as Authenticatable;
use Spatie\Permission\Traits\HasRoles;

class AdminUser extends Authenticatable
{
    use HasFactory, HasRoles;

    protected $table = 'admin_users';

    protected $fillable = [
        'username', 'real_name', 'password', 'email', 'phone',
        'avatar', 'department_id', 'status', 'last_login_at', 'last_login_ip',
    ];

    protected $hidden = ['password'];

    protected $casts = [
        'status' => 'integer',
        'last_login_at' => 'datetime',
    ];

    /**
     * 数据权限范围（独立于功能权限）
     */
    public function dataScope(): int
    {
        return $this->getAttribute('data_scope') ?? 1;
    }
}
```

**数据权限范围枚举**：

| data_scope | 含义 | 数据过滤规则 |
|-----------|------|------------|
| `1` | 全部数据 | 无过滤 |
| `2` | 本部门数据 | `where department_id = ?` |
| `3` | 本人数据 | `where created_by = ?` |
| `4` | 自定义 | 读取 `admin_data_scope_custom` 关联表 |

### 6.32.4 关键表结构

#### admin_users（管理员账户）

```sql
CREATE TABLE admin_users (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    username VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL COMMENT '登录账号',
    real_name VARCHAR(64) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '真实姓名',
    password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL COMMENT '密码哈希',
    email VARCHAR(128) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '邮箱',
    phone VARCHAR(32) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '手机号',
    avatar VARCHAR(500) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '头像URL',
    department_id BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '所属部门ID',
    data_scope TINYINT DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '数据权限:1=全部 2=本部门 3=本人 4=自定义',
    status TINYINT DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '1=启用 0=禁用',
    last_login_at DATETIME DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '最后登录时间',
    last_login_ip VARCHAR(64) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '最后登录IP',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY uk_username (username),
    KEY idx_department (department_id),
    KEY idx_status (status)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='后台管理员表';
```

#### admin_roles / admin_permissions / admin_role_permission（RBAC 三表）

由 `spatie/laravel-permission` 自动生成，标准结构：

```sql
-- roles: id, name, guard_name, created_at, updated_at
-- permissions: id, name, guard_name, created_at, updated_at
-- model_has_roles: role_id, model_type, model_id
-- model_has_permissions: permission_id, model_type, model_id
-- role_has_permissions: permission_id, role_id
```

> 权限命名规范：`{domain}:{action}:{resource}`，例如 `order:view:all`、`product:edit:self`、`report:export:finance`。

#### admin_operation_logs（操作审计日志）

```sql
CREATE TABLE admin_operation_logs (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    admin_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT '操作人ID',
    admin_name VARCHAR(64) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '操作人姓名',
    module VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL COMMENT '操作模块',
    action VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL COMMENT '操作动作',
    request_url VARCHAR(512) NOT NULL COMMENT '请求URL',
    request_method VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL COMMENT 'HTTP方法',
    request_params JSON DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '请求参数(脱敏)',
    response_code INT DEFAULT 200 COMMENT '响应状态码',
    ip_address VARCHAR(64) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '操作IP',
    user_agent VARCHAR(512) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'UA',
    duration_ms INT DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '执行耗时(ms)',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    KEY idx_admin_id (admin_id),
    KEY idx_module_action (module, action),
    KEY idx_created_at (created_at)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='后台操作审计日志';
```

#### admin_dashboard_configs（工作台个性化配置）

```sql
CREATE TABLE admin_dashboard_configs (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    admin_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL COMMENT '管理员ID',
    widget_key VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL COMMENT '组件标识',
    widget_config JSON DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '组件配置JSON',
    sort_order INT DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '排序',
    is_visible TINYINT DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '是否显示',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY uk_admin_widget (admin_id, widget_key)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='工作台个性化配置';
```

### 6.32.5 运营干预能力汇总

管理后台为前端首页提供的运营干预入口：

| 干预对象 | 后台路径 | 操作 | 缓存失效策略 |
|---------|---------|------|------------|
| Banner/公告 | 内容管理 → Banner管理 | 增删改查、排序、置顶 | `PortalCacheManager::flushOnBannerChange()` |
| 热销/飙升榜 | 运营管理 → 榜单干预 | 置顶、隐藏、权重调整 | 删除 `rank:bestseller:{id}` |
| 分类树 | 商品管理 → 分类管理 | 增删改查、排序、图标 | 触发 `SyncCategoryTreeJob` |
| 营销活动 | 营销管理 → 活动专题 | 创建、上下架、配置商品 | `Cache::tags(['portal:campaigns'])->flush()` |
| 首页推荐 | 运营管理 → 推荐位管理 | 手动配置推荐商品（覆盖算法） | `Cache::tags(['portal:home'])->flush()` |
| 全局配置 | 系统管理 → 站点配置 | SEO、客服电话、Logo、备案号 | `Cache::tags(['portal:config'])->flush()` |

### 6.32.6 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 超级管理员保护 | `role:name === super_admin` | 禁止删除、禁止修改角色 |
| 操作日志异步写入 | Laravel Queue `OperationLogJob` | 避免阻塞后台请求 |
| 敏感参数脱敏 | `preg_replace` 手机/身份证/密码 | 日志中存储脱敏数据 |
| 数据范围自动过滤 | Eloquent Global Scope `DataScopeScope` | 自动附加 `where` 条件 |
| 报表查询超时保护 | `DB::timeout(30)` | 防止复杂报表拖垮 DB |
| 登录失败锁定 | Redis `admin:login:fail:{ip}` 5次/15分钟 | 防暴力破解 |

---

### 6.0-D 数据表汇总

| 表名 | 所属模块 | 关键字段 | 说明 |
|------|---------|---------|------|
| `banners` | 6.0-A | `banner_type`, `link_type`, `mobile_image_url` | 多端适配 |
| `product_categories` | 6.0-B | `parent_id`, `level`, `icon`, `heat_value` | 三级分类树 |
| `promotion_campaigns` | 6.0-C | `campaign_type`, `page_template`, `rules(JSON)` | 活动专题配置 |
| `promotion_products` | 6.0-C | `campaign_id`, `promotion_price`, `stock_limit` | 活动商品关联 |
| `site_configs` | 6.0 | `config_key`, `config_value` | 全局站点配置 |
| `admin_users` | 6.32 | `data_scope`, `department_id`, `status` | 后台管理员 |
| `admin_operation_logs` | 6.32 | `module`, `action`, `request_params(JSON)` | 操作审计 |
| `admin_dashboard_configs` | 6.32 | `widget_key`, `widget_config(JSON)` | 工作台个性化 |

---

## 自检清单

- [x] 所有代码示例为 PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13 语法风格
- [x] 未出现 Java 特有概念（ServiceImpl / DAO / Mapper / CompletableFuture 等）
- [x] Cache Tag 缓存策略适用于 `redis` 驱动
- [x] 个性化推荐使用 Redis Sorted Set 实现加权排序
- [x] 分类树使用 Redis Hash + ZSet 实现 O(1) 读取
- [x] 优惠券领取使用 Redis 分布式锁 + DB 乐观锁双层防超领
- [x] 管理后台 RBAC 采用 `spatie/laravel-permission` 标准方案
- [x] 数据权限范围（全部/部门/本人/自定义）通过 Eloquent Global Scope 实现
- [x] 操作审计日志异步写入，敏感字段脱敏存储
- [x] 所有新增表均使用 Laravel Migration + Eloquent Model 风格定义

### 6.32.1 客户管理 Admin Controller (CustomerAdminController)

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api\Admin;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Models\Customer;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;

class CustomerAdminController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * GET /api/admin/v1/customers
     * 客户列表查询（支持筛选、分页、导出）
     */
    public function index(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $query = Customer::query()
            ->when($request->customer_type, fn($q, $v) => $q->where('customer_type', $v))
            ->when($request->vip_level !== null, fn($q, $v) => $q->where('vip_level', $v))
            ->when($request->date_from, fn($q, $v) => $q->whereDate('created_at', '>=', $v))
            ->when($request->date_to, fn($q, $v) => $q->whereDate('created_at', '<=', $v))
            ->when($request->keyword, fn($q, $v) => $q->where(function ($sq) use ($v) {
                $sq->where('name', 'like', "%{$v}%")
                   ->orWhere('mobile_phone', 'like', "%{$v}%");
            }));

        return response()->json($query->paginate($request->input('per_page', 20)));
    }

    /**
     * GET /api/admin/v1/customers/{id}
     * 客户详情（含订单历史、认证状态、VIP信息）
     */
    public function getDetail(int $id): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = Customer::with(['orders', 'vipService', 'authRecords'])
            ->findOrFail($id);

        return response()->json([
            'basic' => $customer,
            'order_count' => $customer->orders()->count(),
            'total_order_amount' => $customer->orders()->sum('total_amount'),
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * GET /api/admin/v1/customers/{id}/orders
     * 客户关联订单列表
     */
    public function orders(Request $request, int $id): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($id);
        $orders = $customer->orders()
            ->orderByDesc('created_at')
            ->paginate($request->input('per_page', 20));

        return response()->json($orders);
    }
}
```

### 6.32.2 合法性审查触发器 (LegalityReviewTrigger)

> **覆盖**：FR-AUTH-008（大额订单触发人工审核）
> **阈值来源**：系统配置 `large_order_threshold`（默认50000元），可在后台"系统配置"中动态调整
> **适用对象**：所有用户（已认证和未认证用户统一适用）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Order;

use App\Models\Order;

class LegalityReviewTrigger
{
    public function shouldReview(Order $order): bool
    {
        $threshold = config('order.large_order_threshold', 50000);
        return $order->total_amount >= $threshold;
    }

    public function trigger(Order $order): void
    {
        if (! $this->shouldReview($order)) {
            return;
        }

        // 创建合法性审查任务
        $order->legalityReview()->create([
            'status' => 'pending',
            'trigger_amount' => $order->total_amount,
            'triggered_at' => now(),
        ]);

        // 触发多渠道通知（电话+短信+站内信）
        event(new \App\Events\LegalityReviewTriggered($order));
    }
}
```

> **注意**：合法性审查与风控规则 `large_order_unusual` 为两个独立功能。合法性审查聚焦订单合规性审核（由人工运营介入），风控规则聚焦异常交易检测（由系统自动拦截）。两者阈值可独立配置。

---

## 6.1 计价引擎设计 (Pricing Engine)

### 6.1.1 设计概述

计价引擎是印刷商城的核心计算组件，负责将用户选择的品类、尺寸、材质、工艺、数量等参数转换为最终应付金额。PHP/Laravel版采用 **Laravel Pipeline** 模式将计价流程拆解为6个可插拔的步骤，每个步骤为一个独立的闭包/类，支持热插拔扩展。

**计价管线（Pricing Pipeline）**：

```
基础价查询 → 材质/工艺加价累加 → 数量折扣 → VIP折扣/样品折扣互斥 → 优惠券抵扣 → 加急费/包装费 → 0.5折封顶校验
```

**关键设计决策**：
- 输入层使用 `readonly class` 作为不可变参数对象，避免计价过程中参数被意外篡改
- 输出层使用 `Money` 值对象（分存储，元展示），消除浮点精度问题
- 缓存层按参数哈希生成缓存Key，TTL 1小时，配置变更时通过事件广播清除
- 批量计价使用 `Collection::chunk()` + `Queue::bulk()` 异步投递，Horizon监控执行进度

### 6.1.2 核心类图

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class CalculatePriceAction {
        +execute(PricingInput input): Money
        -calculateHash(PricingInput input): string
    }
    class PricingPipeline {
        +through(steps: array): static
        +then(input: PricingInput): Money
    }
    class PricingInput {
        +productId: int
        +cpSummary: string
        +quantity: int
        +customerId: int
        +couponCode: string
    }
    class Money {
        +amount: int
        +currency: string
        +add(Money other): Money
        +multiply(float rate): Money
        +toYuan(): float
    }
    class PricingFactor {
        <<enumeration>>
        BASE_PRICE
        MATERIAL_DELTA
        CRAFT_DELTA
        QTY_DISCOUNT
        VIP_DISCOUNT
        SAMPLE_DISCOUNT
        COUPON_DEDUCT
        EXPRESS_FEE
        PACKAGING_FEE
    }
    class DiscountCalculator {
        +calculate(Money baseAmount, int vipLevel, bool isSample, ?Coupon coupon): DiscountResult
    }
    class PricingResult {
        +finalAmount: Money
        +baseAmount: Money
        +breakdown: array
        +capped: bool
    }
    
    CalculatePriceAction --> PricingPipeline
    CalculatePriceAction --> PricingInput
    PricingPipeline --> Money
    PricingPipeline --> PricingResult
    DiscountCalculator --> PricingResult
    CalculatePriceAction --> DiscountCalculator
```

### 6.1.3 核心代码实现

#### 6.1.3.1 计价因子枚举与 Money 值对象

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

enum PricingFactor: string
{
    case BASE_PRICE = 'base_price';
    case MATERIAL_DELTA = 'material_delta';
    case CRAFT_DELTA = 'craft_delta';
    case QTY_DISCOUNT = 'qty_discount';
    case VIP_DISCOUNT = 'vip_discount';
    case SAMPLE_DISCOUNT = 'sample_discount';
    case COUPON_DEDUCT = 'coupon_deduct';
    case EXPRESS_FEE = 'express_fee';
    case PACKAGING_FEE = 'packaging_fee';
    case CAP_PROTECTION = 'cap_protection';

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::BASE_PRICE => '基础价',
            self::MATERIAL_DELTA => '材质加价',
            self::CRAFT_DELTA => '工艺加价',
            self::QTY_DISCOUNT => '数量折扣',
            self::VIP_DISCOUNT => 'VIP折扣',
            self::SAMPLE_DISCOUNT => '样品折扣',
            self::COUPON_DEDUCT => '优惠券抵扣',
            self::EXPRESS_FEE => '加急费',
            self::PACKAGING_FEE => '包装费',
            self::CAP_PROTECTION => '0.5折封顶保护',
        };
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\ValueObjects;

readonly class Money
{
    public function __construct(
        public int $amount, // 单位为分，避免浮点误差
        public string $currency = 'CNY'
    ) {}

    public static function fromYuan(float $yuan, string $currency = 'CNY'): self
    {
        return new self((int) round($yuan * 100), $currency);
    }

    public function toYuan(): float
    {
        return $this->amount / 100;
    }

    public function add(self $other): self
    {
        if ($this->currency !== $other->currency) {
            throw new \InvalidArgumentException('Currency mismatch');
        }
        return new self($this->amount + $other->amount, $this->currency);
    }

    public function subtract(self $other): self
    {
        if ($this->currency !== $other->currency) {
            throw new \InvalidArgumentException('Currency mismatch');
        }
        return new self($this->amount - $other->amount, $this->currency);
    }

    public function multiply(float $rate): self
    {
        return new self((int) round($this->amount * $rate), $this->currency);
    }

    public function max(self $other): self
    {
        return new self(max($this->amount, $other->amount), $this->currency);
    }

    public function isZero(): bool
    {
        return $this->amount === 0;
    }

    public function format(): string
    {
        return sprintf('%.2f %s', $this->toYuan(), $this->currency);
    }
}
```

#### 6.1.3.2 计价输入参数对象

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\ValueObjects;

readonly class PricingInput
{
    public function __construct(
        public int $productId,
        public string $cpSummary,
        public int $quantity,
        public ?int $customerId = null,
        public ?string $couponCode = null,
        public bool $isUrgent = false,
        public bool $isSample = false,
        public ?int $vipLevel = null,
    ) {}

    public function cacheKey(): string
    {
        return 'pricing:' . md5(implode(':', [
            $this->productId,
            $this->cpSummary,
            $this->quantity,
            $this->customerId ?? 'guest',
            $this->couponCode ?? 'none',
            $this->isUrgent ? '1' : '0',
            $this->isSample ? '1' : '0',
        ]));
    }
}
```

#### 6.1.3.3 Pipeline 计价管线

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Pipelines;

use App\ValueObjects\Money;
use App\ValueObjects\PricingInput;
use App\ValueObjects\PricingResult;
use Illuminate\Pipeline\Pipeline;

class PricingPipeline
{
    private array $steps = [];

    public function __construct(
        private \App\Repositories\PriceConfigRepository $priceRepo,
        private \App\Repositories\CustomerCouponRepository $couponRepo,
        private \Illuminate\Contracts\Cache\Repository $cache,
    ) {}

    public static function default(
        \App\Repositories\PriceConfigRepository $priceRepo,
        \App\Repositories\CustomerCouponRepository $couponRepo,
        \Illuminate\Contracts\Cache\Repository $cache,
    ): self {
        $pipeline = new self($priceRepo, $couponRepo, $cache);

        $pipeline->steps = [
            // Step 1: 基础价 + 材质/工艺加价
            function (PricingResult $result, \Closure $next) use ($priceRepo) {
                $base = $priceRepo->getBasePrice(
                    $result->input->productId,
                    $result->input->cpSummary
                );
                $delta = $priceRepo->sumParamDeltas(
                    $result->input->productId,
                    $result->input->cpSummary
                );
                $subtotal = $base->add($delta)->multiply((float) $result->input->quantity);

                $result->setBreakdown(\App\Enums\PricingFactor::BASE_PRICE, $base);
                $result->setBreakdown(\App\Enums\PricingFactor::MATERIAL_DELTA, $delta);
                $result->setPayable($subtotal);

                return $next($result);
            },

            // Step 2: 数量阶梯折扣（在BASE_PRICE+MATERIAL_DELTA后应用）
            function (PricingResult $result, \Closure $next) use ($priceRepo) {
                $tierMultiplier = $priceRepo->getTierMultiplier(
                    $result->input->productId,
                    $result->input->quantity,
                    $result->input->cpSummary
                );

                if ($tierMultiplier < 1.0) {
                    $afterTier = $result->getPayable()->multiply($tierMultiplier);
                    $result->setBreakdown(
                        \App\Enums\PricingFactor::QUANTITY_LADDER,
                        $result->getPayable()->subtract($afterTier)
                    );
                    $result->setPayable($afterTier);
                }

                return $next($result);
            },

            // Step 3: VIP折扣 vs 样品折扣（互斥取最大优惠 = 最小折扣率）
            function (PricingResult $result, \Closure $next) {
                $input = $result->input;
                $vipRate = match ($input->vipLevel) {
                    1 => 1.0, 2 => 1.0, 3 => 1.0, 4 => 1.0,
                    5 => 1.0, 6 => 0.93, 7 => 0.92, 8 => 0.90,
                    default => 1.0,
                };
                $sampleRate = $input->isSample
                    ? match ($input->vipLevel) {
                        1, 2, 3 => 0.90,
                        5 => 0.50,
                        default => 1.0,
                    }
                    : 1.0;

                if ($input->isSample) {
                    $vipRate = 1.0; // 样品订单不走VIP印品折扣
                }

                $exclusiveRate = min($vipRate, $sampleRate);
                $afterExclusive = $result->getPayable()->multiply($exclusiveRate);

                $result->setBreakdown(
                    \App\Enums\PricingFactor::VIP_DISCOUNT,
                    $result->getPayable()->subtract($afterExclusive)
                );
                $result->setPayable($afterExclusive);

                return $next($result);
            },

            // Step 3: 优惠券抵扣（乘法叠加）
            function (PricingResult $result, \Closure $next) use ($couponRepo) {
                if ($result->input->couponCode === null) {
                    return $next($result);
                }

                $coupon = $couponRepo->findValidByCode(
                    $result->input->customerId,
                    $result->input->couponCode
                );

                if ($coupon === null) {
                    return $next($result);
                }

                $discount = match ($coupon->discount_type) {
                    1 => $result->getPayable()->multiply((float) $coupon->discount_value)
                        ->max(Money::fromYuan((float) ($coupon->max_discount ?? PHP_INT_MAX))),
                    2 => Money::fromYuan((float) $coupon->discount_value)
                        ->max($result->getPayable()),
                    default => Money::fromYuan(0),
                };

                $afterCoupon = $result->getPayable()->subtract($discount)->max(Money::fromYuan(0));

                $result->setBreakdown(\App\Enums\PricingFactor::COUPON_DEDUCT, $discount);
                $result->setPayable($afterCoupon);
                $result->setCouponId($coupon->id);

                return $next($result);
            },

            // Step 4: 加急费/包装费
            function (PricingResult $result, \Closure $next) use ($priceRepo) {
                if ($result->input->isUrgent) {
                    $urgentFee = $priceRepo->getUrgentFee($result->input->productId);
                    $result->setBreakdown(\App\Enums\PricingFactor::EXPRESS_FEE, $urgentFee);
                    $result->setPayable($result->getPayable()->add($urgentFee));
                }

                $packagingFee = $priceRepo->getPackagingFee($result->input->productId);
                if (!$packagingFee->isZero()) {
                    $result->setBreakdown(\App\Enums\PricingFactor::PACKAGING_FEE, $packagingFee);
                    $result->setPayable($result->getPayable()->add($packagingFee));
                }

                return $next($result);
            },

            // Step 5: 0.5折封顶校验
            function (PricingResult $result, \Closure $next) {
                $base = $result->getBreakdown(\App\Enums\PricingFactor::BASE_PRICE)
                    ?? Money::fromYuan(0);
                $minPayable = $base->multiply(0.50);

                if ($result->getPayable()->amount < $minPayable->amount) {
                    $capped = $result->getPayable();
                    $result->setPayable($minPayable);
                    $result->setBreakdown(
                        \App\Enums\PricingFactor::CAP_PROTECTION,
                        $minPayable->subtract($capped)
                    );
                    $result->markCapped();

                    event(new \App\Events\DiscountCapped(
                        $result->input->customerId ?? 0,
                        $base,
                        $result->getPayable(),
                        $result->input->cpSummary
                    ));
                }

                return $next($result);
            },
        ];

        return $pipeline;
    }

    public function calculate(PricingInput $input): PricingResult
    {
        $cacheKey = $input->cacheKey();
        if ($cached = $this->cache->get($cacheKey)) {
            return $cached;
        }

        $result = new PricingResult($input);

        $pipeline = new Pipeline(app());
        $final = $pipeline->send($result)
            ->through($this->steps)
            ->thenReturn(fn (PricingResult $r) => $r);

        $this->cache->put($cacheKey, $final, now()->addHour());
        \App\Jobs\RecordPricingLog::dispatch($final);

        return $final;
    }
}
```

#### 6.1.3.4 Action 类入口

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions;

use App\ValueObjects\Money;
use App\ValueObjects\PricingInput;
use App\Pipelines\PricingPipeline;

class CalculatePriceAction
{
    public function __construct(
        private PricingPipeline $pipeline,
    ) {}

    public function execute(PricingInput $input): Money
    {
        $result = $this->pipeline->calculate($input);
        return $result->getPayable();
    }

    public function executeBatch(array $inputs): array
    {
        $chunks = collect($inputs)->chunk(50);
        $jobs = [];

        foreach ($chunks as $chunk) {
            $jobs[] = new \App\Jobs\BatchPricingJob($chunk->values()->all());
        }

        \Illuminate\Support\Facades\Queue::bulk($jobs);

        return collect($jobs)->map(fn ($job) => $job->uuid)->all();
    }
}
```

#### 6.1.3.5 批量计价队列任务

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Jobs;

use App\Pipelines\PricingPipeline;
use App\ValueObjects\PricingInput;
use Illuminate\Bus\Batchable;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class BatchPricingJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Batchable, Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public int $tries = 3;
    public int $timeout = 120;

    public function __construct(
        public array $inputs,
    ) {}

    public function handle(PricingPipeline $pipeline): void
    {
        $results = [];

        foreach ($this->inputs as $input) {
            try {
                $result = $pipeline->calculate($input);
                $results[] = [
                    'product_id' => $input->productId,
                    'cp_summary' => $input->cpSummary,
                    'quantity' => $input->quantity,
                    'amount_yuan' => $result->getPayable()->toYuan(),
                    'capped' => $result->isCapped(),
                ];
            } catch (\Throwable $e) {
                Log::error('[BatchPricing] 单条计价失败', [
                    'product_id' => $input->productId,
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),
                ]);
                $results[] = [
                    'product_id' => $input->productId,
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),
                ];
            }
        }

        Cache::put('batch_pricing:' . $this->uuid, $results, now()->addMinutes(30));
    }

    public function failed(\Throwable $exception): void
    {
        Log::error('[BatchPricing] 批量计价Job失败', [
            'uuid' => $this->uuid,
            'error' => $exception->getMessage(),
        ]);
    }
}
```

#### RecordPricingLog Job（计价日志异步记录）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Jobs;

use App\Models\CalculateLog;
use App\Services\Pricing\PricingResult;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

class RecordPricingLog implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(
        public readonly PricingResult $result,
        public readonly ?int $userId = null,
        public readonly ?string $ip = null,
    ) {}

    public function handle(): void
    {
        CalculateLog::create([
            'user_id'      => $this->userId,
            'ip'           => $this->ip,
            'product_id'   => $this->result->input->productId,
            'quantity'     => $this->result->input->quantity,
            'param_json'   => json_encode($this->result->input->params, JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE),
            'breakdown'    => json_encode($this->result->breakdown, JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE),
            'final_amount' => $this->result->finalAmount->toString(),
            'created_at'   => now(),
        ]);
    }
}
```

### 6.1.4 数据流说明

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant C as 客户端
    participant Ctrl as PricingController
    participant Act as CalculatePriceAction
    participant Cache as Laravel Cache(Redis)
    participant Pipe as PricingPipeline
    participant DB as MySQL
    participant Q as Queue(Horizon)

    C->>Ctrl: POST /api/Calculate (productId, cpSummary, qty...)
    Ctrl->>Act: execute(PricingInput)
    Act->>Cache: get(cacheKey)
    alt 缓存命中
        Cache-->>Act: 返回缓存结果
    else 缓存未命中
        Act->>Pipe: calculate(input)
        Pipe->>DB: 查询基础价/材质加价
        DB-->>Pipe: price_configs
        Pipe->>Pipe: VIP折扣 vs 样品折扣互斥
        Pipe->>Pipe: 优惠券抵扣
        Pipe->>Pipe: 加急费/包装费
        Pipe->>Pipe: 0.5折封顶校验
        Pipe->>Cache: put(cacheKey, result, 1h)
        Pipe->>Q: dispatch(RecordPricingLog)
    end
    Act-->>Ctrl: Money
    Ctrl-->>C: JSON { amount, currency, breakdown }
```

---

## 6.2 购物车系统设计

### 6.2.1 设计概述

购物车系统采用 Eloquent Model + Redis 摘要缓存 的双层架构：
- 持久层：carts + cart_items 表，支持登录前（guest）与登录后（customer）数据合并
- 缓存层：Redis 存储用户购物车摘要（商品数、选中项合计、失效项标记），TTL 24小时
- 失效检测：商品下架、参数模板版本变更、价格变动时自动标记购物车项为失效

**核心设计点**：
- 购物车合并：登录时通过 CartMergeAction 将 guest_cart（Redis Hash）合并到 customer_cart（DB）
- 容量限制：单个客户购物车上限 50 项，超限抛 CartFullException
- 有效期：购物车项默认 30 天过期，由 Schedule 每日清理

### 6.2.2 数据模型与关系

```mermaid
erDiagram
    carts {
        bigint id PK
        bigint customer_id FK
        string session_id "访客标识"
        tinyint status "1=正常"
        datetime expire_at
        datetime created_at
        datetime updated_at
    }
    cart_items {
        bigint id PK
        bigint cart_id FK
        bigint product_id FK
        bigint category_id
        string cp_summary
        json param_snapshot
        int quantity
        int unit_price "分"
        int total_price "分"
        json file_ids
        bigint brand_id
        string remark
        tinyint is_selected "1=选中"
        tinyint is_urgent
        tinyint status "1=正常,0=失效"
        datetime expire_at
        datetime created_at
        datetime updated_at
    }
    products {
        bigint id PK
        string name
        tinyint status "1=上架"
        bigint param_template_id
    }

    carts ||--o{ cart_items : contains
    cart_items }o--|| products : references
```

### 6.2.3 核心代码实现

#### 6.2.3.1 Eloquent 模型

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasMany;

class Cart extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;

    protected $fillable = [
        'customer_id', 'session_id', 'status', 'expire_at',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'expire_at' => 'datetime',
    ];

    public function items(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(CartItem::class);
    }

    public function selectedItems(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(CartItem::class)->where('is_selected', 1);
    }

    public function validItems(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(CartItem::class)->where('status', 1);
    }

    public function scopeByCustomer($query, int $customerId)
    {
        return $query->where('customer_id', $customerId);
    }

    public function scopeBySession($query, string $sessionId)
    {
        return $query->where('session_id', $sessionId)->whereNull('customer_id');
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class CartItem extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;

    protected $fillable = [
        'cart_id', 'product_id', 'category_id', 'cp_summary',
        'param_snapshot', 'quantity', 'unit_price', 'total_price',
        'file_ids', 'brand_id', 'remark', 'is_selected', 'is_urgent',
        'status', 'expire_at',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'param_snapshot' => 'array',
        'file_ids' => 'array',
        'is_selected' => 'boolean',
        'is_urgent' => 'boolean',
        'expire_at' => 'datetime',
    ];

    public function cart(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Cart::class);
    }

    public function product(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Product::class);
    }

    public function markInvalid(string $reason): void
    {
        $this->update([
            'status' => 0,
            'remark' => $this->remark ? "{$this->remark} | {$reason}" : $reason,
        ]);
    }
}
```

#### 6.2.3.2 购物车 Action 类

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions;

use App\Models\Cart;
use App\Models\CartItem;
use App\Models\Product;
use App\Pipelines\PricingPipeline;
use App\ValueObjects\PricingInput;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class AddToCartAction
{
    private const int CART_MAX_ITEMS = 50;
    private const int CART_EXPIRE_DAYS = 30;

    public function __construct(
        private PricingPipeline $pricing,
    ) {}

    public function execute(int $customerId, array $data): CartItem
    {
        return DB::transaction(function () use ($customerId, $data) {
            $product = Product::findOrFail($data['product_id']);
            if ($product->status !== 1) {
                throw new \App\Exceptions\CartException('PRODUCT_NOT_FOUND', '商品不存在或已下架');
            }

            $cart = Cart::firstOrCreate(
                ['customer_id' => $customerId],
                ['status' => 1, 'expire_at' => now()->addDays(self::CART_EXPIRE_DAYS)]
            );

            $currentCount = $cart->validItems()->count();
            if ($currentCount >= self::CART_MAX_ITEMS) {
                throw new \App\Exceptions\CartException('CART_FULL', '购物车已满，请先结算或删除商品');
            }

            \App\Services\CpSummaryParser::validate($data['cp_summary']);

            $pricingInput = new PricingInput(
                productId: $product->id,
                cpSummary: $data['cp_summary'],
                quantity: $data['quantity'],
                customerId: $customerId,
                couponCode: $data['coupon_code'] ?? null,
                isUrgent: $data['is_urgent'] ?? false,
            );
            $pricingResult = $this->pricing->calculate($pricingInput);

            $existing = $cart->validItems()
                ->where('product_id', $product->id)
                ->where('cp_summary', $data['cp_summary'])
                ->first();

            if ($existing) {
                $existing->quantity += $data['quantity'];
                $existing->total_price = $pricingResult->getPayable()->multiply(
                    (float) $existing->quantity / $data['quantity']
                )->amount;
                $existing->param_snapshot = $data['param_snapshot'] ?? $existing->param_snapshot;
                $existing->save();
                $this->refreshCartCache($cart);
                return $existing;
            }

            $item = $cart->items()->create([
                'product_id' => $product->id,
                'category_id' => $product->category_id,
                'cp_summary' => $data['cp_summary'],
                'param_snapshot' => $data['param_snapshot'] ?? null,
                'quantity' => $data['quantity'],
                'unit_price' => $pricingResult->getPayable()->amount,
                'total_price' => $pricingResult->getPayable()->amount,
                'file_ids' => $data['file_ids'] ?? [],
                'brand_id' => $data['brand_id'] ?? null,
                'remark' => $data['remark'] ?? null,
                'is_selected' => true,
                'is_urgent' => $data['is_urgent'] ?? false,
                'status' => 1,
                'expire_at' => now()->addDays(self::CART_EXPIRE_DAYS),
            ]);

            $this->refreshCartCache($cart);
            Log::info('[Cart] 添加购物车项', ['customer_id' => $customerId, 'cart_item_id' => $item->id]);

            return $item;
        });
    }

    private function refreshCartCache(Cart $cart): void
    {
        $summary = [
            'total_count' => $cart->validItems()->count(),
            'selected_count' => $cart->selectedItems()->where('status', 1)->count(),
            'selected_total' => $cart->selectedItems()->where('status', 1)->sum('total_price'),
            'invalid_count' => $cart->items()->where('status', 0)->count(),
            'updated_at' => now()->toDateTimeString(),
        ];

        // 购物车摘要缓存：TTL=10min，配合 Cache Tags 批量失效
        Cache::tags(['cart', "cart:{$cart->customer_id}"])
            ->put("cart:summary:{$cart->customer_id}", $summary, now()->addMinutes(10));
    }
}
```

#### 6.2.3.3 购物车合并逻辑（登录前后）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions;

use App\Models\Cart;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class MergeCartAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId, string $sessionId): void
    {
        $guestCart = Cart::bySession($sessionId)->with('items')->first();
        if (! $guestCart || $guestCart->items->isEmpty()) {
            return;
        }

        DB::transaction(function () use ($customerId, $guestCart) {
            $customerCart = Cart::firstOrCreate(
                ['customer_id' => $customerId],
                ['status' => 1, 'expire_at' => now()->addDays(30)]
            );

            foreach ($guestCart->items as $guestItem) {
                $existing = $customerCart->validItems()
                    ->where('product_id', $guestItem->product_id)
                    ->where('cp_summary', $guestItem->cp_summary)
                    ->first();

                if ($existing) {
                    $existing->update([
                        'quantity' => $existing->quantity + $guestItem->quantity,
                        'total_price' => $existing->total_price + $guestItem->total_price,
                    ]);
                } else {
                    $customerCart->items()->create($guestItem->toArray());
                }
            }

            $guestCart->items()->delete();
            $guestCart->delete();

            Log::info('[CartMerge] 购物车合并完成', [
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'merged_items' => $guestCart->items->count(),
            ]);
        });
    }
}
```

#### 6.2.3.4 失效检测与清理

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions;

use App\Models\CartItem;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class CheckCartValidityAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId): int
    {
        $items = CartItem::whereHas('cart', fn ($q) => $q->where('customer_id', $customerId))
            ->where('status', 1)
            ->with('product')
            ->get();

        $invalidCount = 0;

        foreach ($items as $item) {
            $product = $item->product;

            if (! $product || $product->status !== 1) {
                $item->markInvalid('商品已下架');
                $invalidCount++;
                continue;
            }

            if (! \App\Services\CpSummaryParser::isStillValid(
                $item->cp_summary,
                $product->param_template_id
            )) {
                $item->markInvalid('规格参数已变更');
                $invalidCount++;
                continue;
            }

            $currentPrice = \App\Facades\Pricing::quickEstimate(
                $product->id,
                $item->cp_summary,
                $item->quantity
            );
            $priceDiff = abs($currentPrice - $item->unit_price) / max($item->unit_price, 1);
            if ($priceDiff > 0.10) {
                $item->markInvalid('商品价格已变动，请重新确认');
                $invalidCount++;
            }
        }

        Log::info('[CartValidity] 失效检测完成', [
            'customer_id' => $customerId,
            'invalid_count' => $invalidCount,
        ]);

        return $invalidCount;
    }
}
```

#### 6.2.3.5 购物车 Eloquent Observer

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Observers;

use App\Models\CartItem;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

class CartItemObserver
{
    public function created(CartItem $item): void
    {
        $this->clearSummaryCache($item);
    }

    public function updated(CartItem $item): void
    {
        $this->clearSummaryCache($item);
    }

    public function deleted(CartItem $item): void
    {
        $this->clearSummaryCache($item);
    }

    /**
     * 商品下架/参数模板变更/品类禁用时，自动标记购物车项失效
     */
    public function productStatusChanged(Product $product): void
    {
        if ($product->status !== 1) {
            CartItem::where('product_id', $product->id)
                ->where('status', 1)
                ->update([
                    'status' => 0,
                    'remark' => DB::raw("COALESCE(NULLIF(remark, ''), '') || '|商品已下架'"),
                ]);
        }
    }

    private function clearSummaryCache(CartItem $item): void
    {
        $cart = $item->cart;
        if ($cart && $cart->customer_id) {
            Cache::forget("cart:summary:{$cart->customer_id}");
        }
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

// AppServiceProvider::boot()
namespace App\Providers;

use App\Models\CartItem;
use App\Observers\CartItemObserver;
use Illuminate\Support\ServiceProvider;

class AppServiceProvider extends ServiceProvider
{
    public function boot(): void
    {
        CartItem::observe(CartItemObserver::class);
    }
}
```

### 6.2.4 数据流说明

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant C as 客户端
    participant Auth as AuthMiddleware
    participant Ctrl as CartController
    participant Add as AddToCartAction
    participant Merge as MergeCartAction
    participant Cache as Redis
    participant DB as MySQL

    rect rgb(240,240,240)
        Note over C,DB: 未登录状态
        C->>Auth: 访问（无Token）
        Auth-->>C: session_id
        C->>Ctrl: POST /api/Cart/Add
        Ctrl->>Add: execute(session_id, data)
        Add->>DB: insert cart_items
        Add->>Cache: put cart:summary:session
    end

    rect rgb(230,245,255)
        Note over C,DB: 登录触发合并
        C->>Auth: POST /api/Login
        Auth-->>C: customer_id + token
        C->>Ctrl: POST /api/Cart/Merge
        Ctrl->>Merge: execute(customer_id, session_id)
        Merge->>DB: 查询guest_cart
        Merge->>DB: 合并到customer_cart
        Merge->>DB: 删除guest_cart
        Merge->>Cache: clear cart:summary:session, put cart:summary:customer
    end
```

---

## 6.3 热销榜与飙升榜服务 (BestsellerRankService)

### 6.3.1 设计概述

热销榜与飙升榜数据存储在 Redis Sorted Set 中，利用 ZADD / ZREVRANGE 实现高性能排序与分页查询。每日凌晨 2:00 由 Laravel Schedule 触发 SyncBestsellerRank Queue Job 异步刷新数据。

**双榜分离策略**：
- 热销榜（Bestseller）：heatValue = 近30天订单量×0.5 + 近30天浏览量×0.3 + 近30天收藏量×0.2
- 飙升榜（Rising）：growthRate = (近7天销量 - 前7天销量) / 前7天销量 × 100%

**运营干预**：后台通过 bestseller_rank_items 表配置置顶、隐藏、权重调整，刷新Job时读取运营配置与计算数据合并。

### 6.3.2 核心类图

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class BestsellerRankService {
        +getBestsellerRank(int categoryId, int limit): array
        +getRisingRank(int categoryId, int limit): array
        -loadFromDb(int categoryId): array
    }
    class SyncBestsellerRank {
        +handle(BestsellerRankService service): void
    }
    class RankItemAdminController {
        +pin(int id): void
        +hide(int id): void
        +adjustWeight(int id, int weight): void
    }
    class Schedule {
        +job(SyncBestsellerRank)->dailyAt('02:00')
    }
    
    BestsellerRankService --> SyncBestsellerRank
    RankItemAdminController --> BestsellerRankService
    Schedule --> SyncBestsellerRank
```

### 6.3.3 核心代码实现

#### 6.3.3.1 Redis Sorted Set 存储结构

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services;

use App\Models\BestsellerRankItem;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class BestsellerRankService
{
    private const string BESTSELLER_KEY = 'rank:bestseller:%s';
    private const string RISING_KEY = 'rank:rising:%s';
    private const int BESTSELLER_TTL_HOURS = 24;
    private const int RISING_TTL_HOURS = 12;

    public function getBestsellerRank(int $categoryId, int $limit = 20): array
    {
        $redisKey = sprintf(self::BESTSELLER_KEY, $categoryId);
        $items = Redis::zrevrange($redisKey, 0, $limit - 1, ['withscores' => true]);
        if (! empty($items)) {
            return $this->hydrateFromRedis($items, 'bestseller');
        }

        $items = $this->loadBestsellerFromDb($categoryId, $limit);
        $this->syncToRedis($redisKey, $items, 'heat_value', self::BESTSELLER_TTL_HOURS);
        return $items;
    }

    public function getRisingRank(int $categoryId, int $limit = 20): array
    {
        $redisKey = sprintf(self::RISING_KEY, $categoryId);
        $items = Redis::zrevrange($redisKey, 0, $limit - 1, ['withscores' => true]);
        if (! empty($items)) {
            return $this->hydrateFromRedis($items, 'rising');
        }

        $items = $this->loadRisingFromDb($categoryId, $limit);
        $this->syncToRedis($redisKey, $items, 'growth_rate', self::RISING_TTL_HOURS);
        return $items;
    }

    private function loadBestsellerFromDb(int $categoryId, int $limit): array
    {
        $since = now()->subDays(30);

        $orderStats = DB::table('orders')
            ->select('cd_category_id', DB::raw('COUNT(*) as count'))
            ->where('category_id', $categoryId)
            ->where('created_at', '>=', $since)
            ->whereNotIn('status', [0, 255])
            ->groupBy('cd_category_id')
            ->pluck('count', 'cd_category_id')
            ->all();

        $viewStats = DB::table('product_view_logs')
            ->select('cd_category_id', DB::raw('COUNT(*) as count'))
            ->where('category_id', $categoryId)
            ->where('created_at', '>=', $since)
            ->groupBy('cd_category_id')
            ->pluck('count', 'cd_category_id')
            ->all();

        $favoriteStats = DB::table('product_favorites')
            ->select('cd_category_id', DB::raw('COUNT(*) as count'))
            ->where('category_id', $categoryId)
            ->where('created_at', '>=', $since)
            ->groupBy('cd_category_id')
            ->pluck('count', 'cd_category_id')
            ->all();

        $heatMap = [];
        $allKeys = array_unique(array_merge(
            array_keys($orderStats),
            array_keys($viewStats),
            array_keys($favoriteStats)
        ));
        foreach ($allKeys as $key) {
            $heatMap[$key] = ($orderStats[$key] ?? 0) * 0.5
                + ($viewStats[$key] ?? 0) * 0.3
                + ($favoriteStats[$key] ?? 0) * 0.2;
        }

        $manualItems = BestsellerRankItem::where('category_id', $categoryId)
            ->where('rank_type', 1)
            ->get()
            ->keyBy('cd_category_id');

        $result = [];
        foreach ($heatMap as $cdId => $heat) {
            $manual = $manualItems[$cdId] ?? null;
            if ($manual && $manual->is_show === 0) {
                continue;
            }

            $result[] = [
                'cd_category_id' => $cdId,
                'category_name' => $manual?->category_name ?? $cdId,
                'heat_value' => round($heat, 2),
                'score' => $manual?->score ?? 5.00,
                'labels' => $manual?->labels ?? '-',
                'icon' => $manual?->icon ?? null,
                'is_pinned' => $manual?->is_pinned ?? false,
                'sort_weight' => $manual?->sort_weight ?? 0,
                'is_show' => $manual?->is_show ?? true,
            ];
        }

        usort($result, function ($a, $b) {
            if ($a['is_pinned'] !== $b['is_pinned']) {
                return $b['is_pinned'] <=> $a['is_pinned'];
            }
            if ($a['sort_weight'] !== $b['sort_weight']) {
                return $b['sort_weight'] <=> $a['sort_weight'];
            }
            return $b['heat_value'] <=> $a['heat_value'];
        });

        return array_slice($result, 0, $limit);
    }

    private function loadRisingFromDb(int $categoryId, int $limit): array
    {
        $last7Start = now()->subDays(14);
        $last7End = now()->subDays(7);
        $recent7Start = now()->subDays(7);

        $recent = DB::table('orders')
            ->select('cd_category_id', DB::raw('COUNT(*) as count'))
            ->where('category_id', $categoryId)
            ->whereBetween('created_at', [$recent7Start, now()])
            ->groupBy('cd_category_id')
            ->pluck('count', 'cd_category_id')
            ->all();

        $previous = DB::table('orders')
            ->select('cd_category_id', DB::raw('COUNT(*) as count'))
            ->where('category_id', $categoryId)
            ->whereBetween('created_at', [$last7Start, $last7End])
            ->groupBy('cd_category_id')
            ->pluck('count', 'cd_category_id')
            ->all();

        $result = [];
        foreach ($recent as $cdId => $recentCount) {
            $prevCount = $previous[$cdId] ?? 0;
            if ($prevCount === 0) {
                continue;
            }
            $growthRate = ($recentCount - $prevCount) / $prevCount * 100;

            $result[] = [
                'cd_category_id' => $cdId,
                'category_name' => $cdId,
                'growth_rate' => round($growthRate, 2),
                'score' => 5.00,
                'labels' => '-',
                'icon' => null,
            ];
        }

        usort($result, fn ($a, $b) => $b['growth_rate'] <=> $a['growth_rate']);
        return array_slice($result, 0, $limit);
    }

    private function syncToRedis(string $key, array $items, string $scoreField, int $ttlHours): void
    {
        Redis::del($key);
        foreach ($items as $item) {
            $score = $item[$scoreField] ?? 0;
            Redis::zadd($key, $score, json_encode($item));
        }
        Redis::expire($key, $ttlHours * 3600);
    }

    private function hydrateFromRedis(array $items, string $type): array
    {
        return collect($items)->map(fn ($json) => json_decode($json, true))->values()->all();
    }
}
```

#### 6.3.3.2 每日刷新队列任务

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Jobs;

use App\Services\BestsellerRankService;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class SyncBestsellerRank implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public int $tries = 3;

    public function handle(BestsellerRankService $service): void
    {
        Log::info('[RankSync] 开始刷新榜单');

        $categoryIds = \App\Models\ProductCategory::pluck('id')->all();

        foreach ($categoryIds as $categoryId) {
            try {
                $redisKey = sprintf('rank:bestseller:%s', $categoryId);
                Redis::del($redisKey);
                $service->getBestsellerRank($categoryId, 20);

                $redisKeyRising = sprintf('rank:rising:%s', $categoryId);
                Redis::del($redisKeyRising);
                $service->getRisingRank($categoryId, 20);
            } catch (\Throwable $e) {
                Log::error('[RankSync] 品类榜单刷新失败', [
                    'category_id' => $categoryId,
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),
                ]);
            }
        }

        Log::info('[RankSync] 榜单刷新完成');
    }
}
```

#### 6.3.3.3 Schedule 配置

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console;

use App\Jobs\SyncBestsellerRank;
use Illuminate\Console\Scheduling\Schedule;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Console\Kernel as ConsoleKernel;

class Kernel extends ConsoleKernel
{
    protected function schedule(Schedule $schedule): void
    {
        $schedule->job(new SyncBestsellerRank)
            ->dailyAt('02:00')
            ->withoutOverlapping(3600);
    }
}
```
