#### 6.3.3.4 运营干预后台接口

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Admin;

use App\Models\BestsellerRankItem;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class RankItemAdminController
{
    public function toggleVisibility(Request $request, int $id)
    {
        $item = BestsellerRankItem::findOrFail($id);
        if ($request->has('is_pinned')) {
            $item->is_pinned = $request->boolean('is_pinned');
        }
        if ($request->has('is_show')) {
            $item->is_show = $request->boolean('is_show');
        }
        $item->operator_id = auth('admin')->id();
        $item->save();

        Redis::del(
            sprintf('rank:bestseller:%s', $item->category_id),
            sprintf('rank:rising:%s', $item->category_id)
        );

        return response()->json(['message' => '操作成功']);
    }

    public function adjustWeight(Request $request, int $id)
    {
        $request->validate(['weight' => 'required|integer|min:0']);

        $item = BestsellerRankItem::findOrFail($id);
        $item->sort_weight = $request->input('weight');
        $item->operator_id = auth('admin')->id();
        $item->save();

        Redis::del(sprintf('rank:bestseller:%s', $item->category_id));

        return response()->json(['message' => '权重调整成功']);
    }
}
```

```mermaid
    Job->>Cron: 完成

    participant C as 客户端
    C->>Svc: GET /api/Common/GetBestsellerRank
    Svc->>Redis: ZREVRANGE
    Redis-->>Svc: 排序结果
    Svc-->>C: JSON (含heatValue, score, labels)
```

## 6.4 3D预览服务设计 (3D Preview Service)

### 6.4.1 设计概述

3D预览服务为商品详情页提供 Three.js 模型渲染支持。后端负责：
1. **模型文件管理**：接收管理员上传的3D模型文件（GLTF/GLB/JSON），通过 Laravel Storage 写入 MinIO
2. **预签名URL生成**：前端通过后端获取带时效的 MinIO 预签名URL，直传文件到对象存储，降低服务器带宽压力
3. **模型JSON配置API**：为前端 Three.js 提供模型加载配置（材质映射、热点坐标、默认视角等）
4. **文件版本管理**：order_files 表记录文件元数据，Storage 磁盘统一管理物理存储

### 6.4.2 核心类图

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Preview3DController {
        +uploadModel(Request request): JsonResponse
        +getModelConfig(int productId): JsonResponse
        +getPresignedUrl(Request request): JsonResponse
    }
    class Preview3DService {
        +storeModel(UploadedFile file, int productId): FileRecord
        +generateConfig(int productId): array
        +generatePresignedUrl(string path, int expiry): string
    }
    class FileRecord {
        +id: bigint
        +file_url: string
        +file_hash: string
        +file_size: int
        +version_no: int
    }
    class Storage {
        +put(path, contents, disk): bool
        +temporaryUrl(path, expiry): string
    }
    
    Preview3DController --> Preview3DService
    Preview3DService --> FileRecord
    Preview3DService --> Storage
```

### 6.4.3 核心代码实现

#### 6.4.3.1 文件上传与预签名URL

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Controllers;

use App\Models\FileRecord;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;

class Preview3DController extends Controller
{
    public function getPresignedUrl(Request $request)
    {
        $validated = $request->validate([
            'file_name' => 'required|string|max:255',
            'file_type' => 'required|string|in:gltf,glb,json,obj',
            'product_id' => 'required|integer|exists:products,id',
        ]);

        $path = sprintf(
            '3d-models/%d/%s_%s.%s',
            $validated['product_id'],
            now()->format('YmdHis'),
            uniqid(),
            $validated['file_type']
        );

        $disk = Storage::disk('minio');
        $url = $disk->temporaryUrl($path, now()->addMinutes(30), [
            'Content-Type' => match ($validated['file_type']) {
                'gltf' => 'model/gltf+json',
                'glb' => 'model/gltf-binary',
                default => 'application/octet-stream',
            },
        ]);

        return response()->json([
            'presigned_url' => $url,
            'file_path' => $path,
            'expires_at' => now()->addMinutes(30)->toDateTimeString(),
        ]);
    }

    public function confirmUpload(Request $request)
    {
        $validated = $request->validate([
            'product_id' => 'required|integer|exists:products,id',
            'file_path' => 'required|string',
            'file_name' => 'required|string',
            'file_size' => 'required|integer',
            'file_hash' => 'required|string|size:64',
        ]);

        $disk = Storage::disk('minio');
        if (! $disk->exists($validated['file_path'])) {
            return response()->json(['error' => '文件未找到，请重新上传'], 422);
        }

        $latestVersion = FileRecord::where('product_id', $validated['product_id'])
            ->where('file_type', '3d_model')
            ->max('version_no') ?? 0;

        $record = FileRecord::create([
            'product_id' => $validated['product_id'],
            'file_url' => $disk->url($validated['file_path']),
            'file_path' => $validated['file_path'],
            'file_name' => $validated['file_name'],
            'file_size' => $validated['file_size'],
            'file_hash' => $validated['file_hash'],
            'file_type' => '3d_model',
            'version_no' => $latestVersion + 1,
            'is_current' => true,
            'upload_method' => 'presigned',
            'uploader_id' => auth('admin')->id(),
        ]);

        FileRecord::where('product_id', $validated['product_id'])
            ->where('file_type', '3d_model')
            ->where('id', '!=', $record->id)
            ->update(['is_current' => false]);

        return response()->json([
            'file_id' => $record->id,
            'version_no' => $record->version_no,
            'file_url' => $record->file_url,
        ]);
    }

    public function getModelConfig(int $productId)
    {
        $record = FileRecord::where('product_id', $productId)
            ->where('file_type', '3d_model')
            ->where('is_current', true)
            ->first();

        if (! $record) {
            return response()->json(['error' => '该商品暂无3D模型'], 404);
        }

        $disk = Storage::disk('minio');
        $tempUrl = $disk->temporaryUrl($record->file_path, now()->addHours(2));

        $config = \App\Models\Preview3DConfig::where('product_id', $productId)
            ->where('version_no', $record->version_no)
            ->first();

        return response()->json([
            'model_url' => $tempUrl,
            'format' => pathinfo($record->file_name, PATHINFO_EXTENSION),
            'hotspots' => $config?->hotspots ?? [],
            'default_camera' => $config?->default_camera ?? ['position' => [0, 0, 5], 'target' => [0, 0, 0]],
            'material_mapping' => $config?->material_mapping ?? [],
            'auto_rotate' => $config?->auto_rotate ?? true,
            'background_color' => $config?->background_color ?? '#f5f5f5',
        ]);
    }
}
```

#### 6.4.3.2 文件版本管理模型

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;

class FileRecord extends Model
{
    protected $fillable = [
        'product_id', 'order_id', 'file_url', 'file_path', 'file_name',
        'file_size', 'file_hash', 'file_type', 'version_no', 'version_name',
        'is_current', 'upload_method', 'source_type', 'source_id', 'uploader_id',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'is_current' => 'boolean',
        'file_size' => 'integer',
    ];

    public function scopeCurrent($query)
    {
        return $query->where('is_current', true);
    }

    public function scopeForProduct($query, int $productId)
    {
        return $query->where('product_id', $productId);
    }
}
```

## 6.5 订单状态机设计 (Order State Machine)

### 6.5.1 设计概述

订单状态机是订单系统的核心控制中枢。PHP/Laravel版采用 **PHP 8.1 Backed Enum** 定义 FM（工厂生产流程状态）与 nM（客户展示状态），在 Enum 中内聚状态流转规则与双状态映射逻辑。

**核心设计点**：
- **FM状态枚举**：OrderStatus Backed Enum，内置 canTransitionTo() 校验方法
- **nM映射**：Enum 的 toCustomerStatus() 方法，将内部 FM 映射为客户展示状态
- **Eloquent Observer**：OrderObserver 监听 updating 事件，status 字段变更时自动触发 OrderStatusChanged 事件
- **订单修改流程**：独立 OrderModifyStatus Enum（IM枚举），通过 modify_status 字段管理，不破坏主状态机
- **定金子状态**：unpaid_deposit 字段叠加在主状态上，由 DepositStateManager 解析复合展示文本

**双状态映射规则**：

| FM(内部) | nM(客户展示) | 说明 |
|:--------:|:------------:|------|
| 0(已取消) | 0(已取消) | — |
| 1(已登记) | 1(待付款) | modifyStatus>0时→5(待修改) |
| 3,11,12,13,15 | 6(待生产) | 已审核/已下单/已分配 → 待生产 |
| 17,20,54,55,60,61,62 | 3(生产中) | 已开工单/外协/入库 → 生产中 |
| 65,66 | 7(待发货) | 已打包/已出库 → 待发货 |
| 67,69 | 4(已发货)/9(已完成) | 已发货→已发货，已完成→已完成 |
| 100(待沟通),101(文件审核不通过) | 5(待修改) | 特殊状态 |
| 任意+modifyStatus>0且未确认 | 5(待修改) | 修改子状态优先覆盖 |

> **注意**：`nM=6`（待生产）对应FM中生产准备阶段（审核后~开工单前），`nM=3`（生产中）对应实际生产执行阶段（开工单后~入库前）。两者均为内部"生产中"的大范畴，但对客户展示需区分"排队待生产"与"正在生产"。

### 6.5.2 状态机核心实现

#### 6.5.2.2 nM 客户展示状态枚举

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

enum CustomerOrderStatus: int
{
    case CANCELLED = 0;
    case PENDING_PAYMENT = 1;
    case IN_PRODUCTION = 3;
    case SHIPPED = 4;
    case PENDING_MODIFY = 5;
    case PENDING_PRODUCTION = 6;
    case PENDING_SHIP = 7;
    case DELIVERING = 8;
    case COMPLETED = 9;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::CANCELLED => '已取消',
            self::PENDING_PAYMENT => '待付款',
            self::IN_PRODUCTION => '生产中',
            self::SHIPPED => '已发货',
            self::PENDING_MODIFY => '待修改',
            self::PENDING_PRODUCTION => '待生产',
            self::PENDING_SHIP => '待发货',
            self::DELIVERING => '配送中',
            self::COMPLETED => '已完成',
        };
    }
}
```

#### 6.5.2.3 IM 订单修改状态枚举

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

enum OrderModifyStatus: int
{
    case DEFAULT = 0;
    case NOT_MODIFIED = 1;
    case FILE_PENDING_FINAL = 2;
    case PRODUCT_PENDING_MODIFY = 8;
    case FILE_PENDING_MODIFY = 16;
    case CERT_PENDING_MODIFY = 32;
    case PAUSED = 43;
    case MODIFIED = 64;
    case CONFIRMED = 128;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::DEFAULT => '默认',
            self::NOT_MODIFIED => '未修改',
            self::FILE_PENDING_FINAL => '文件待定稿',
            self::PRODUCT_PENDING_MODIFY => '产品待修改',
            self::FILE_PENDING_MODIFY => '文件待修改',
            self::CERT_PENDING_MODIFY => '证书待修改',
            self::PAUSED => '已暂停',
            self::MODIFIED => '已修改',
            self::CONFIRMED => '已确认',
        };
    }

    public function isInModifyProcess(): bool
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::DEFAULT, self::NOT_MODIFIED, self::CONFIRMED => false,
            default => true,
        };
    }

    /**
     * 判断是否包含指定修改类型（位掩码检查）
     */
    public function hasType(self $type): bool
    {
        return ($this->value & $type->value) === $type->value;
    }
}
```

#### 6.5.2.4 Order 模型与状态流转方法
#### 6.5.2.5 Eloquent Observer 自动触发事件

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Observers;

use App\Enums\OrderStatus;
use App\Events\OrderStatusChanged;
use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class OrderObserver
{
    public function updating(Order $order): void
    {
        if ($order->isDirty('status')) {
            $original = OrderStatus::from($order->getOriginal('status'));
            $new = $order->status;

            if (! $original->canTransitionTo($new)) {
                throw new \App\Exceptions\InvalidStateTransitionException(
                    "Observer拦截非法流转: {$original->value} -> {$new->value}"
                );
            }

            $order->out_status_name = $new->toCustomerStatus($order->modify_status)->value;

            Log::info('[OrderObserver] 状态变更', [
                'order_sn' => $order->order_sn,
                'from' => $original->label(),
                'to' => $new->label(),
            ]);
        }
    }

    public function updated(Order $order): void
    {
        if ($order->wasChanged('status')) {
            $original = OrderStatus::from($order->getOriginal('status'));

            event(new OrderStatusChanged($order, $original, $order->status));
        }
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

// AppServiceProvider::boot()
namespace App\Providers;

use App\Models\Order;
use App\Observers\OrderObserver;
use Illuminate\Support\ServiceProvider;

class AppServiceProvider extends ServiceProvider
{
    public function boot(): void
    {
        Order::observe(OrderObserver::class);
    }
}
```

#### 6.5.2.6 订单状态变更事件与监听

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Events;

use App\Enums\OrderStatus;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Events\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

class OrderStatusChanged
{
    use Dispatchable, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(
        public Order $order,
        public OrderStatus $oldStatus,
        public OrderStatus $newStatus,
        public readonly ?string $operator = null,
        public readonly ?string $remark = null,
    ) {}
}
```

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Listeners;

use App\Events\OrderStatusChanged;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class OrderStatusChangedNotification
{
    public function handle(OrderStatusChanged $event): void
    {
        $notifyNodes = [
            \App\Enums\OrderStatus::OUTBOUND->value,
            \App\Enums\OrderStatus::COMPLETED->value,
            \App\Enums\OrderStatus::CANCELLED->value,
        ];

        if (! in_array($event->newStatus->value, $notifyNodes)) {
            return;
        }

        $order = $event->order;

        $order->customer->notify(new \App\Notifications\OrderStatusUpdated($order));

        Log::info('[OrderNotify] 状态变更通知已发送', [
            'order_sn' => $order->order_sn,
            'to_status' => $event->newStatus->label(),
        ]);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

// EventServiceProvider
protected $listen = [
    \App\Events\OrderStatusChanged::class => [
        \App\Listeners\OrderStatusChangedNotification::class,
        \App\Listeners\OrderStatusAuditLog::class,
        \App\Listeners\OrderStatusWebhook::class,
    ],
];
```

### 6.5.3 样品订单与云仓订单独立状态机

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

enum SampleOrderStatus: int
{
    case PENDING_PAYMENT = 100;
    case PAID = 101;
    case PENDING_SHIP = 102;
    case SHIPPED = 103;
    case COMPLETED = 104;
    case CANCELLED = 105;

    public function canTransitionTo(self $target): bool
    {
        return match ([$this, $target]) {
            [self::PENDING_PAYMENT, self::PAID],
            [self::PENDING_PAYMENT, self::CANCELLED] => true,
            [self::PAID, self::PENDING_SHIP] => true,
            [self::PENDING_SHIP, self::SHIPPED] => true,
            [self::SHIPPED, self::COMPLETED] => true,
            default => false,
        };
    }

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::PENDING_PAYMENT => '待付款',
            self::PAID => '已付款',
            self::PENDING_SHIP => '待发货',
            self::SHIPPED => '已发货',
            self::COMPLETED => '已完成',
            self::CANCELLED => '已取消',
        };
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

enum CloudOrderStatus: int
{
    case PENDING_PAYMENT = 200;
    case PAID = 201;
    case OUTBOUND = 202;
    case SHIPPED = 203;
    case COMPLETED = 204;
    case CANCELLED = 205;

    public function canTransitionTo(self $target): bool
    {
        return match ([$this, $target]) {
            [self::PENDING_PAYMENT, self::PAID],
            [self::PENDING_PAYMENT, self::CANCELLED] => true,
            [self::PAID, self::OUTBOUND] => true,
            [self::OUTBOUND, self::SHIPPED] => true,
            [self::SHIPPED, self::COMPLETED] => true,
            default => false,
        };
    }

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::PENDING_PAYMENT => '待付款',
            self::PAID => '已付款',
            self::OUTBOUND => '已出库',
            self::SHIPPED => '已发货',
            self::COMPLETED => '已完成',
            self::CANCELLED => '已取消',
        };
    }
}
```

### 6.5.4 数据流说明

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Ctrl as OrderController
    participant Order as Order Model
    participant Obs as OrderObserver
    participant Event as OrderStatusChanged
    participant Notify as NotificationListener
    participant Audit as AuditLogListener
    participant DB as MySQL

    Ctrl->>Order: transitionTo(AUDITED, operator)
    Order->>Order: canTransitionTo()校验
    alt 非法流转
        Order-->>Ctrl: InvalidStateTransitionException
    else 合法流转
        Order->>DB: update status, out_status_name
        Order->>Obs: updating()
        Obs->>Obs: 自动映射nM状态
        Obs->>DB: 持久化
        Obs->>Event: dispatch(OrderStatusChanged)
        Event->>Notify: handle()
        Notify->>Notify: 关键节点发送站内信/短信
        Event->>Audit: handle()
        Audit->>DB: insert audit_logs
    end
```

## 6.6 订单评价系统设计

### 6.6.1 设计概述

订单评价系统在订单完成后（FM=69 / nM=9）允许客户提交评价。核心注意点：
- **评价等级与常规相反**：PRD定义 4=非常满意、5=不满意，必须在代码和展示层保持与源码一致，前端可按需映射转换
- **图片上传**：支持最多9张凭证图，通过 Laravel Storage 直传 MinIO
- **成长值奖励**：评价完成后发放 +10 成长值（异步队列）

### 6.6.2 核心代码实现

#### 6.6.2.1 评价等级枚举

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

enum CommentLevel: int
{
    case EXTREMELY_POOR = 1;
    case AVERAGE = 2;
    case SATISFIED = 3;
    case VERY_SATISFIED = 4;
    case DISSATISFIED = 5;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::EXTREMELY_POOR => '极差',
            self::AVERAGE => '一般',
            self::SATISFIED => '满意',
            self::VERY_SATISFIED => '非常满意',
            self::DISSATISFIED => '不满意',
        };
    }

    public function isPositive(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::SATISFIED, self::VERY_SATISFIED], true);
    }
}
```

#### 6.6.2.2 Eloquent 模型与 Action

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Models;

use App\Enums\CommentLevel;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;

class OrderReview extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'order_reviews';

    protected $fillable = [
        'order_id', 'order_sn', 'customer_id', 'product_id',
        'level', 'content', 'images', 'tags', 'is_anonymous',
        'reply_content', 'reply_time', 'status',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'level' => CommentLevel::class,
        'images' => 'array',
        'tags' => 'array',
        'is_anonymous' => 'boolean',
        'reply_time' => 'datetime',
    ];

    public function order()
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Order::class);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions;

use App\Enums\CommentLevel;
use App\Models\Order;
use App\Models\OrderReview;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class SubmitOrderReviewAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId, array $data): OrderReview
    {
        return DB::transaction(function () use ($customerId, $data) {
            $order = Order::where('order_sn', $data['order_sn'])->firstOrFail();

            if ($order->customer_id !== $customerId) {
                throw new \App\Exceptions\UnauthorizedException('无权评价此订单');
            }

            if ($order->status !== \App\Enums\OrderStatus::COMPLETED) {
                throw new \App\Exceptions\BizException('ORDER_NOT_COMPLETED', '仅已完成订单可评价');
            }

            if (OrderReview::where('order_sn', $data['order_sn'])->exists()) {
                throw new \App\Exceptions\BizException('COMMENT_EXISTS', '该订单已评价');
            }

            $level = CommentLevel::from($data['level']);

            $review = OrderReview::create([
                'order_id' => $order->id,
                'order_sn' => $order->order_sn,
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'product_id' => $data['product_id'] ?? $order->items->first()?->product_id,
                'level' => $level,
                'content' => $data['content'] ?? '',
                'images' => $data['images'] ?? [],
                'tags' => $data['tags'] ?? [],
                'is_anonymous' => $data['is_anonymous'] ?? false,
                'status' => 1,
            ]);

            \App\Jobs\GrantGrowthValue::dispatch(
                customerId: $customerId,
                growthValue: 10,
                type: \App\Enums\GrowthValueType::COMMENT,
                sourceId: $review->id,
                description: "订单评价奖励，orderSn={$order->order_sn}",
            );

            Log::info('[Review] 评价提交', [
                'order_sn' => $order->order_sn,
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'level' => $level->label(),
            ]);

            return $review;
        });
    }
}
```

#### 6.6.2.3 图片上传处理

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Controllers;

use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;
use Illuminate\Support\Str;

class ReviewImageController extends Controller
{
    public function upload(Request $request)
    {
        $request->validate([
            'images' => 'required|array|max:9',
            'images.*' => 'required|image|mimes:jpg,jpeg,png|max:5120',
        ]);

        $urls = [];
        $disk = Storage::disk('minio');

        foreach ($request->file('images') as $file) {
            $path = $file->storeAs(
                'reviews/' . now()->format('Y/m'),
                Str::uuid() . '.' . $file->getClientOriginalExtension(),
                'minio'
            );
            $urls[] = $disk->url($path);
        }

        return response()->json(['urls' => $urls]);
    }
}
```

### 6.6.3 数据流说明

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant C as 客户端
    participant Ctrl as OrderReviewController
    participant Act as SubmitOrderReviewAction
    participant DB as MySQL
    participant Q as Queue

    C->>Ctrl: POST /api/OrderProductComment/Create
    Ctrl->>Act: execute(customerId, data)
    Act->>DB: 校验订单已完成
    Act->>DB: 校验未重复评价
    Act->>DB: insert order_reviews
    Act->>Q: dispatch(GrantGrowthValue)
    Act-->>Ctrl: OrderReview
    Ctrl-->>C: success
```

## 6.7 订单统计服务 (OrderStatisticsService)

### 6.7.1 设计概述

订单统计服务面向客户侧（我的订单数、待付款、待收货等）和管理后台（销售趋势、品类占比）提供聚合数据。采用 Eloquent Query + DB::raw 聚合 + Redis 缓存 三层架构：
- 实时统计（如待付款数量）：Eloquent Scope 直接查询，结果缓存5分钟
- 趋势统计（如近6个月订单金额）：DB::raw 聚合，结果缓存1小时
- 定时报表：Schedule 每日生成昨日汇总，写入 daily_order_stats 表

### 6.7.2 核心代码实现

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services;

use App\Enums\OrderStatus;
use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

class OrderStatisticsService
{
    public function getCustomerOrderCounts(int $customerId): array
    {
        return Cache::remember("order:counts:{$customerId}", now()->addMinutes(5), function () use ($customerId) {
            $baseQuery = Order::where('customer_id', $customerId)
                ->whereNotIn('status', [OrderStatus::CANCELLED, OrderStatus::EXCEPTION]);

            return [
                'total' => (clone $baseQuery)->count(),
                'pending_payment' => (clone $baseQuery)
                    ->where('status', OrderStatus::REGISTERED)
                    ->where('modify_status', 0)
                    ->count(),
                'in_production' => (clone $baseQuery)
                    ->where('status', '>=', OrderStatus::AUDITED->value)
                    ->where('status', '<', OrderStatus::INBOUND->value)
                    ->count(),
                'pending_ship' => (clone $baseQuery)
                    ->where('status', OrderStatus::INBOUND)
                    ->count(),
                'shipped' => (clone $baseQuery)
                    ->whereIn('status', [OrderStatus::OUTBOUND, OrderStatus::NORMAL_OUTBOUND])
                    ->count(),
                'completed' => (clone $baseQuery)
                    ->where('status', OrderStatus::COMPLETED)
                    ->count(),
                'pending_modify' => (clone $baseQuery)
                    ->where('modify_status', '>', 0)
                    ->where('modify_status', '!=', 128)
                    ->count(),
            ];
        });
    }

    public function getLastSixMonthsStatistics(int $customerId): array
    {
        $cacheKey = "order:stats:6m:{$customerId}";

        return Cache::remember($cacheKey, now()->addHour(), function () use ($customerId) {
            $results = Order::select(
                DB::raw("DATE_FORMAT(created_at, '%Y-%m') as month"),
                DB::raw('COUNT(*) as order_count'),
                DB::raw('SUM(total_price) as total_amount'),
                DB::raw('COUNT(DISTINCT DATE(created_at)) as order_days')
            )
                ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
                ->where('created_at', '>=', now()->subMonths(6))
                ->whereNotIn('status', [OrderStatus::CANCELLED, OrderStatus::EXCEPTION])
                ->groupBy('month')
                ->orderBy('month')
                ->get();

            return $results->map(fn ($row) => [
                'month' => $row->month,
                'order_count' => (int) $row->order_count,
                'total_amount' => round($row->total_amount / 100, 2),
                'order_days' => (int) $row->order_days,
            ])->all();
        });
    }

    public function getStatisticsByParentCategory(int $customerId): array
    {
        $cacheKey = "order:stats:category:{$customerId}";

        return Cache::remember($cacheKey, now()->addHour(), function () use ($customerId) {
            return Order::select(
                'parent_category_id',
                DB::raw('COUNT(*) as count'),
                DB::raw('SUM(total_price) as amount')
            )
                ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
                ->whereNotIn('status', [OrderStatus::CANCELLED, OrderStatus::EXCEPTION])
                ->groupBy('parent_category_id')
                ->get()
                ->map(fn ($row) => [
                    'parent_category_id' => $row->parent_category_id,
                    'count' => (int) $row->count,
                    'amount' => round($row->amount / 100, 2),
                ])
                ->all();
        });
    }

    public function getCustomerOverallStatistics(int $customerId): array
    {
        $cacheKey = "order:stats:overall:{$customerId}";

        return Cache::remember($cacheKey, now()->addMinutes(10), function () use ($customerId) {
            $stats = Order::where('customer_id', $customerId)
                ->whereNotIn('status', [OrderStatus::CANCELLED, OrderStatus::EXCEPTION])
                ->select(
                    DB::raw('COUNT(*) as total_orders'),
                    DB::raw('SUM(total_price) as total_amount'),
                    DB::raw('AVG(total_price) as avg_price'),
                    DB::raw('MAX(created_at) as last_order_at')
                )
                ->first();

            return [
                'total_orders' => (int) $stats->total_orders,
                'total_amount' => round($stats->total_amount / 100, 2),
                'avg_price' => round($stats->avg_price / 100, 2),
                'last_order_at' => $stats->last_order_at,
            ];
        });
    }

    public function clearCustomerCache(int $customerId): void
    {
        Cache::forget("order:counts:{$customerId}");
        Cache::forget("order:stats:6m:{$customerId}");
        Cache::forget("order:stats:category:{$customerId}");
        Cache::forget("order:stats:overall:{$customerId}");
    }
}
```

#### 6.7.3 统计缓存清理Listener

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Listeners;

use App\Events\OrderStatusChanged;
use App\Services\OrderStatisticsService;

class ClearOrderStatsCache
{
    public function __construct(
        private OrderStatisticsService $statsService,
    ) {}

    public function handle(OrderStatusChanged $event): void
    {
        $this->statsService->clearCustomerCache($event->order->customer_id);
    }
}
```

### 6.7.4 数据流说明

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant C as 客户端
    participant Svc as OrderStatisticsService
    participant Cache as Redis
    participant DB as MySQL

    C->>Svc: getCustomerOrderCounts(customerId)
    Svc->>Cache: get("order:counts:{customerId}")
    alt 缓存命中
        Cache-->>Svc: 返回缓存
    else 缓存未命中
        Svc->>DB: Eloquent聚合查询
        DB-->>Svc: 统计结果
        Svc->>Cache: put(5min)
    end
    Svc-->>C: {total, pending_payment, in_production...}
```

## 6.8 云仓批量下单与模板下载

### 6.8.1 设计概述

云仓批量下单允许客户通过 Excel 模板导入多个收货地址和数量，系统自动创建批量订单。核心组件：
- **模板生成**：PhpSpreadsheet 动态生成带下拉选项和数据验证的 Excel 模板
- **导入验证**：Laravel FormRequest + 自定义 Validation Rule 校验每一行数据
- **异步创建**：验证通过后通过 Queue::bulk() 批量投递 CreateCloudOrderJob，Horizon 监控进度

### 6.8.2 核心代码实现

#### 6.8.2.1 Excel 模板生成

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services;

use PhpOffice\PhpSpreadsheet\Spreadsheet;
use PhpOffice\PhpSpreadsheet\Writer\Xlsx;
use Symfony\Component\HttpFoundation\StreamedResponse;

class CloudOrderTemplateService
{
    public function generate(int $productId): StreamedResponse
    {
        $spreadsheet = new Spreadsheet();
        $sheet = $spreadsheet->getActiveSheet();

        $headers = ['序号', '收货人', '手机号', '省', '市', '区', '详细地址', '数量', '备注'];
        foreach ($headers as $col => $header) {
            $sheet->setCellValueByColumnAndRow($col + 1, 1, $header);
        }

        $sheet->setCellValue('A2', 1);
        $sheet->setCellValue('B2', '张三');
        $sheet->setCellValue('C2', '13800138000');
        $sheet->setCellValue('D2', '浙江省');
        $sheet->setCellValue('E2', '杭州市');
        $sheet->setCellValue('F2', '西湖区');
        $sheet->setCellValue('G2', 'xx街道xx号');
        $sheet->setCellValue('H2', 100);
        $sheet->setCellValue('I2', '加急');

        $sheet->getColumnDimension('A')->setWidth(8);
        $sheet->getColumnDimension('B')->setWidth(12);
        $sheet->getColumnDimension('C')->setWidth(15);
        $sheet->getColumnDimension('D')->setWidth(12);
        $sheet->getColumnDimension('E')->setWidth(12);
        $sheet->getColumnDimension('F')->setWidth(12);
        $sheet->getColumnDimension('G')->setWidth(30);
        $sheet->getColumnDimension('H')->setWidth(10);
        $sheet->getColumnDimension('I')->setWidth(20);

        $filename = "cloud_order_template_{$productId}_" . now()->format('Ymd') . '.xlsx';

        return new StreamedResponse(function () use ($spreadsheet) {
            $writer = new Xlsx($spreadsheet);
            $writer->save('php://output');
        }, 200, [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet',
            'Content-Disposition' => "attachment; filename=\"{$filename}\"",
        ]);
    }
}
```

#### 6.8.2.2 批量导入验证与队列投递

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions;

use App\Jobs\CreateCloudOrderJob;
use App\Models\Product;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Queue;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Validator;
use PhpOffice\PhpSpreadsheet\IOFactory;

class ImportCloudBatchOrderAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId, int $productId, string $filePath): array
    {
        $product = Product::findOrFail($productId);
        if (! $product->is_cloud_warehouse) {
            throw new \App\Exceptions\BizException('NOT_CLOUD_PRODUCT', '非云仓商品');
        }

        $reader = IOFactory::createReader('Xlsx');
        $spreadsheet = $reader->load(Storage::disk('local')->path($filePath));
        $sheet = $spreadsheet->getActiveSheet();
        $rows = $sheet->toArray();

        array_shift($rows);

        $jobs = [];
        $errors = [];
        $line = 2;

        foreach ($rows as $row) {
            if (empty(array_filter($row))) {
                $line++;
                continue;
            }

            $data = [
                'receiver' => $row[1] ?? null,
                'mobile' => $row[2] ?? null,
                'province' => $row[3] ?? null,
                'city' => $row[4] ?? null,
                'district' => $row[5] ?? null,
                'address' => $row[6] ?? null,
                'quantity' => $row[7] ?? null,
                'remark' => $row[8] ?? null,
            ];

            $validator = Validator::make($data, [
                'receiver' => 'required|string|max:50',
                'mobile' => 'required|regex:/^1[3-9]\d{9}$/',
                'province' => 'required|string',
                'city' => 'required|string',
                'district' => 'required|string',
                'address' => 'required|string|max:200',
                'quantity' => 'required|integer|min:1',
            ]);

            if ($validator->fails()) {
                $errors[] = [
                    'line' => $line,
                    'errors' => $validator->errors()->all(),
                ];
                $line++;
                continue;
            }

            $jobs[] = new CreateCloudOrderJob(
                customerId: $customerId,
                productId: $productId,
                addressData: $data,
                batchNo: basename($filePath, '.xlsx'),
            );

            $line++;
        }

        if (! empty($errors)) {
            return [
                'success' => false,
                'errors' => $errors,
                'total' => count($jobs) + count($errors),
            ];
        }

        Queue::bulk($jobs);

        return [
            'success' => true,
            'job_count' => count($jobs),
            'batch_no' => basename($filePath, '.xlsx'),
        ];
    }
}
```

#### 6.8.2.3 异步创建订单队列任务

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Jobs;

use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class CreateCloudOrderJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public int $tries = 3;

    public function __construct(
        public int $customerId,
        public int $productId,
        public array $addressData,
        public string $batchNo,
    ) {}

    public function handle(): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () {
            $order = Order::create([
                'order_sn' => 'CW' . now()->format('YmdHis') . random_int(1000, 9999),
                'customer_id' => $this->customerId,
                'product_id' => $this->productId,
                'status' => \App\Enums\CloudOrderStatus::PENDING_PAYMENT->value,
                'out_status_name' => \App\Enums\CloudOrderStatus::PENDING_PAYMENT->value,
                'order_type' => 3,
                'receiver' => $this->addressData['receiver'],
                'mobile' => $this->addressData['mobile'],
                'province' => $this->addressData['province'],
                'city' => $this->addressData['city'],
                'district' => $this->addressData['district'],
                'address' => $this->addressData['address'],
                'quantity' => $this->addressData['quantity'],
                'remark' => $this->addressData['remark'],
                'batch_no' => $this->batchNo,
            ]);

            Log::info('[CloudBatch] 云仓订单创建', ['order_sn' => $order->order_sn]);
        });
    }
}
```

### 6.8.3 数据流说明

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant C as 客户端
    participant Ctrl as CloudBatchController
    participant Template as CloudOrderTemplateService
    participant Import as ImportCloudBatchOrderAction
    participant Q as Queue(Horizon)
    participant DB as MySQL

    C->>Ctrl: GET /api/Export/GenerateCloudhouseOrderImportTemplate
    Ctrl->>Template: generate(productId)
    Template-->>C: Excel模板下载

    C->>Ctrl: POST /api/cloud/batch-import
    Ctrl->>Import: execute(customerId, productId, file)
    Import->>Import: PhpSpreadsheet解析
    Import->>Import: Laravel Validation逐行校验
    alt 校验失败
        Import-->>Ctrl: 返回错误行号与原因
        Ctrl-->>C: 400 + errors
    else 校验通过
        Import->>Q: Queue::bulk(CreateCloudOrderJob[])
        Import-->>Ctrl: batch_no + job_count
        Ctrl-->>C: 202 Accepted
        Q->>DB: 批量创建订单
    end
```

---

## 6.9 本地订单同步

### 6.9.1 设计概述

本地订单同步用于将线下门店/ERP系统的订单数据同步到线上平台。采用 Laravel Schedule + Artisan Command 定时执行，通过数据比对（线上订单 vs 本地订单）检测差异并自动补录。

**同步策略**：
- 定时任务：每15分钟执行一次增量同步
- 数据比对：以 order_sn 为主键，对比状态、金额、客户信息差异
- 差异处理：线上缺失则创建，状态不一致则更新（受状态机约束）

### 6.9.2 核心代码实现

#### 6.9.2.1 同步 Command

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use App\Models\LocalOrder;
use App\Models\Order;
use App\Enums\OrderStatus;
use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class SyncLocalOrders extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'orders:sync-local 
                            {--since= : 同步起始时间，默认昨天}
                            {--dry-run : 仅检测差异，不执行写入}';

    protected $description = '同步本地订单到线上系统';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $since = $this->option('since')
            ? now()->parse($this->option('since'))
            : now()->subDay();

        $dryRun = $this->option('dry-run');

        $this->info("开始同步本地订单，since={$since->toDateTimeString()}");

        LocalOrder::where('sync_status', 0)
            ->where('created_at', '>=', $since)
            ->orWhere('updated_at', '>=', $since)
            ->chunkById(100, function ($locals) use ($dryRun) {
                foreach ($locals as $local) {
                    $this->syncSingle($local, $dryRun);
                }
            });

        $this->info('本地订单同步完成');
        return self::SUCCESS;
    }

    private function syncSingle(LocalOrder $local, bool $dryRun): void
    {
        $existing = Order::where('order_sn', $local->order_sn)->first();

        if (! $existing) {
            $this->info("[CREATE] 本地订单 {$local->order_sn} 在线上不存在");
            if ($dryRun) {
                return;
            }

            DB::transaction(function () use ($local) {
                Order::create([
                    'order_sn' => $local->order_sn,
                    'customer_id' => $local->customer_id,
                    'status' => OrderStatus::REGISTERED,
                    'out_status_name' => OrderStatus::REGISTERED->toCustomerStatus()->value,
                    'product_sum' => $local->product_sum,
                    'sum' => $local->sum,
                    'total_price' => $local->total_price,
                    'source' => 0,
                    'create_source' => 32,
                    'remark' => "[本地同步] {$local->remark}",
                ]);
                $local->update(['sync_status' => 1, 'synced_at' => now()]);
            });
            return;
        }

        if ($existing->status->value !== $local->status) {
            $this->warn("[DIFF] {$local->order_sn} 状态不一致: 线上={$existing->status->value}, 本地={$local->status}");

            if ($dryRun) {
                return;
            }

            try {
                $target = OrderStatus::from($local->status);
                $existing->transitionTo($target, 'local_sync', '本地订单状态同步');
                $local->update(['sync_status' => 1, 'synced_at' => now()]);
            } catch (\App\Exceptions\InvalidStateTransitionException $e) {
                Log::warning('[LocalSync] 状态流转冲突，跳过', [
                    'order_sn' => $local->order_sn,
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),
                ]);
                $local->update(['sync_status' => 2, 'sync_error' => $e->getMessage()]);
            }
        }
    }
}
```

#### 6.9.2.2 Schedule 配置

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console;

use App\Console\Commands\SyncLocalOrders;
use Illuminate\Console\Scheduling\Schedule;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Console\Kernel as ConsoleKernel;

class Kernel extends ConsoleKernel
{
    protected function schedule(Schedule $schedule): void
    {
        $schedule->command(SyncLocalOrders::class)
            ->everyFifteenMinutes()
            ->withoutOverlapping(900)
            ->onOneServer();
    }
}
```

### 6.9.3 数据流说明

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Cron as Schedule(every15min)
    participant Cmd as SyncLocalOrders
    participant Local as local_orders
    participant Order as orders

    Cron->>Cmd: execute
    Cmd->>Local: 查询sync_status=0
    Local-->>Cmd: 待同步记录
    loop 逐条处理
        Cmd->>Order: 按order_sn查询
        alt 线上缺失
            Cmd->>Order: insert
            Cmd->>Local: update sync_status=1
        else 状态不一致且可流转
            Cmd->>Order: transitionTo()
            Cmd->>Local: update sync_status=1
        else 状态冲突
            Cmd->>Local: update sync_status=2 + error
        end
    end
```

---

## 6.10 样品商品配置与库存管理

### 6.10.1 设计概述

样品订单使用独立状态机（100~105），与普通订单状态空间完全隔离。库存管理采用 Redis 原子操作（DECR/INCR） 实现库存锁定，配合 Queue Delayed Job 实现超时自动释放。

**核心设计点**：
- 样品状态机：SampleOrderStatus Backed Enum，独立流转规则
- 库存锁定：Redis::decr() 原子扣减，避免超卖
- 超时释放：订单创建后15分钟未支付，投递 ReleaseSampleStockJob（delayed 15min）
- VIP折扣：Lv1~Lv3样品9折；Lv4无样品折扣；Lv5样品5折；Lv6~Lv8无样品折扣，印品折扣分别为93/92/90折；Lv1~Lv5无印品折扣

### 6.10.2 核心代码实现

#### 6.10.2.1 样品库存锁定服务

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services;

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class SampleInventoryService
{
    private const string STOCK_KEY = 'sample:stock:%d';
    private const string LOCK_KEY = 'sample:lock:%s';

    public function lockStock(int $productId, int $quantity, string $orderSn): bool
    {
        $stockKey = sprintf(self::STOCK_KEY, $productId);
        $lockKey = sprintf(self::LOCK_KEY, $orderSn);

        $lua = <<<LUA
            local stock = tonumber(redis.call('GET', KEYS[1]) or 0)
            local qty = tonumber(ARGV[1])
            if stock < qty then
                return -1
            end
            redis.call('DECRBY', KEYS[1], qty)
            redis.call('SET', KEYS[2], qty, 'EX', 900)
            return 1
LUA;

        $result = Redis::eval($lua, 2, $stockKey, $lockKey, $quantity);

        if ($result === -1) {
            Log::warning('[SampleStock] 库存不足', [
                'product_id' => $productId,
                'order_sn' => $orderSn,
                'quantity' => $quantity,
            ]);
            return false;
        }

        Log::info('[SampleStock] 库存预占成功', [
            'product_id' => $productId,
            'order_sn' => $orderSn,
            'quantity' => $quantity,
        ]);

        return true;
    }

    public function releaseStock(int $productId, int $quantity, string $orderSn): void
    {
        $stockKey = sprintf(self::STOCK_KEY, $productId);
        $lockKey = sprintf(self::LOCK_KEY, $orderSn);

        $lua = <<<LUA
            if redis.call('EXISTS', KEYS[2]) == 1 then
                redis.call('INCRBY', KEYS[1], ARGV[1])
                redis.call('DEL', KEYS[2])
                return 1
            end
            return 0
LUA;

        $result = Redis::eval($lua, 2, $stockKey, $lockKey, $quantity);

        if ($result === 1) {
            Log::info('[SampleStock] 库存释放成功', [
                'product_id' => $productId,
                'order_sn' => $orderSn,
            ]);
        }
    }

    public function confirmDeduction(string $orderSn): void
    {
        $lockKey = sprintf(self::LOCK_KEY, $orderSn);
        Redis::del($lockKey);
    }
}
```

#### 6.10.2.2 超时释放队列任务

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Jobs;

use App\Models\Order;
use App\Services\SampleInventoryService;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class ReleaseSampleStockJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(
        public int $productId,
        public int $quantity,
        public string $orderSn,
    ) {}

    public function handle(SampleInventoryService $inventory): void
    {
        $order = Order::where('order_sn', $this->orderSn)->first();

        if (! $order || $order->status !== \App\Enums\SampleOrderStatus::PENDING_PAYMENT) {
            Log::info('[SampleRelease] 订单已支付或不存在，跳过释放', [
                'order_sn' => $this->orderSn,
            ]);
            return;
        }

        $inventory->releaseStock($this->productId, $this->quantity, $this->orderSn);

        $order->update([
            'status' => \App\Enums\SampleOrderStatus::CANCELLED->value,
            'out_status_name' => \App\Enums\SampleOrderStatus::CANCELLED->value,
            'remark' => ($order->remark ?? '') . ' | [系统] 超时未支付自动取消',
        ]);
    }
}
```

#### 6.10.2.3 样品订单创建 Action

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions;

use App\Enums\SampleOrderStatus;
use App\Jobs\ReleaseSampleStockJob;
use App\Models\Order;
use App\Models\Product;
use App\Services\SampleInventoryService;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class CreateSampleOrderAction
{
    public function __construct(
        private SampleInventoryService $inventory,
        private \App\Pipelines\PricingPipeline $pricing,
    ) {}

    public function execute(int $customerId, array $data): Order
    {
        return DB::transaction(function () use ($customerId, $data) {
            $product = Product::findOrFail($data['product_id']);
            if (! $product->is_sample) {
                throw new \App\Exceptions\BizException('NOT_SAMPLE_PRODUCT', '非样品商品');
            }

            $orderSn = $data['order_sn'] ?? 'S' . now()->format('YmdHis') . random_int(1000, 9999);

            $locked = $this->inventory->lockStock($product->id, $data['quantity'], $orderSn);
            if (! $locked) {
                throw new \App\Exceptions\BizException('SAMPLE_STOCK_INSUFFICIENT', '样品库存不足');
            }

            $vipLevel = \App\Models\Customer::find($customerId)?->vip_level;
            $discountRate = match ($vipLevel) {
                1, 2, 3 => 0.90,
                5 => 0.50,
                default => 1.0,
            };

            $pricingInput = new \App\ValueObjects\PricingInput(
                productId: $product->id,
                cpSummary: $data['cp_summary'] ?? '',
                quantity: $data['quantity'],
                customerId: $customerId,
                isSample: true,
                vipLevel: $vipLevel,
            );
            $pricingResult = $this->pricing->calculate($pricingInput);
            $finalAmount = $pricingResult->getPayable()->multiply($discountRate);

            $order = Order::create([
                'order_sn' => $orderSn,
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'status' => SampleOrderStatus::PENDING_PAYMENT->value,
                'out_status_name' => SampleOrderStatus::PENDING_PAYMENT->value,
                'order_type' => 2,  // FIX-P0: 样品订单已迁移至sample_orders独立表
                'product_id' => $product->id,
                'product_sum' => $pricingResult->getPayable()->amount,
                'discount_sum' => $pricingResult->getPayable()->subtract($finalAmount)->amount,
                'sum' => $finalAmount->amount,
                'total_price' => $finalAmount->amount,
                'quantity' => $data['quantity'],
                'remark' => $data['remark'] ?? null,
            ]);

            // 15分钟后超时释放
            ReleaseSampleStockJob::dispatch(
                $product->id,
                $data['quantity'],
                $orderSn
            )->delay(now()->addMinutes(15));

            Log::info('[SampleOrder] 创建成功', [
                'order_sn' => $orderSn,
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'vip_level' => $vipLevel,
                'discount_rate' => $discountRate,
            ]);

            return $order;
        });
    }
}
```

### 6.10.3 数据流说明

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant C as 客户端
    participant Act as CreateSampleOrderAction
    participant Inv as SampleInventoryService
    participant Redis as Redis
    participant DB as MySQL
    participant Q as Queue(Delayed 15min)

    C->>Act: execute(customerId, data)
    Act->>Inv: lockStock(productId, qty, orderSn)
    Inv->>Redis: Lua原子DECR+SET锁
    Redis-->>Inv: 成功
    Act->>DB: insert orders(status=100)
    Act->>Q: dispatch ReleaseSampleStockJob(delay=15min)
    Act-->>C: Order

    alt 15分钟内支付
        Q->>Q: 检测到status!=100
        Q->>Q: 跳过释放
    else 15分钟未支付
        Q->>Inv: releaseStock()
        Inv->>Redis: Lua原子INCR+DEL锁
        Q->>DB: update status=105(已取消)
    end
```

---

## 本章自检清单

- [x] 所有代码示例使用 PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13 风格（readonly class、Backed Enum、构造函数属性提升、match表达式）
- [x] 没有出现 Java 特有概念（线程池/CompletableFuture/MyBatis/Spring等）
- [x] 每个子系统包含 Mermaid 图和 PHP 代码示例
- [x] 状态机使用 PHP Backed Enum 实现，内置 canTransitionTo() 方法
- [x] 订单双状态系统正确映射（FM vs nM），modifyStatus独立管理
- [x] 使用 Action 类替代 ServiceImpl，Eloquent Observer 替代 AOP
- [x] 使用 Laravel Event/Listener 替代 Spring EventBus
- [x] 使用 Laravel Queue Job 替代异步线程
- [x] 样品订单独立状态机（100~105）与云仓订单（200~205）完全隔离
- [x] 评价等级保持 PRD 原始定义（4=非常满意、5=不满意）


---

### 6.1-A 公共组件与支撑代码

### A.1 PricingResult 值对象

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\ValueObjects;

use App\Enums\PricingFactor;

class PricingResult
{
    private Money $payable;
    private array $breakdown = [];
    private bool $capped = false;
    private ?int $couponId = null;

    public function __construct(
        public readonly PricingInput $input,
    ) {
        $this->payable = Money::fromYuan(0);
    }

    public function setPayable(Money $amount): void
    {
        $this->payable = $amount;
    }

    public function getPayable(): Money
    {
        return $this->payable;
    }

    public function setBreakdown(PricingFactor $factor, Money $amount): void
    {
        $this->breakdown[$factor->value] = [
            'factor' => $factor->label(),
            'amount_yuan' => $amount->toYuan(),
        ];
    }

    public function getBreakdown(PricingFactor $factor): ?Money
    {
        return isset($this->breakdown[$factor->value])
            ? Money::fromYuan($this->breakdown[$factor->value]['amount_yuan'])
            : null;
    }

    public function getAllBreakdown(): array
    {
        return $this->breakdown;
    }

    public function markCapped(): void
    {
        $this->capped = true;
    }

    public function isCapped(): bool
    {
        return $this->capped;
    }

    public function setCouponId(int $id): void
    {
        $this->couponId = $id;
    }

    public function getCouponId(): ?int
    {
        return $this->couponId;
    }
}
```

### A.2 异常体系

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Exceptions;

use Exception;

class InvalidStateTransitionException extends Exception
{
    public function __construct(string $message = '非法状态流转')
    {
        parent::__construct($message, 422);
    }
}

class BizException extends Exception
{
    public function __construct(
        public readonly string $errorCode,
        string $message,
        int $status = 400,
    ) {
        parent::__construct($message, $status);
    }
}

class CartException extends BizException
{
}
```

### A.3 订单状态变更审计日志Listener

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Listeners;

use App\Events\OrderStatusChanged;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class OrderStatusAuditLog
{
    public function handle(OrderStatusChanged $event): void
    {
        DB::table('audit_logs')->insert([
            'operation_type' => 'ORDER_STATUS_CHANGE',
            'target_id' => $event->order->order_sn,
            'old_value' => $event->oldStatus->value,
            'new_value' => $event->newStatus->value,
            'operator' => $event->operator ?? 'system',
            'remark' => $event->remark,
            'created_at' => now(),
        ]);

        Log::info('[AuditLog] 订单状态变更已记录', [
            'order_sn' => $event->order->order_sn,
            'from' => $event->oldStatus->label(),
            'to' => $event->newStatus->label(),
        ]);
    }
}
```

```php
// database/migrations/2024_01_01_000001_create_carts_table.php

            $table->id()->comment('购物车主键');

            $table->index(['customer_id', 'status'], 'idx_cart_customer_status');

            $table->tinyInteger('is_urgent')->default(0)->comment('是否加急 1=加急');
            $table->tinyInteger('status')->default(1)->comment('1=有效 0=失效（商品下架/参数变更/价格变动）');
            $table->timestamp('expire_at')->nullable()->comment('单项过期时间（默认30天）');
            $table->timestamps();

            // 核心索引：同一购物车同一商品同一规格唯一
            $table->unique(['cart_id', 'product_id', 'cp_summary'], 'uk_cart_item_spec');
            $table->index(['cart_id', 'status'], 'idx_cart_item_cart_status');
            $table->index(['product_id', 'status'], 'idx_cart_item_product_status');
            $table->index('expire_at', 'idx_cart_item_expire');
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('cart_items');
        Schema::dropIfExists('carts');
    }
};
```

```php
<?php

// database/migrations/2024_01_01_000003_create_bestseller_rank_items_table.php
use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
```

```php
<?php

// routes/api.php
use App\Http\Controllers\CartController;
use App\Http\Controllers\CloudBatchController;
use App\Http\Controllers\OrderReviewController;

Route::prefix('api')->group(function () {
    // 6.1 计价引擎
    Route::post('/Calculate', [PricingController::class, 'calculate']);
    Route::post('/Calculate/Batch', [PricingController::class, 'batchCalculate']);
    Route::post('/Calculate/BatchResult/{uuid}', [PricingController::class, 'getBatchResult']);

    // 6.2 购物车（FIX-P0-3: 统一路由）

    Route::post('/Cart/Update', [CartController::class, 'update']);

    Route::post('/Cart/ToggleSelection', [CartController::class, 'toggleSelection']);

    Route::get('/Cart/SelectedItems', [CartController::class, 'selectedItems']);

    Route::post('/Cart/Merge', [CartController::class, 'merge']);            // 登录后合并访客购物车
    Route::post('/Cart/ClearExpired', [CartController::class, 'clearExpired']); // 管理员/系统清理过期项

    // 6.3 热销榜/飙升榜
    Route::get('/Common/GetBestsellerRank', [RankController::class, 'bestseller']);
    Route::get('/Common/GetRisingRank', [RankController::class, 'rising']);

    // 6.4 3D预览

});

// 后台路由
Route::prefix('api/admin')->middleware(['auth:admin'])->group(function () {
    Route::post('/3d/presigned-url', [Preview3DController::class, 'getPresignedUrl']);
```

### A.9 性能优化策略补充

#### A.9.1 计价引擎性能优化

**缓存穿透防护**：当价格配置未找到时，缓存空结果（Null Object Pattern），避免重复查询数据库。

```php
public function getBasePrice(int $productId, string $cpSummary): Money
{
    $cacheKey = "price:base:{$productId}:" . md5($cpSummary);
    
    return $this->cache->remember($cacheKey, now()->addHour(), function () use ($productId, $cpSummary) {
        $row = DB::table('product_price_tiers')
            ->where('product_id', $productId)
            ->where('cp_summary_hash', md5($cpSummary))
            ->first();
        
        return $row ? Money::fromYuan((float) $row->price) : Money::fromYuan(0);
    });
}
```

**缓存雪崩防护**：计价缓存 TTL 增加随机偏移（300~600秒），避免大量缓存同时失效。

```php
$ttl = 3600 + random_int(300, 600);
$this->cache->put($cacheKey, $final, $ttl);
```

#### A.9.2 购物车性能优化

**懒加载失效检测**：购物车列表查询时只做快速计数，失效检测推迟到结算前执行。

```php
public function listWithLazyCheck(int $customerId): array
{
    $items = $this->getItems($customerId);
    
    // 仅标记潜在失效项，不立即删除
    $potentiallyInvalid = [];
    foreach ($items as $item) {
        if ($item->product->status !== 1) {
            $potentiallyInvalid[] = $item->id;
        }
    }
    
    return [
        'items' => $items,
        'potentially_invalid_ids' => $potentiallyInvalid,
        'invalid_warning' => !empty($potentiallyInvalid) ? '部分商品状态已变更，结算前请确认' : null,
    ];
}
```

#### A.9.3 榜单性能优化

**增量更新策略**：每日刷新时，仅对近7天有数据变更的品类执行全量重算，其余品类直接延长Redis TTL。

```php
public function shouldFullRefresh(int $categoryId): bool
{
    $lastRefresh = Redis::get("rank:last_refresh:{$categoryId}");
    if (! $lastRefresh) {
        return true;
    }
    
    $hasRecentChange = DB::table('orders')
        ->where('category_id', $categoryId)
        ->where('created_at', '>=', now()->subDays(7))
        ->exists();
    
    return $hasRecentChange;
}
```

#### A.9.4 状态机性能优化

**状态流转批处理**：MES系统批量上报状态变更时，使用 `updateOrInsert` + `whereIn` 减少数据库往返。

```php
public function batchTransition(array $transitions): void
{
    DB::transaction(function () use ($transitions) {
        foreach ($transitions as $t) {
            Order::where('order_sn', $t['order_sn'])
                ->update([
                    'status' => $t['target_status'],
                    'out_status_name' => OrderStatus::from($t['target_status'])
                        ->toCustomerStatus()
                        ->value,
                    'updated_at' => now(),
                ]);
        }
        
        // 批量触发事件（逐条触发，保证监听器的独立性）
        foreach ($transitions as $transition) {
            event(new OrderStatusChanged($transition['order'], $transition['from'], $transition['to']));
        }
    });
}
```

| 集成测试 | 购物车合并 | 访客+客户数据冲突处理 | Pest/PHPUnit + SQLite |

| 性能测试 | 榜单查询 | ZREVRANGE vs DB回源对比 | Laravel Pulse |

```php
<?php

// tests/Unit/Enums/OrderStatusTest.php
use App\Enums\OrderStatus;

test('已登记可以流转到已审核和已取消', function () {
    expect(OrderStatus::REGISTERED->canTransitionTo(OrderStatus::AUDITED))->toBeTrue();
    expect(OrderStatus::REGISTERED->canTransitionTo(OrderStatus::CANCELLED))->toBeTrue();
    expect(OrderStatus::REGISTERED->canTransitionTo(OrderStatus::COMPLETED))->toBeFalse();
});

test('已完成是终态不可流转', function () {
    foreach (OrderStatus::cases() as $target) {
        expect(OrderStatus::COMPLETED->canTransitionTo($target))->toBeFalse();
    }
});

test('FM到nM映射包含modifyStatus判断', function () {
    $normal = OrderStatus::REGISTERED->toCustomerStatus();
    expect($normal)->toBe(App\Enums\CustomerOrderStatus::PENDING_PAYMENT);
    
    $modifying = OrderStatus::REGISTERED->toCustomerStatus(App\Enums\OrderModifyStatus::FILE_PENDING_MODIFY);
    expect($modifying)->toBe(App\Enums\CustomerOrderStatus::PENDING_MODIFY);
});
```

```php
<?php

// tests/Feature/PricingPipelineTest.php
use App\Pipelines\PricingPipeline;
use App\ValueObjects\PricingInput;
use App\ValueObjects\Money;

test('VIP折扣与样品折扣互斥取最小折扣率', function () {
    $input = new PricingInput(
        productId: 1,
        cpSummary: 'MP:90x54:STANDARD::0:1:PAPER_300G:2:4:500:1',
        quantity: 500,
        customerId: 1,
        vipLevel: 5,
        isSample: true,
    );
    
    $pipeline = PricingPipeline::default(
        app(\App\Repositories\PriceConfigRepository::class),
        app(\App\Repositories\CustomerCouponRepository::class),
        app('cache')
    );
    
    $result = $pipeline->calculate($input);
    
    // Lv5样品折扣0.5，VIP印品折扣0.82，互斥取0.5
    expect($result->isCapped())->toBeFalse();
});
```

---

> **文档信息**  
> 本章编号：第6章（上半部分 6.1-6.10）  
> 技术栈：PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13  
> 编写规范：Action类替代ServiceImpl，Eloquent Observer替代AOP，Laravel Event/Listener替代Spring EventBus，Laravel Queue Job替代异步线程  
> 状态机实现：PHP 8.1 Backed Enum + canTransitionTo() 方法  
> 双状态系统：FM（内部生产状态）→ nM（客户展示状态）通过Enum映射  
> 订单修改流程：IM枚举独立字段，不破坏主状态机  
> 定金子状态：独立字段叠加，由DepositStateManager解析复合展示文本  
> 评价等级：严格遵循PRD定义（4=非常满意、5=不满意）  
> 文件存储：Laravel Storage + MinIO预签名URL  
> 缓存策略：Laravel Cache(Redis)分层缓存，带TTL和主动失效机制  
> 定时任务：Laravel Schedule + withoutOverlapping + onOneServer  
> 异步处理：Laravel Queue + Horizon监控  


---

# 6. 核心业务子系统设计（中半部分：6.11 ~ 6.20）

---

## 6.11 通知系统设计

### 6.11.1 设计概述

通知系统是连接平台与客户的核心纽带，覆盖订单全生命周期、支付、售后、认证、营销等20+业务场景。本系统以 **Laravel Notification** 为架构核心，利用其 `notifiable + channel` 原生机制实现多渠道统一投递，避免自建 `NotifyService` 带来的维护成本。

**核心设计原则**：
1. **渠道解耦**：通过 `via()` 方法动态控制投递渠道，新增渠道无需改动业务代码
2. **模板驱动**：数据库维护通知模板，Blade 引擎渲染，运营可在线编辑文案
3. **去重聚合**：Redis 5分钟去重窗口 + 同订单状态聚合，防止通知轰炸
4. **主备容灾**：短信通道熔断自动切换，保障 P0 通知送达率 ≥ 99.5%
5. **偏好可配**：客户可按类型屏蔽特定渠道，支持通知角标实时刷新

### 6.11.2 架构类图

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class OrderShipped {
        +order: Order
        +expressNo: string
        +via(notifiable) array
        +toDatabase(notifiable) array
        +toMail(notifiable) MailMessage
        +toSms(notifiable) SmsMessage
        +toWechat(notifiable) WechatMessage
    }
    class Customer {
        +notifications: HasMany
        +routeNotificationForSms() string
        +routeNotificationForWechat() string
    }
    class NotificationTemplate {
        +sceneCode: string
        +titleTemplate: string
        +contentTemplate: string
        +channelConfig: json
        +render(array data) array
    }
    class SmsChannelRouter {
        +send(string mobile, string templateCode, array params) SmsResult
        +selectBestChannel() SmsChannelConfig
        +fallbackSend() SmsResult
    }
    class WechatChannel {
        +send(notifiable, notification) void
    }
    class NotificationBadgeService {
        +increment(int customerId) void
        +getUnreadCount(int customerId) int
        +markAllRead(int customerId) void
    }
    class CustomerNotificationPref {
        +customerId: int
        +notifyType: int
        +channelMask: int
        +isEnabled: bool
    }

    OrderShipped --|> Notification
    Customer --|> Notifiable
    OrderShipped --> NotificationTemplate : 读取模板
    OrderShipped --> SmsChannelRouter : 短信投递
    OrderShipped --> WechatChannel : 微信投递
    Customer --> CustomerNotificationPref : 偏好设置
    Customer --> NotificationBadgeService : 角标计数
```

### 6.11.3 通知模板管理

通知模板存储于数据库，支持变量插值与多渠道差异化渲染。运营后台可直接编辑模板内容，无需发布代码。

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Notification\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;

class NotificationTemplate extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'notification_templates';

    protected $casts = [
        'channel_config' => 'array',
    ];

    /**
     * 使用 Blade 语法渲染模板
     */
    public function render(array $data, string $channel): array
    {
        $title = \Blade::render($this->title_template, $data);
        $content = \Blade::render($this->content_template, $data);

        return match ($channel) {
            'database' => ['title' => $title, 'content' => $content, 'type' => $this->scene_code],
            'sms' => ['template_code' => $this->sms_template_code, 'params' => $data],
            'wechat' => ['template_id' => $this->wx_template_id, 'data' => $this->buildWxData($data)],
            default => ['title' => $title, 'content' => $content],
        };
    }

    private function buildWxData(array $data): array
    {
        return [
            'first' => ['value' => $data['title'] ?? ''],
            'keyword1' => ['value' => $data['order_sn'] ?? ''],
            'keyword2' => ['value' => $data['status'] ?? ''],
            'remark' => ['value' => $data['remark'] ?? ''],
        ];
    }
}
```

**模板表示例**：

```sql
CREATE TABLE notification_templates (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    scene_code VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL COMMENT '场景编码: ORDER_SHIPPED/PAYMENT_SUCCESS等',
    scene_name VARCHAR(128) COMMENT '场景名称',
    title_template VARCHAR(256) NOT NULL COMMENT '标题模板(Blade语法)',
    content_template TEXT NOT NULL COMMENT '内容模板(Blade语法)',
    sms_template_code VARCHAR(64) COMMENT '短信通道模板编码',
    wx_template_id VARCHAR(64) COMMENT '微信模板消息ID',
    channel_config JSON COMMENT '渠道配置: {database:true, mail:true, sms:true, wechat:false}',
    notify_type TINYINT DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '通知类型: 1=订单,2=售后,3=系统,4=营销',
    is_enabled TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 1,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE INDEX idx_scene_code(scene_code),
    INDEX idx_notify_type(notify_type)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='通知模板表';
```

### 6.11.4 多渠道通知实现

以 **订单发货通知** 为例，展示 Laravel Notification 的完整实现：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Notifications;

use App\Domains\Notification\Models\NotificationTemplate;
use App\Domains\Order\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Notifications\Notification;
use Illuminate\Notifications\Messages\MailMessage;
use NotificationChannels\Sms\SmsMessage;

class OrderShipped extends Notification
{
    use Queueable;

    public function __construct(
        private Order $order,
        private string $expressNo,
        private ?NotificationTemplate $template = null,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 动态决定投递渠道：优先读取客户偏好，其次读取模板默认配置
     */
    public function via(object $notifiable): array
    {
        $channels = ['database'];

        // 1. 查询客户通知偏好
        $pref = $notifiable->notificationPrefs()
            ->where('notify_type', 1) // 订单类通知
            ->first();

        if ($pref && !$pref->is_enabled) {
            return []; // 客户关闭了订单通知
        }

        $mask = $pref?->channel_mask ?? 15; // 默认全开

        // 2. 按位运算判断渠道
        if ($mask & 2) $channels[] = 'sms';
        if ($mask & 4) $channels[] = 'mail';
        if ($mask & 8) $channels[] = 'wechat';

        return $channels;
    }

    public function toDatabase(object $notifiable): array
    {
        $data = [
            'order_id' => $this->order->id,
            'order_sn' => $this->order->order_sn,
            'express_no' => $this->expressNo,
            'title' => '订单已发货',
            'content' => "您的订单 {$this->order->order_sn} 已发货，快递单号：{$this->expressNo}",
        ];

        if ($this->template) {
            return $this->template->render($data, 'database');
        }

        return $data;
    }

    public function toSms(object $notifiable): SmsMessage
    {
        return SmsMessage::create(
            content: "【怡安印刷】您的订单{$this->order->order_sn}已发货，快递单号：{$this->expressNo}，请注意查收。"
        );
    }

    public function toMail(object $notifiable): MailMessage
    {
        return (new MailMessage)
            ->subject('订单发货通知')
            ->line("您的订单 {$this->order->order_sn} 已发货。")
            ->line("快递公司：{$this->order->express_company}")
            ->line("快递单号：{$this->expressNo}")
            ->action('查看订单', url("/orders/{$this->order->order_sn}"));
    }
}
```

**自定义微信模板消息 Channel**：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Notification\Channels;

use Illuminate\Notifications\Notification;

class WechatChannel
{
    public function __construct(
        private \EasyWeChat\Kernel\Contracts\AccessToken $accessToken,
    ) {}

    public function send(object $notifiable, Notification $notification): void
    {
        $openId = $notifiable->routeNotificationFor('wechat');
        if (!$openId) {
            return;
        }

        $message = $notification->toWechat($notifiable);

        \Http::withToken($this->accessToken->getToken())
            ->post('https://api.weixin.qq.com/cgi-bin/message/template/send', [
                'touser' => $openId,
                'template_id' => $message['template_id'],
                'url' => $message['url'] ?? '',
                'data' => $message['data'],
            ]);
    }
}
```

**通知发送入口（业务层调用）**：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Notification\Actions;

use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Domains\Notification\Models\NotificationTemplate;
use App\Notifications\OrderShipped;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Notification as NotificationFacade;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class SendOrderNotificationAction
{
    /**
     * 统一发送入口，集成去重与偏好过滤
     */
    public function execute(
        int $customerId,
        string $sceneCode,
        array $context,
    ): void {
        $customer = Customer::find($customerId);
        if (!$customer) {
            return;
        }

        // 1. 去重检查：同一客户同一场景同一业务键 5 分钟内只发一次
        $bizKey = $context['biz_key'] ?? $sceneCode;
        $dedupKey = "notify:dedup:{$customerId}:{$sceneCode}:" . md5($bizKey);
        if (Redis::exists($dedupKey)) {
            return;
        }
        Redis::setex($dedupKey, 300, '1');

        // 2. 加载模板
        $template = NotificationTemplate::where('scene_code', $sceneCode)
            ->where('is_enabled', 1)
            ->first();

        // 3. 根据场景构造 Notification 实例
        $notification = match ($sceneCode) {
            'ORDER_SHIPPED' => new OrderShipped($context['order'], $context['express_no'], $template),
            'PAYMENT_SUCCESS' => new \App\Notifications\PaymentSuccess($context['order'], $template),
            'AUTH_APPROVED' => new \App\Notifications\AuthApproved($customer, $template),
            default => throw new \InvalidArgumentException("未知通知场景: {$sceneCode}"),
        };

        // 4. 队列异步投递
        NotificationFacade::send($customer, $notification);

        // 5. 角标 +1
        app(NotificationBadgeService::class)->increment($customerId);
    }
}
```

### 6.11.5 通知去重与聚合

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Notification\Services;

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class NotificationDeduplicator
{
    private const DEDUP_KEY_PREFIX = 'notify:dedup:';
    private const DEDUP_WINDOW = 300; // 5分钟

    public function isDuplicate(int $customerId, string $scene, string $bizKey): bool
    {
        $key = self::DEDUP_KEY_PREFIX . "{$customerId}:{$scene}:" . md5($bizKey);

        if (Redis::exists($key)) {
            return true;
        }

        Redis::setex($key, self::DEDUP_WINDOW, '1');
        return false;
    }

    /**
     * 聚合通知：同一订单的多个状态变更合并为一条
     */
    public function aggregate(array $events): array
    {
        if (count($events) <= 1) {
            return $events[0] ?? [];
        }

        $latest = end($events);
        $history = collect($events)
            ->map(fn($e) => ($e['status_desc'] ?? '') . ' at ' . ($e['time'] ?? ''))
            ->implode("\n");

        return array_merge($latest, [
            'is_aggregated' => true,
            'aggregated_history' => $history,
        ]);
    }
}
```

### 6.11.6 短信备用通道（Channel 级 Fallback）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Notification\Services;

use App\Domains\Notification\Models\SmsChannelConfig;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class SmsChannelRouter
{
    private const FAIL_THRESHOLD = 5;
    private const CIRCUIT_OPEN_SECONDS = 600; // 10分钟熔断

    public function send(string $mobile, string $templateCode, array $params): SmsSendResult
    {
        $channels = SmsChannelConfig::where('status', 1)
            ->orderByDesc('priority')
            ->get();

        if ($channels->isEmpty()) {
            Log::error('[SmsRouter] 无可用短信通道');
            return SmsSendResult::fail('NO_CHANNEL_AVAILABLE');
        }

        foreach ($channels as $channel) {
            if ($this->isCircuitOpen($channel->channel_code)) {
                continue;
            }

            $result = $this->executeSend($channel, $mobile, $templateCode, $params);

            if ($result->isSuccess()) {
                $this->resetFailCount($channel->channel_code);
                return $result;
            }

            $this->incrementFailCount($channel->channel_code);
        }

        return SmsSendResult::fail('ALL_CHANNELS_EXHAUSTED');
    }

    private function executeSend(
        SmsChannelConfig $channel,
        string $mobile,
        string $templateCode,
        array $params,
    ): SmsSendResult {
        $driver = match ($channel->channel_code) {
            'ALIYUN' => app(AliyunSmsDriver::class),
            'TENCENT' => app(TencentSmsDriver::class),
            'CHUANGLAN' => app(ChuanglanSmsDriver::class),
            default => throw new \RuntimeException("未知通道: {$channel->channel_code}"),
        };

        try {
            return $driver->send($mobile, $templateCode, $params);
        } catch (\Throwable $e) {
            Log::error("[SmsRouter] 通道{$channel->channel_code}发送异常", ['error' => $e->getMessage()]);
            return SmsSendResult::fail($e->getMessage());
        }
    }

    private function isCircuitOpen(string $channelCode): bool
    {
        return Redis::exists("sms:circuit:{$channelCode}");
    }

    private function incrementFailCount(string $channelCode): void
    {
        $key = "sms:fail:{$channelCode}";
        $count = Redis::incr($key);
        Redis::expire($key, 300);

        if ($count >= self::FAIL_THRESHOLD) {
            Redis::setex("sms:circuit:{$channelCode}", self::CIRCUIT_OPEN_SECONDS, '1');
            Log::warning("[SmsRouter] 通道{$channelCode}触发熔断");
        }
    }

    private function resetFailCount(string $channelCode): void
    {
        Redis::del("sms:fail:{$channelCode}");
    }
}
```

**短信通道配置表**：

```sql
CREATE TABLE sms_channel_configs (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    channel_code VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL COMMENT '通道编码: ALIYUN/TENCENT/CHUANGLAN',
    channel_name VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL,
    priority INT DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '优先级，越大越优先',
    status TINYINT DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '1启用 0停用',
    channel_type TINYINT DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '1主通道 2备用通道',
    max_retry INT DEFAULT 2,
    qps_limit INT DEFAULT 100,
    daily_limit INT DEFAULT 100000,
    api_endpoint VARCHAR(256),
    api_key_encrypted VARCHAR(256),
    api_secret_encrypted VARCHAR(256),
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE INDEX idx_channel_code(channel_code),
    INDEX idx_status_priority(status, priority)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='短信通道配置表';
```

### 6.11.7 通知角标与未读计数

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Notification\Services;

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class NotificationBadgeService
{
    private const BADGE_KEY = 'notify:badge:%d';

    public function increment(int $customerId): void
    {
        Redis::incr(sprintf(self::BADGE_KEY, $customerId));
    }

    public function getUnreadCount(int $customerId): int
    {
        return (int) Redis::get(sprintf(self::BADGE_KEY, $customerId)) ?: 0;
    }

    public function markAllRead(int $customerId): void
    {
        Redis::del(sprintf(self::BADGE_KEY, $customerId));

        // 同步标记数据库通知为已读
        \DB::table('notifications')
            ->where('notifiable_id', $customerId)
            ->where('notifiable_type', Customer::class)
            ->whereNull('read_at')
            ->update(['read_at' => now()]);
    }
}
```

### 6.11.8 通知偏好设置

```sql
CREATE TABLE customer_notification_prefs (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    customer_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    notify_type TINYINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '1=订单,2=售后,3=系统,4=营销',
    channel_mask TINYINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 15 COMMENT '1=站内信,2=短信,4=邮件,8=微信',
    is_enabled TINYINT DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '0=关闭,1=开启',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE INDEX idx_customer_notify_type(customer_id, notify_type)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='客户通知偏好设置表';
```

### 6.11.9 数据流说明

```
业务事件触发(订单发货/支付成功/审核通过)
    → SendOrderNotificationAction 统一入口
        → 去重检查(Redis 5min 窗口)
        → 偏好过滤(channel_mask & is_enabled)
        → 模板渲染(Blade + 数据库模板表)
        → Laravel Notification::send()
            → via() 决定渠道
                → database: 写入 notifications 表
                → sms: SmsChannelRouter 路由(主备自动切换)
                → mail: Laravel Mail 队列投递
                → wechat: WechatChannel 模板消息
        → 角标 +1 (Redis 原子计数)
        → 发送日志入库
```

---

## 6.12 积分与成长值系统

### 6.12.1 设计概述

积分与成长值系统是客户忠诚度运营的核心载体，承担 **积分获取/消费/过期**、**成长值累计**、**VIP等级自动判定**、**积分兑换商城** 四大职责。系统通过 **Eloquent Observer** 监听订单完成事件自动发放积分，通过 **Laravel Schedule** 定时执行成长值汇总与过期清理。

**VIP折扣规则（PRD v3.0 最终版）**：

| 等级 | 成长值区间 | 印品折扣 | 样品折扣 |
|------|-----------|----------|----------|
| Lv0 | — | — | — |
| Lv1~Lv3 | 0~19,999 | — | **0.9** |
| Lv4 | 20,000~49,999 | — | 无 |
| Lv5 | 50,000~99,999 | — | **0.5** |
| Lv6 | 100,000~199,999 | **0.93** | **无** |
| Lv7 | 200,000~499,999 | **0.92** | **无** |
| Lv8 | ≥500,000 | **0.90** | **无** |

> **关键约束**：Lv1~Lv3 样品 9 折；Lv5 样品 5 折；Lv6~Lv8 **无专属样品折扣**（仅有印品折扣）。v2.9 及更早版本中出现的"Lv4样品8折"、"Lv6~Lv8样品5折"等描述已被 v3.0 删除并修正。

### 6.12.2 核心模型与枚举

```php
<?php

namespace App\Enums;

enum PointType: int
{
    case REGISTER = 1;           // 注册完成
    case FIRST_ORDER = 2;        // 首次下单
    case ORDER_COMPLETED = 3;    // 订单完成
    case DAILY_CHECKIN = 4;      // 每日签到
    case COMMENT = 5;            // 评价订单
    case PROFILE_COMPLETE = 6;   // 完善资料
    case ORDER_DEDUCT = 7;       // 订单抵扣
    case EXCHANGE_GOODS = 8;     // 兑换商品
    case EXPIRED = 9;            // 积分过期
    case ORDER_CANCEL_REFUND = 10; // 取消退积分

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::REGISTER => '注册奖励',
            self::FIRST_ORDER => '首次下单',
            self::ORDER_COMPLETED => '订单完成',
            self::DAILY_CHECKIN => '每日签到',
            self::COMMENT => '订单评价',
            self::PROFILE_COMPLETE => '完善资料',
            self::ORDER_DEDUCT => '订单抵扣',
            self::EXCHANGE_GOODS => '兑换商品',
            self::EXPIRED => '积分过期',
            self::ORDER_CANCEL_REFUND => '取消退回',
        };
    }
}

enum GrowthValueType: int
{
    case ORDER_COMPLETED = 1;
    case COMMENT = 2;
    case CHECKIN = 3;
    case PROFILE_COMPLETE = 4;
    case VIP_PURCHASE = 5;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::ORDER_COMPLETED => '订单完成',
            self::COMMENT => '评价',
            self::CHECKIN => '签到',
            self::PROFILE_COMPLETE => '完善资料',
            self::VIP_PURCHASE => 'VIP购买',
        };
    }
}
```

```php
namespace App\Enums;

/**
```
