### 6.12.3 积分自动发放（Observer + Queue）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Order\Observers;

use App\Domains\Order\Models\Order;
use App\Domains\Point\Jobs\GrantOrderPointJob;
use App\Enums\OrderStatus;

class OrderPointObserver
{
    /**
     * 监听订单状态变更，当订单完成时自动发放积分与成长值
     */
    public function updated(Order $order): void
    {
        if (!$order->isDirty('status')) {
            return;
        }

        // 订单完成 (FM=69)
        if ($order->status === OrderStatus::COMPLETED) {
            // 异步队列发放积分，避免阻塞订单状态更新事务
            GrantOrderPointJob::dispatch($order)->onQueue('points');
        }
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Point\Jobs;

use App\Domains\Order\Models\Order;
use App\Domains\Point\Services\PointGrantService;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

class GrantOrderPointJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public int $tries = 3;

    public function __construct(private Order $order) {}

    public function handle(PointGrantService $service): void
    {
        // 幂等检查：biz_no = order_sn 唯一索引防重发
        $service->grantForOrder($this->order);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Point\Services;

use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Domains\Order\Models\Order;
use App\Domains\Point\Models\PointRecord;
use App\Enums\GrowthValueType;
use App\Enums\PointType;
use App\Enums\VipLevel;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class PointGrantService
{
    public function __construct(
        private GrowthValueService $growthValueService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 订单完成后发放积分与成长值（事务内）
     */
    public function grantForOrder(Order $order): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order) {
            // 1. 计算积分：每100元 +10 积分，向下取整
            $points = (int) ($order->total_price / 100) * 10;
            if ($points <= 0) {
                return;
            }

            // 2. 写入积分流水（负向为消费，正向为获取）
            PointRecord::create([
                'customer_id' => $order->customer_id,
                'point_type' => PointType::ORDER_COMPLETED,
                'points' => $points,
                'balance_after' => $this->addPoints($order->customer_id, $points),
                'source_id' => $order->order_sn,
                'source_type' => 'order',
                'description' => "订单完成获得积分，order_sn={$order->order_sn}",
                'expire_at' => now()->addYear(),
            ]);

            // 3. 同步发放成长值
            $growthValue = (int) ($order->total_price / 100) * 5;
            $this->growthValueService->grant(
                customerId: $order->customer_id,
                growthValue: $growthValue,
                type: GrowthValueType::ORDER_COMPLETED,
                sourceId: $order->order_sn,
            );

            Log::info("[PointGrant] 积分发放成功", [
                'order_sn' => $order->order_sn,
                'points' => $points,
                'growth' => $growthValue,
            ]);
        });
    }

    private function addPoints(int $customerId, int $points): int
    {
        Customer::where('id', $customerId)->increment('point_balance', $points);
        return Customer::where('id', $customerId)->value('point_balance');
    }
}
```

### 6.12.4 成长值计算与VIP等级判定

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Point\Services;

use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Domains\Point\Models\GrowthValueRecord;
use App\Enums\GrowthValueType;
use App\Enums\VipLevel;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

class GrowthValueService
{
    /**
     * 发放成长值并检查VIP等级晋升
     */
    public function grant(
        int $customerId,
        int $growthValue,
        GrowthValueType $type,
        string $sourceId,
        string $description = '',
    ): void {
        if ($growthValue <= 0) {
            return;
        }

        DB::transaction(function () use ($customerId, $growthValue, $type, $sourceId, $description) {
            // 1. 乐观锁更新客户成长值
            Customer::where('id', $customerId)->increment('grow_value', $growthValue);

            $customer = Customer::find($customerId);
            $balanceAfter = $customer->grow_value;

            // 2. 写入成长值流水
            GrowthValueRecord::create([
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'growth_value' => $growthValue,
                'type' => $type,
                'source_id' => $sourceId,
                'balance_after' => $balanceAfter,
                'description' => $description ?: $type->label(),
            ]);

            // 3. VIP等级晋升检查
            $this->checkAndUpgrade($customer);
        });
    }

    /**
     * VIP等级自动晋升
     */
    private function checkAndUpgrade(Customer $customer): void
    {
        $currentLevel = VipLevel::from($customer->vip_level);
        $newLevel = VipLevel::fromGrowthValue($customer->grow_value);

        if ($newLevel->value > $currentLevel->value) {
            $customer->update(['vip_level' => $newLevel->value]);

            // 发送升级通知
            $customer->notify(new \App\Notifications\VipUpgraded($customer, $newLevel));

            \Log::info('[VIP] 等级晋升', [
                'customer_id' => $customer->id,
                'old_level' => $currentLevel->value,
                'new_level' => $newLevel->value,
            ]);
        }
    }

    /**
     * 查询成长值汇总（含升级进度）
     */
    public function summary(int $customerId): array
    {
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);
        $currentLevel = VipLevel::from($customer->vip_level);
        $nextLevel = VipLevel::from($currentLevel->value + 1);

        $thresholds = [
            0, 0, 1_000, 5_000, 20_000, 50_000, 100_000, 200_000, 500_000,
        ];
        $prevMin = $thresholds[$currentLevel->value] ?? 0;
        $nextMin = $thresholds[$nextLevel->value] ?? PHP_INT_MAX;

        $progress = $nextMin === PHP_INT_MAX
            ? 100
            : min(100, (int) (($customer->grow_value - $prevMin) * 100 / max(1, $nextMin - $prevMin)));

        return [
            'current_growth' => $customer->grow_value,
            'vip_level' => $currentLevel->value,
            'vip_level_name' => "Lv{$currentLevel->value}",
            'next_level_min' => $nextMin === PHP_INT_MAX ? null : $nextMin,
            'next_level_name' => $nextMin === PHP_INT_MAX ? null : "Lv{$nextLevel->value}",
            'remaining' => $nextMin === PHP_INT_MAX ? 0 : max(0, $nextMin - $customer->grow_value),
            'progress_percent' => $progress,
            'sample_discount' => $currentLevel->sampleDiscount(),
            'print_discount' => $currentLevel->printDiscount(),
        ];
    }
}
```

### 6.12.5 积分抵扣集成（计价引擎）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Pricing\Steps;

use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Domains\Pricing\Data\PricingContext;
use App\Domains\Point\Services\PointService;

class PointDeductStep
{
    public function __construct(
        private PointService $pointService,
    ) {}

    public function apply(PricingContext $ctx): PricingContext
    {
        if (!$ctx->usePoints) {
            return $ctx;
        }

        $customer = Customer::find($ctx->customerId);
        if (!$customer || $customer->point_balance < config('yian.point.min_deduct_points', 100)) {
            return $ctx;
        }

        $payable = $ctx->productSum + $ctx->expressSum + $ctx->packagingSum - $ctx->discountSum;
        $maxDeductRate = config('yian.point.max_deduct_rate', 10) / 100;
        $exchangeRate = config('yian.point.exchange_rate', 100); // 100积分 = 1元

        $maxDeductAmount = (int) ($payable * $maxDeductRate);
        $maxPoints = $maxDeductAmount * $exchangeRate;

        $actualPoints = min($customer->point_balance, $maxPoints, $ctx->maxDeductPoints ?? PHP_INT_MAX);
        $actualAmount = $actualPoints / $exchangeRate;

        $ctx->pointDeductPoints = $actualPoints;
        $ctx->pointDeductAmount = $actualAmount;
        $ctx->payableAmount = $payable - $actualAmount;

        return $ctx;
    }
}
```

### 6.12.6 积分过期清理（Schedule）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use App\Domains\Point\Models\PointRecord;
use App\Enums\PointType;
use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class PointExpireCommand extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'points:expire';
    protected $description = '清理过期积分';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $expired = PointRecord::where('expire_at', '<', now())
            ->where('status', 0) // 0=未过期
            ->where('points', '>', 0) // 只处理正向积分
            ->limit(500)
            ->get();

        foreach ($expired as $record) {
            DB::transaction(function () use ($record) {
                // 乐观锁：仅当 status=0 时更新
                $updated = PointRecord::where('id', $record->id)
                    ->where('status', 0)
                    ->update(['status' => 1]); // 1=已过期

                if ($updated) {
                    DB::table('customers')
                        ->where('id', $record->customer_id)
                        ->decrement('point_balance', $record->points);

                    PointRecord::create([
                        'customer_id' => $record->customer_id,
                        'point_type' => PointType::EXPIRED,
                        'points' => -$record->points,
                        'balance_after' => DB::table('customers')->where('id', $record->customer_id)->value('point_balance'),
                        'source_id' => $record->source_id,
                        'source_type' => 'expire',
                        'description' => '积分过期扣除',
                    ]);
                }
            });
        }

        Log::info('[PointExpire] 过期积分清理完成', ['count' => $expired->count()]);
        return self::SUCCESS;
    }
}
```

在 `routes/console.php` 中注册定时任务：

```php
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schedule;

Schedule::command('points:expire')->dailyAt('03:00');
```

### 6.12.7 VIP降级检查（Schedule）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Enums\VipLevel;
use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

class VipDowngradeCommand extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'vip:downgrade';
    protected $description = 'VIP等级降级检查（每月1日执行）';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        // 计算有效成长值（排除12个月前的记录）
        $customers = Customer::where('vip_level', '>', 0)->get();

        foreach ($customers as $customer) {
            $validGrowth = DB::table('growth_value_records')
                ->where('customer_id', $customer->id)
                ->where('created_at', '>=', now()->subMonths(12))
                ->sum('growth_value');

            $expectedLevel = VipLevel::fromGrowthValue($validGrowth);

            if ($expectedLevel->value < $customer->vip_level) {
                // 检查宽限期
                if ($customer->vip_grace_end_time && $customer->vip_grace_end_time->isFuture()) {
                    continue;
                }

                $customer->update([
                    'vip_level' => $expectedLevel->value,
                    'vip_grace_end_time' => now()->addDays(30),
                ]);

                $customer->notify(new \App\Notifications\VipDowngraded($customer, $expectedLevel));
            }
        }

        return self::SUCCESS;
    }
}
```

```php
// routes/console.php
Schedule::command('vip:downgrade')->monthlyOn(1, '00:00');
```

## 6.13 客户投诉与工单系统

### 6.13.1 设计概述

工单系统支撑客户投诉、售后沟通、内部问题追踪三类场景。核心设计采用 **PHP Backed Enum** 定义工单状态机，通过 Eloquent 模型访问器自动校验状态流转合法性。SLA 预警通过 Redis 延迟队列 + Schedule 定时扫描双机制保障，工单分配采用 Round Robin 算法结合客服负载均衡。

### 6.13.3 工单模型与多态关联

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Ticket\Models;

use App\Enums\TicketStatus;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\MorphTo;

class Ticket extends Model
{
    protected $casts = [
        'status' => TicketStatus::class,
        'sla_deadline' => 'datetime',
        'assigned_at' => 'datetime',
    ];

    /**
     * 多态关联：支持关联订单/售后/支付
     */
    public function ticketable(): MorphTo
    {
        return $this->morphTo();
    }

    public function replies()
    {
        return $this->hasMany(TicketReply::class);
    }

    public function assignee()
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(\App\Domains\Admin\Models\AdminUser::class, 'assigned_to');
    }

    /**
     * 状态流转封装（自动校验合法性）
     */
    public function transitionTo(TicketStatus $target): void
    {
        throw_unless(
            $this->status->canTransitionTo($target),
            new \InvalidArgumentException(
                "非法状态流转: {$this->status->label()} → {$target->label()}"
            )
        );

        $this->update(['status' => $target]);

        // 触发领域事件
        event(new \App\Domains\Ticket\Events\TicketStatusChanged($this, $target));
    }
}
```

**多态关联的数据库设计**：

```sql
CREATE TABLE tickets (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    ticket_no VARCHAR(32) UNIQUE NOT NULL COMMENT '工单编号',
    customer_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    ticketable_type VARCHAR(64) COMMENT '关联模型: Order/AfterSale/Payment',
    ticketable_id BIGINT UNSIGNED COMMENT '关联模型ID',
    subject VARCHAR(256) NOT NULL COMMENT '工单主题',
    ticket_category TINYINT DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '1=投诉 2=售后 3=支付 4=其他',
    complaint_type TINYINT DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '投诉细分类型',
    priority TINYINT DEFAULT 3 COMMENT '1=紧急 2=高 3=中 4=低',
    status TINYINT DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '0待分配/1处理中/2待复核/3已解决/4已关闭/5已撤诉',
    assigned_to BIGINT UNSIGNED COMMENT '分配客服ID',
    assigned_at DATETIME COMMENT '分配时间',
    sla_deadline DATETIME COMMENT 'SLA截止时间',
    resolved_at DATETIME,
    closed_at DATETIME,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_customer_id(customer_id),
    INDEX idx_status(status),
    INDEX idx_assigned_to(assigned_to),
    INDEX idx_ticketable(ticketable_type, ticketable_id),
    INDEX idx_sla_deadline(sla_deadline),
    INDEX idx_created_at(created_at)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='工单表';

CREATE TABLE ticket_replies (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    ticket_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    sender_type TINYINT NOT NULL COMMENT '1=客户 2=客服 3=系统',
    sender_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    content TEXT,
    attachments JSON,
    is_internal TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '是否内部备注',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_ticket_id(ticket_id),
    INDEX idx_created_at(created_at)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='工单回复记录表';
```

### 6.13.4 工单自动分配（Round Robin + 负载均衡）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Ticket\Services;

use App\Domains\Admin\Models\AdminUser;
use App\Domains\Ticket\Models\Ticket;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class TicketAutoAssigner
{
    private const AGENT_INDEX_KEY = 'ticket:assign:agent_index';

    public function assign(Ticket $ticket): void
    {
        $agents = $this->getAvailableAgents();

        if ($agents->isEmpty()) {
            \Log::warning('[TicketAssign] 无可用客服，工单进入待分配队列', ['ticket_id' => $ticket->id]);
            return;
        }

        // 策略1: 技能匹配（根据工单类型匹配专长客服）
        $skilledAgents = $agents->filter(
            fn($a) => $a->skills->contains($ticket->ticket_category)
        );

        $candidates = $skilledAgents->isNotEmpty() ? $skilledAgents : $agents;

        // 策略2: 负载最低优先（当前处理中工单数最少）
        $bestAgent = $candidates->sortBy(fn($a) => $a->active_tickets_count)->first();

        // 策略3: Round Robin 兜底（Redis 原子递增索引）
        if (!$bestAgent) {
            $index = Redis::incr(self::AGENT_INDEX_KEY) % $agents->count();
            $bestAgent = $agents->values()[$index];
        }

        // 计算 SLA 截止时间
        $slaHours = match ($ticket->priority) {
            1 => 2,   // 紧急
            2 => 4,   // 高
            3 => 24,  // 中
            4 => 72,  // 低
            default => 24,
        };

        $ticket->update([
            'assigned_to' => $bestAgent->id,
            'assigned_at' => now(),
            'status' => \App\Enums\TicketStatus::PROCESSING,
            'sla_deadline' => now()->addHours($slaHours),
        ]);

        // 通知客服
        $bestAgent->notify(new \App\Notifications\TicketAssigned($ticket));
    }

    private function getAvailableAgents()
    {
        return AdminUser::where('status', 1)
            ->where('is_online', 1)
            ->where('department', 'customer_service')
            ->withCount(['tickets as active_tickets_count' => fn($q) =>
                $q->whereIn('status', [0, 1, 2])
            ])
            ->get();
    }
}
```

### 6.13.5 SLA 预警（Redis 延迟队列 + Schedule）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Ticket\Services;

use App\Domains\Ticket\Models\Ticket;
use App\Enums\TicketStatus;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class TicketSlaService
{
    /**
     * 创建工单时推送 SLA 延迟队列
     */
    public function pushSlaQueue(Ticket $ticket): void
    {
        if (!$ticket->sla_deadline) {
            return;
        }

        // Redis Sorted Set: score = 到期时间戳
        Redis::zadd('ticket:sla:queue', $ticket->sla_deadline->timestamp, $ticket->id);
    }

    /**
     * 扫描即将超时和已超时的工单
     */
    public function scanOverdue(): array
    {
        $now = now()->timestamp;
        $approaching = $now + 1800; // 30分钟后

        // 即将超时（30分钟内）
        $approachingIds = Redis::zrangebyscore('ticket:sla:queue', $now, $approaching);

        // 已超时
        $overdueIds = Redis::zrangebyscore('ticket:sla:queue', 0, $now);

        return [
            'approaching' => $approachingIds,
            'overdue' => $overdueIds,
        ];
    }

    public function removeFromQueue(int $ticketId): void
    {
        Redis::zrem('ticket:sla:queue', $ticketId);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use App\Domains\Ticket\Models\Ticket;
use App\Domains\Ticket\Services\TicketSlaService;
use App\Enums\TicketStatus;
use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class TicketSlaMonitorCommand extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'ticket:sla-monitor';
    protected $description = '工单SLA超时监控';

    public function handle(TicketSlaService $slaService): int
    {
        $result = $slaService->scanOverdue();

        // 1. 即将超时预警
        foreach ($result['approaching'] as $ticketId) {
            $ticket = Ticket::find($ticketId);
            if ($ticket && in_array($ticket->status->value, [0, 1])) {
                $ticket->assignee?->notify(new \App\Notifications\TicketSlaApproaching($ticket));
            }
        }

        // 2. 已超时升级
        foreach ($result['overdue'] as $ticketId) {
            $ticket = Ticket::find($ticketId);
            if ($ticket && in_array($ticket->status->value, [0, 1])) {
                // 记录 SLA 告警
                \DB::table('ticket_sla_alerts')->insert([
                    'ticket_id' => $ticket->id,
                    'alert_type' => 2, // 已超时
                    'created_at' => now(),
                ]);

                // 升级到主管
                $supervisor = \App\Domains\Admin\Models\AdminUser::where('is_supervisor', 1)->first();
                $supervisor?->notify(new \App\Notifications\TicketSlaExpired($ticket));

                $slaService->removeFromQueue($ticketId);
            }
        }

        // 3. 固定阈值兜底扫描（Redis故障时）
        $this->scanFixedThreshold();

        Log::info('[TicketSla] 监控完成', [
            'approaching' => count($result['approaching']),
            'overdue' => count($result['overdue']),
        ]);

        return self::SUCCESS;
    }

    private function scanFixedThreshold(): void
    {
        // 超24小时未响应
        Ticket::where('status', TicketStatus::PENDING_ASSIGN)
            ->where('created_at', '<', now()->subHours(24))
            ->each(function ($ticket) {
                event(new \App\Domains\Ticket\Events\TicketNoResponse24H($ticket));
            });

        // 超72小时未处理
        Ticket::whereIn('status', [TicketStatus::PENDING_ASSIGN, TicketStatus::PROCESSING])
            ->where('created_at', '<', now()->subHours(72))
            ->each(function ($ticket) {
                event(new \App\Domains\Ticket\Events\TicketUnresolved72H($ticket));
            });
    }
}
```

```php
// routes/console.php
Schedule::command('ticket:sla-monitor')->everyFifteenMinutes();
```

### 6.13.6 工单处理流程时序图

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant C as 客户
    participant S as 工单系统
    participant A as 分配器
    participant Ag as 客服
    participant Sup as 主管

    C->>S: 提交投诉/售后申请
    S->>S: 创建工单(status=待分配)
    S->>A: 请求自动分配
    A->>A: Round Robin + 负载均衡
    A->>S: 分配客服
    S->>Ag: 通知新工单
    Ag->>S: 开始处理(status=处理中)
    S->>S: 设置SLA截止时间
    loop SLA监控(每15分钟)
        S->>S: 检查超时
        alt 即将超时
            S->>Ag: 预警通知
        else 已超时
            S->>Sup: 升级通知
        end
    end
    Ag->>S: 提交处理结果(status=待复核)
    alt 复核通过
        S->>S: status=已解决
        S->>C: 通知处理结果
        C->>S: 确认关闭(status=已关闭)
    else 复核不通过
        S->>S: status=处理中
        S->>Ag: 退回重处理
    end
```

---

## 6.14 线下门店与O2O服务

### 6.14.1 设计概述

线下门店系统支撑 **门店信息展示**、**最近门店分配**、**门店自提核销**、**自营物流配送** 四大场景。门店分配综合考虑距离、产能、历史匹配度加权评分；自提核销基于二维码/验证码双因子验证；自营配送通过司机App回传GPS轨迹实现全程可视化。

### 6.14.2 门店分配算法

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Store\Services;

use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Domains\Order\Models\Order;
use App\Domains\Store\Models\Store;

class StoreAssignmentService
{
    public function assign(Customer $customer, Order $order): Store
    {
        $candidates = Store::where('status', 1)
            ->where(function ($q) use ($customer) {
                $q->where('city_name', $customer->city_name)
                  ->orWhere('province_name', $customer->province_name);
            })
            ->withCount(['orders as daily_orders' => fn($q) => $q->whereDate('created_at', today())])
            ->get();

        if ($candidates->isEmpty()) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('该区域暂无可用门店');
        }

        $scored = $candidates->map(function (Store $store) use ($customer, $order) {
            $score = 0.0;

            // 距离权重 50%
            if ($customer->lat && $customer->lng && $store->lat && $store->lng) {
                $dist = $this->haversine($customer->lat, $customer->lng, $store->lat, $store->lng);
                $score += (1 / (1 + $dist / 1000)) * 0.5;
            }

            // 产能权重 30%
            $capacityRatio = $store->daily_orders / max(1, $store->capacity_daily);
            $score += (1 - min($capacityRatio, 1)) * 0.3;

            // 历史匹配权重 20%
            $historical = $store->orders()->where('customer_id', $customer->id)->count();
            $score += min($historical / 5.0, 1.0) * 0.2;

            return ['store' => $store, 'score' => $score];
        });

        return $scored->sortByDesc('score')->first()['store'];
    }

    private function haversine(float $lat1, float $lng1, float $lat2, float $lng2): float
    {
        $earthRadius = 6371;
        $dLat = deg2rad($lat2 - $lat1);
        $dLng = deg2rad($lng2 - $lng1);
        $a = sin($dLat / 2) ** 2 +
             cos(deg2rad($lat1)) * cos(deg2rad($lat2)) * sin($dLng / 2) ** 2;
        return 2 * $earthRadius * atan2(sqrt($a), sqrt(1 - $a));
    }
}
```

### 6.14.3 门店自提核销

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Store\Services;

use App\Domains\Order\Models\Order;
use App\Enums\OrderStatus;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;
use Illuminate\Support\Str;
use SimpleSoftwareIO\QrCode\Facades\QrCode;

class StorePickupService
{
    /**
     * 生成自提二维码与验证码
     */
    public function generatePickupCode(Order $order): array
    {
        $code = strtoupper(Str::random(8));
        $qrData = json_encode([
            'order_sn' => $order->order_sn,
            'code' => $code,
            'expire_at' => now()->addDays(7)->timestamp,
        ]);

        Cache::put("pickup:{$order->order_sn}", $code, now()->addDays(7));

        return [
            'verify_code' => $code,
            'qr_code' => QrCode::format('png')->size(300)->generate($qrData),
            'expire_at' => now()->addDays(7),
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 门店核销
     */
    public function verifyPickup(string $input, int $storeId): Order
    {
        // 支持扫码解析或手动输入验证码
        if (str_starts_with($input, '{')) {
            $data = json_decode($input, true);
            $orderSn = $data['order_sn'] ?? '';
            $code = $data['code'] ?? '';
        } else {
            $order = Order::where('pickup_code', $input)->first();
            if (!$order) {
                throw new \InvalidArgumentException('无效的取货码');
            }
            $orderSn = $order->order_sn;
            $code = $input;
        }

        $order = Order::where('order_sn', $orderSn)
            ->where('delivery_type', 3) // 自提
            ->first();

        if (!$order) {
            throw new \InvalidArgumentException('订单不存在或非自提订单');
        }

        $cachedCode = Cache::get("pickup:{$order->order_sn}");
        if (!$cachedCode || $cachedCode !== $code) {
            throw new \InvalidArgumentException('取货码错误或已过期');
        }

        // 核销成功
        $order->update([
            'status' => OrderStatus::COMPLETED,
            'pickup_verified_at' => now(),
            'pickup_store_id' => $storeId,
        ]);

        Cache::forget("pickup:{$order->order_sn}");

        return $order;
    }
}
```

### 6.14.4 自营物流配送轨迹

```sql
CREATE TABLE stores (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    store_code VARCHAR(32) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,
    province_name VARCHAR(32),
    city_name VARCHAR(32),
    county_name VARCHAR(32),
    detail_address VARCHAR(256),
    lat DECIMAL(10, 8),
    lng DECIMAL(11, 8),
    contact_person VARCHAR(64),
    contact_phone VARCHAR(20),
    capacity_daily INT DEFAULT 100 COMMENT '日产能上限',
    status TINYINT DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '1=营业 0=停业',
    open_time VARCHAR(64) COMMENT '营业时间',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_city(status, city_name),
    INDEX idx_location(lat, lng)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='门店信息表';

-- FIX-P0: 门店客户经理表（store_manager_profiles 别名 store_managers）
CREATE TABLE store_managers (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    store_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL,
    mobile_phone VARCHAR(20),
    email VARCHAR(128),
    is_primary TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 0 COMMENT '是否主负责人',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_store_id(store_id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='门店客户经理表';

CREATE TABLE delivery_tracks (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    order_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    driver_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    lat DECIMAL(10, 8) NOT NULL,
    lng DECIMAL(11, 8) NOT NULL,
    address VARCHAR(256),
    speed DECIMAL(5, 2) COMMENT '速度 km/h',
    recorded_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_order_id(order_id),
    INDEX idx_recorded_at(recorded_at)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='配送轨迹表';
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api\Driver;

use App\Domains\Logistics\Models\DeliveryTrack;
use App\Domains\Order\Models\Order;
use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class DriverLocationController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * 司机App上报GPS轨迹
     */
    public function uploadTrack(Request $request)
    {
        $validated = $request->validate([
            'order_id' => ['required', 'exists:orders,id'],
            'lat' => ['required', 'numeric', 'between:-90,90'],
            'lng' => ['required', 'numeric', 'between:-180,180'],
            'speed' => ['nullable', 'numeric'],
        ]);

        DeliveryTrack::create([
            'order_id' => $validated['order_id'],
            'driver_id' => auth('driver')->id(),
            'lat' => $validated['lat'],
            'lng' => $validated['lng'],
            'speed' => $validated['speed'] ?? null,
            'address' => $this->reverseGeocode($validated['lat'], $validated['lng']),
        ]);

        return response()->json(['message' => '位置上报成功']);
    }

    /**
     * 客户查询配送轨迹
     */
    public function getTrack(string $orderSn)
    {
        $order = Order::where('order_sn', $orderSn)
            ->where('customer_id', auth('customer')->id())
            ->firstOrFail();

        $tracks = DeliveryTrack::where('order_id', $order->id)
            ->orderBy('recorded_at')
            ->get(['lat', 'lng', 'address', 'speed', 'recorded_at']);

        return response()->json([
            'order_sn' => $orderSn,
            'current_location' => $tracks->last(),
            'path' => $tracks,
            'estimated_arrival' => $this->estimateArrival($tracks, $order),
        ]);
    }
}
```

## 6.15 系统配置管理

### 6.15.1 设计概述

系统配置管理覆盖 **全局参数**、**功能开关(Feature Flag)**、**维护模式**、**价格策略** 四大维度。配置以数据库为权威源，Laravel Config 缓存为读取加速层，支持热更新无需重启服务。功能开关通过 Middleware 控制接口放行，维护模式支持白名单透传。

### 6.15.2 全局参数配置

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Platform\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

class SystemConfig extends Model
{
    protected $primaryKey = 'config_key';
    public $incrementing = false;
    protected $keyType = 'string';

    protected static function booted(): void
    {
        static::saved(fn() => Cache::forget('system:configs'));
        static::deleted(fn() => Cache::forget('system:configs'));
    }

    public static function get(string $key, mixed $default = null): mixed
    {
        return Cache::remember('system:configs', 60, function () {
            return self::all()->mapWithKeys(
                fn($c) => [$c->config_key => self::castValue($c->config_value, $c->value_type)]
            )->toArray();
        })[$key] ?? $default;
    }

    private static function castValue(string $value, string $type): mixed
    {
        return match ($type) {
            'int' => (int) $value,
            'float' => (float) $value,
            'bool' => in_array($value, ['1', 'true', 'yes'], true),
            'json' => json_decode($value, true),
            'array' => explode(',', $value),
            default => $value,
        };
    }
}
```

```sql
CREATE TABLE system_configs (
    config_key VARCHAR(128) PRIMARY KEY COMMENT '配置键',
    config_value TEXT NOT NULL COMMENT '配置值',
    value_type VARCHAR(16) DEFAULT 'string' COMMENT 'string/int/float/bool/json/array',
    description VARCHAR(256),
    is_editable TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 1,
    category VARCHAR(32) DEFAULT 'general' COMMENT '分类: general/pricing/feature/security',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_category(category)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='系统配置表';
```

### 6.15.3 功能开关（Feature Flag）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Platform\Services;

use App\Domains\Platform\Models\FeatureSwitch;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

class FeatureFlagService
{
    public function isEnabled(string $flag, ?int $customerId = null, ?string $customerGroup = null): bool
    {
        $switch = Cache::remember("feature:{$flag}", 60, function () use ($flag) {
            return FeatureSwitch::where('flag_name', $flag)->first();
        });

        if (!$switch || !$switch->is_enabled) {
            return false;
        }

        // 灰度：按客户ID哈希
        if ($switch->rollout_percent < 100 && $customerId) {
            return (crc32((string) $customerId) % 100) < $switch->rollout_percent;
        }

        // 按客户分组
        if ($switch->target_groups && $customerGroup) {
            return in_array($customerGroup, json_decode($switch->target_groups, true), true);
        }

        return true;
    }
}
```

```sql
CREATE TABLE feature_switches (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    flag_name VARCHAR(64) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    description VARCHAR(256),
    is_enabled TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 0,
    rollout_percent INT DEFAULT 100 COMMENT '灰度百分比 0~100',
    target_groups JSON COMMENT '目标分组白名单',
    start_at DATETIME COMMENT '生效时间',
    end_at DATETIME COMMENT '失效时间',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='功能开关表';
```

**Feature Flag 中间件**：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Middleware;

use App\Domains\Platform\Services\FeatureFlagService;
use Closure;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class FeatureFlagMiddleware
{
    public function __construct(private FeatureFlagService $featureFlag) {}

    public function handle(Request $request, Closure $next, string $flag)
    {
        $customerId = auth('customer')->id();
        $customerGroup = auth('customer')->user()?->customer_group;

        if (!$this->featureFlag->isEnabled($flag, $customerId, $customerGroup)) {
            return response()->json([
                'code' => 403,
                'message' => '该功能暂未开放',
            ], 403);
        }

        return $next($request);
    }
}
```

### 6.15.4 维护模式与白名单

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Middleware;

use Closure;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

class MaintenanceModeMiddleware
{
    public function handle(Request $request, Closure $next)
    {
        // 优先读取 Laravel 内置维护状态
        if (app()->isDownForMaintenance()) {
            $allowedIps = Cache::get('maintenance:allow_ips', []);
            $allowedTokens = Cache::get('maintenance:allow_tokens', []);

            if (
                in_array($request->ip(), $allowedIps, true) ||
                in_array($request->bearerToken(), $allowedTokens, true)
            ) {
                return $next($request);
            }

            return response()->json([
                'code' => 503,
                'message' => '系统维护中，请稍后再试',
                'retry_after' => 300,
            ], 503);
        }

        return $next($request);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

class MaintenanceCommand extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'yian:maintenance
                            {action : up|down}
                            {--ips= : 允许访问的IP，逗号分隔}
                            {--tokens= : 允许访问的Token，逗号分隔}';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $action = $this->argument('action');

        if ($action === 'down') {
            // 调用 Laravel 内置维护
            $this->call('down', ['--render' => 'errors::503']);

            Cache::put('maintenance:allow_ips', explode(',', $this->option('ips') ?? ''), 3600);
            Cache::put('maintenance:allow_tokens', explode(',', $this->option('tokens') ?? ''), 3600);

            $this->info('系统已进入维护模式');
        } else {
            $this->call('up');
            Cache::forget('maintenance:allow_ips');
            Cache::forget('maintenance:allow_tokens');
            $this->info('系统已恢复服务');
        }

        return self::SUCCESS;
    }
}
```

## 6.16 企业认证系统

### 6.16.1 设计概述

企业认证系统覆盖客户从提交资料到审核通过的完整生命周期，状态采用 **kM 枚举体系**（0未提交/1待审核/2通过/3不通过/4驳回/20代认证通过）。证件上传使用 Laravel Storage + 图片压缩，OCR 识别为可选增强。审核流程通过 Eloquent Observer 监听状态变更，自动触发通知与权益刷新。

### 6.16.2 认证状态机（PHP Enum）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Enums;

enum AuthStatus: int
{
    case NOT_SUBMITTED = 0;    // 未提交
    case PENDING_AUDIT = 1;    // 待审核
    case APPROVED = 2;         // 通过
    case REJECTED = 3;         // 不通过
    case DISMISSED = 4;        // 驳回
    case PROXY_APPROVED = 20;  // 代认证通过

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::NOT_SUBMITTED => '未提交',
            self::PENDING_AUDIT => '待审核',
            self::APPROVED => '通过',
            self::REJECTED => '不通过',
            self::DISMISSED => '驳回',
            self::PROXY_APPROVED => '代认证通过',
        };
    }

    public function isAuthenticated(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this->value, [self::APPROVED->value, self::PROXY_APPROVED->value], true);
    }

    public function isResubmittable(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this->value, [
            self::NOT_SUBMITTED->value,
            self::REJECTED->value,
            self::DISMISSED->value,
        ], true);
    }

    /**
     * 允许的状态流转路径
     */
    public function canTransitionTo(self $target): bool
    {
        return match ([$this, $target]) {
            [self::NOT_SUBMITTED, self::PENDING_AUDIT] => true,
            [self::PENDING_AUDIT, self::APPROVED] => true,
            [self::PENDING_AUDIT, self::REJECTED] => true,
            [self::PENDING_AUDIT, self::DISMISSED] => true,
            [self::PENDING_AUDIT, self::PROXY_APPROVED] => true,
            [self::REJECTED, self::PENDING_AUDIT] => true,
            [self::DISMISSED, self::PENDING_AUDIT] => true,
            [self::PROXY_APPROVED, self::APPROVED] => true,
            default => false,
        };
    }
}
```

### 6.16.3 认证资料提交与OCR

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Auth\Actions;

use App\Domains\Auth\Models\AuthAuditLog;
use App\Domains\Auth\Services\OcrService;
use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Enums\AuthStatus;
use Illuminate\Http\UploadedFile;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;

class SubmitCustomerAuthAction
{
    public function __construct(
        private OcrService $ocrService,
    ) {}

    public function execute(int $customerId, array $data): void
    {
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);

        throw_unless(
            AuthStatus::from($customer->auth_status)->isResubmittable(),
            new \InvalidArgumentException('当前认证状态不允许重新提交')
        );

        // 1. 存储证件图片（压缩 + 水印）
        $licensePath = $this->storeAuthImage($data['business_license_img'], $customerId);

        // 2. OCR 自动识别（异步，失败不阻断）
        $ocrResult = null;
        try {
            $ocrResult = $this->ocrService->recognize($licensePath);
        } catch (\Throwable $e) {
            \Log::warning("[AuthOCR] 识别失败，转人工: customerId={$customerId}");
        }

        // 3. 更新客户认证资料
        $customer->update([
            'company_name' => $data['company_name'],
            'credit_code' => $data['credit_code'],
            'legal_person' => $data['legal_person'],
            'legal_person_id_card' => $data['legal_person_id_card'] ?? null,
            'business_license_img' => $licensePath,
            'auth_picture_type' => $data['auth_picture_type'] ?? 1,
            'contact_name' => $data['contact_name'],
            'contact_phone' => $data['contact_phone'],
            'register_address' => $data['register_address'] ?? null,
            'office_address' => $data['office_address'] ?? null,
            'valid_date' => $data['valid_date'] ?? null,
            'ocr_result' => $ocrResult ? json_encode($ocrResult) : null,
            'ocr_verified' => $ocrResult && $this->verifyOcrMatch($ocrResult, $data) ? 1 : 0,
            'auth_status' => AuthStatus::PENDING_AUDIT->value,
        ]);

        \Log::info("[AuthSubmit] 资料提交成功，进入待审核", ['customer_id' => $customerId]);
    }

    private function storeAuthImage(UploadedFile $file, int $customerId): string
    {
        $path = $file->storeAs(
            "auth/{$customerId}",
            'license_' . time() . '.' . $file->getClientOriginalExtension(),
            's3'
        );

        return Storage::disk('s3')->url($path);
    }

    private function verifyOcrMatch(array $ocr, array $data): bool
    {
        return str_contains($ocr['company_name'] ?? '', $data['company_name'])
            || str_contains($ocr['credit_code'] ?? '', $data['credit_code']);
    }
}
```

### 6.16.4 认证审核流程

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Auth\Observers;

use App\Domains\Auth\Models\AuthAuditLog;
use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Enums\AuthStatus;

class CustomerAuthObserver
{
    public function updated(Customer $customer): void
    {
        if (!$customer->isDirty('auth_status')) {
            return;
        }

        $from = AuthStatus::from($customer->getOriginal('auth_status'));
        $to = AuthStatus::from($customer->auth_status);

        // 记录审计日志
        AuthAuditLog::create([
            'customer_id' => $customer->id,
            'before_status' => $from->value,
            'after_status' => $to->value,
            'operator_id' => auth('admin')->id(),
            'reason' => request('reason'),
        ]);

        // 认证通过 / 代认证通过：刷新VIP权益缓存，发送通知
        if ($to->isAuthenticated()) {
            Cache::forget("customer:vip:{$customer->id}");
            $customer->notify(new \App\Notifications\AuthApproved($customer));
        }

        // 不通过 / 驳回：发送通知
        if (in_array($to->value, [AuthStatus::REJECTED->value, AuthStatus::DISMISSED->value], true)) {
            $customer->notify(new \App\Notifications\AuthRejected($customer, request('reason')));
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.16.5 认证权限守卫

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Auth\Services;

use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Enums\AuthStatus;

class AuthGuardService
{
    public function checkInvoiceApply(int $customerId): void
    {
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);
        if (!AuthStatus::from($customer->auth_status)->isAuthenticated()) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('认证通过后方可申请发票', 403);
        }
    }

    public function checkVipDiscount(int $customerId): void
    {
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);
        if (!AuthStatus::from($customer->auth_status)->isAuthenticated()) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('认证通过后方可享受VIP折扣', 403);
        }
    }

    public function isUnAuth(int $customerId): bool
    {
        $customer = Customer::find($customerId);
        return !$customer || !AuthStatus::from($customer->auth_status)->isAuthenticated();
    }
}
```

### 6.16.6 电子签约

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Auth\Actions;

use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Enums\AuthStatus;

class CustomerSignAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId, string $agreementVersion): void
    {
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);

        if (!AuthStatus::from($customer->auth_status)->isAuthenticated()) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('请先完成企业认证再签署协议');
        }

        // 幂等：已签约则直接返回
        if ($customer->signed_time && ($customer->sign & 2) === 2) {
            return;
        }

        $customer->update([
            'signed_time' => now(),
            'sign' => ($customer->sign ?? 0) | 2, // 位1=已签协议
        ]);

        event(new \App\Domains\Auth\Events\CustomerSigned($customerId, $agreementVersion));
    }
}
```

## 6.17 网络异常与降级处理

### 6.17.1 设计概述

网络异常处理系统覆盖 **服务降级**、**熔断保护**、**第三方失败重试**、**限流防刷** 四大场景。通过 Laravel Middleware 实现降级开关控制，自定义 CircuitBreaker 类基于 Redis 计数器实现熔断，第三方服务失败通过 Laravel Queue + Horizon 实现自动重试与死信队列，API 限流使用 Laravel Throttle 中间件。

### 6.17.2 服务降级（Middleware + Config 开关）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Middleware;

use App\Domains\Platform\Models\SystemConfig;
use Closure;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class DegradeMiddleware
{
    public function handle(Request $request, Closure $next, string $feature)
    {
        $isDegraded = SystemConfig::get("degrade.{$feature}", false);

        if ($isDegraded) {
            return match ($feature) {
                'search' => response()->json([
                    'code' => 200,
                    'data' => [],
                    'message' => '搜索服务暂不可用，请稍后重试',
                ]),
                'recommend' => $next($request), // 静默跳过推荐
                'third_party_payment' => response()->json([
                    'code' => 503,
                    'message' => '支付通道维护中，请使用余额支付',
                ], 503),
                default => response()->json([
                    'code' => 503,
                    'message' => '服务暂不可用',
                ], 503),
            };
        }

        return $next($request);
    }
}
```

### 6.17.3 熔断器（Redis 计数器实现）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Platform\Services;

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class CircuitBreaker
{
    private const FAIL_KEY = 'circuit:fail:%s';
    private const STATE_KEY = 'circuit:state:%s';
    private const SUCCESS_KEY = 'circuit:success:%s';

    public function __construct(
        private string $name,
        private int $failThreshold = 5,
        private int $timeoutSeconds = 30,
        private int $halfOpenMaxRequests = 3,
    ) {}

    public function call(callable $callback)
    {
        $state = $this->getState();

        if ($state === 'OPEN') {
            throw new \RuntimeException("[CircuitBreaker] {$this->name} 熔断器已开启");
        }

        try {
            $result = $callback();
            $this->recordSuccess();
            return $result;
        } catch (\Throwable $e) {
            $this->recordFailure();
            throw $e;
        }
    }

    private function getState(): string
    {
        $state = Redis::get(sprintf(self::STATE_KEY, $this->name));

        if ($state === 'OPEN') {
            // 检查是否已过熔断期
            $ttl = Redis::ttl(sprintf(self::STATE_KEY, $this->name));
            if ($ttl <= 0) {
                Redis::setex(sprintf(self::STATE_KEY, $this->name), $this->timeoutSeconds, 'HALF_OPEN');
                Redis::setex(sprintf(self::SUCCESS_KEY, $this->name), $this->timeoutSeconds, '0');
                return 'HALF_OPEN';
            }
            return 'OPEN';
        }

        return $state ?: 'CLOSED';
    }

    private function recordFailure(): void
    {
        $key = sprintf(self::FAIL_KEY, $this->name);
        $count = Redis::incr($key);
        Redis::expire($key, 60);

        if ($count >= $this->failThreshold) {
            Redis::setex(sprintf(self::STATE_KEY, $this->name), $this->timeoutSeconds, 'OPEN');
        }
    }

    private function recordSuccess(): void
    {
        Redis::del(sprintf(self::FAIL_KEY, $this->name));

        $state = $this->getState();
        if ($state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
            $successKey = sprintf(self::SUCCESS_KEY, $this->name);
            $successCount = Redis::incr($successKey);
            if ($successCount >= $this->halfOpenMaxRequests) {
                Redis::del(sprintf(self::STATE_KEY, $this->name));
                Redis::del($successKey);
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.17.4 第三方服务失败重试（Queue + Horizon）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Payment\Jobs;

use App\Domains\Payment\Services\PaymentNotifyService;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

class ProcessPaymentNotifyJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public int $tries = 3;
    public array $backoff = [30, 120, 300]; // 30s, 2min, 5min 退避

    public function __construct(
        private string $gateway,
        private array $notifyData,
    ) {}

    public function handle(PaymentNotifyService $service): void
    {
        $service->process($this->gateway, $this->notifyData);
    }

    /**
     * 失败入死信队列（Horizon 自动处理）
     */
    public function failed(\Throwable $exception): void
    {
        \Log::error('[PaymentNotify] 处理失败，入死信队列', [
            'gateway' => $this->gateway,
            'error' => $exception->getMessage(),
        ]);

        // 写入失败日志表，运营后台可人工处理
        \DB::table('failed_payment_notifies')->insert([
            'gateway' => $this->gateway,
            'payload' => json_encode($this->notifyData),
            'error' => $exception->getMessage(),
            'failed_at' => now(),
        ]);
    }
}
```

### 6.17.5 限流（Laravel Throttle）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Middleware;

use Closure;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\RateLimiter;
use Symfony\Component\HttpFoundation\Response;

class CustomThrottleMiddleware
{
    public function handle(Request $request, Closure $next, string $key = 'default', int $maxAttempts = 60, int $decayMinutes = 1)
    {
        $limitKey = "{$key}:" . $request->ip();

        if (RateLimiter::tooManyAttempts($limitKey, $maxAttempts)) {
            $retryAfter = RateLimiter::availableIn($limitKey);
            return response()->json([
                'code' => 429,
                'message' => '请求过于频繁，请稍后重试',
                'retry_after' => $retryAfter,
            ], Response::HTTP_TOO_MANY_REQUESTS);
        }

        RateLimiter::hit($limitKey, $decayMinutes * 60);

        return $next($request);
    }
}
```

**路由配置**：

```php
// routes/api.php
Route::middleware(['throttle:api'])->group(function () {
    Route::post('/orders', [OrderController::class, 'store']);
});

Route::middleware([CustomThrottleMiddleware::class . ':sms,5,1'])->group(function () {
    Route::post('/common/send-sms-code', [AuthController::class, 'sendSmsCode']);
});
```

### 6.17.6 异常处理矩阵

| 异常场景 | 检测机制 | 降级策略 | 恢复策略 |
|----------|----------|----------|----------|
| API 超时(10s) | Middleware 计时 | 返回友好提示 + 重试按钮 | 指数退避重试 |
| 第三方支付失败 | Queue Job 异常捕获 | 入失败队列，转余额支付 | Horizon 手动重试 |
| 短信通道熔断 | CircuitBreaker 计数 | 自动切换备用通道 | 10分钟后半开探测 |
| Redis 不可用 | Cache 异常捕获 | 直连数据库 + 本地缓存 | 健康检查自动恢复 |
| 搜索服务异常 | Scout 异常捕获 | 降级为 MySQL LIKE 查询 | ES 恢复后自动切换 |

---

## 6.18 客服与帮助系统

### 6.18.1 设计概述

客服与帮助系统由 **在线实时客服**、**AI 知识库问答**、**帮助中心/FAQ** 三大模块组成。在线客服基于 Laravel Reverb（或 Soketi）实现 WebSocket 实时双向通信，消息持久化至 MySQL；客服分配采用负载均衡算法；知识库与 FAQ 使用 Laravel Scout + Meilisearch 实现全文检索。

### 6.18.2 WebSocket 实时客服（Laravel Reverb）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Support\Events;

use App\Domains\Support\Models\ChatMessage;
use Illuminate\Broadcasting\Channel;
use Illuminate\Broadcasting\InteractsWithSockets;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Broadcasting\ShouldBroadcastNow;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Events\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

class MessageSent implements ShouldBroadcastNow
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithSockets, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(public ChatMessage $message) {}

    public function broadcastOn(): array
    {
        return [
            new Channel('chat.session.' . $this->message->session_id),
        ];
    }

    public function broadcastAs(): string
    {
        return 'message.sent';
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api\Support;

use App\Domains\Support\Events\MessageSent;
use App\Domains\Support\Models\ChatMessage;
use App\Domains\Support\Models\ChatSession;
use App\Domains\Support\Services\AgentAllocationService;
use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Broadcast;

class ChatController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        private AgentAllocationService $allocator,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 开始会话
     */
    public function startSession(Request $request)
    {
        $customerId = auth('customer')->id();

        // 检查是否有进行中的会话
        $existing = ChatSession::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', 1)
            ->first();

        if ($existing) {
            return response()->json(['session_id' => $existing->id, 'agent_id' => $existing->agent_id]);
        }

        $alloc = $this->allocator->allocate($customerId);

        $session = ChatSession::create([
            'customer_id' => $customerId,
            'agent_id' => $alloc['agent_id'],
            'status' => $alloc['agent_id'] ? 1 : 0, // 1=进行中, 0=等待中
            'source' => $request->input('source', 1),
        ]);

        if (!$alloc['agent_id']) {
            // 进入排队队列
            \Redis::rpush('support:queue', $customerId);
        }

        return response()->json([
            'session_id' => $session->id,
            'agent_id' => $session->agent_id,
            'estimated_wait' => $alloc['estimated_wait'] ?? 0,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 发送消息
     */
    public function sendMessage(Request $request)
    {
        $validated = $request->validate([
            'session_id' => ['required', 'exists:chat_sessions,id'],
            'content' => ['required', 'string', 'max:2000'],
            'message_type' => ['required', 'in:1,2,3'], // 1=文本 2=图片 3=文件
        ]);

        $session = ChatSession::findOrFail($validated['session_id']);
        $senderType = auth('customer')->check() ? 1 : 2;

        $message = ChatMessage::create([
            'session_id' => $session->id,
            'sender_type' => $senderType,
            'sender_id' => auth('customer')->id(),
            'message_type' => $validated['message_type'],
            'content' => $validated['content'],
            'is_read' => 0,
        ]);

        $session->update(['last_active_at' => now()]);

        // WebSocket 广播
        broadcast(new MessageSent($message))->toOthers();

        return response()->json(['message_id' => $message->id]);
    }
}
```

### 6.18.3 客服分配（负载均衡）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Support\Services;

use App\Domains\Admin\Models\AdminUser;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class AgentAllocationService
{
    private const QUEUE_KEY = 'support:queue';
    private const AGENT_LOAD_KEY = 'support:agent:load:%d';

    public function allocate(int $customerId): array
    {
        $agents = AdminUser::where('status', 1)
            ->where('is_online', 1)
            ->where('department', 'customer_service')
            ->withCount(['chatSessions as active_sessions' => fn($q) =>
                $q->where('status', 1)
            ])
            ->get();

        if ($agents->isEmpty()) {
            return ['agent_id' => null, 'estimated_wait' => $this->estimateWaitTime()];
        }

        // 负载最低优先
        $best = $agents->sortBy('active_sessions')->first();

        Redis::incr(sprintf(self::AGENT_LOAD_KEY, $best->id));

        return ['agent_id' => $best->id, 'estimated_wait' => 0];
    }

    private function estimateWaitTime(): int
    {
        $queueSize = Redis::llen(self::QUEUE_KEY) ?: 0;
        return (int) ($queueSize * 5); // 平均5分钟/会话
    }

    /**
     * 处理排队客户（Schedule 每5秒）
     */
    public function processQueue(): void
    {
        while (true) {
            $customerId = Redis::lpop(self::QUEUE_KEY);
            if (!$customerId) break;

            $alloc = $this->allocate((int) $customerId);
            if ($alloc['agent_id']) {
                ChatSession::where('customer_id', $customerId)
                    ->where('status', 0)
                    ->update([
                        'agent_id' => $alloc['agent_id'],
                        'status' => 1,
                    ]);
            } else {
                Redis::lpush(self::QUEUE_KEY, $customerId);
                break;
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.18.4 知识库/FAQ 全文搜索（Scout + Meilisearch）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Support\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Laravel\Scout\Searchable;

class KnowledgeArticle extends Model
{
    use Searchable;

    protected $fillable = ['category_id', 'title', 'content', 'keywords', 'view_count', 'like_count', 'status'];

    public function toSearchableArray(): array
    {
        return [
            'id' => $this->id,
            'title' => $this->title,
            'content' => strip_tags($this->content),
            'keywords' => $this->keywords,
        ];
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Support\Services;

use App\Domains\Support\Models\KnowledgeArticle;
use Laravel\Scout\Builder;

class KnowledgeSearchService
{
    public function search(string $keyword, ?int $categoryId = null, int $limit = 20): array
    {
        $query = KnowledgeArticle::search($keyword, function (\Meilisearch\Client $client, string $query, array $options) {
            $options['attributesToHighlight'] = ['title', 'content'];
            $options['highlightPreTag'] = '<em>';
            $options['highlightPostTag'] = '</em>';
            return $client->index('knowledge_articles')->search($query, $options);
        });

        if ($categoryId) {
            $query->where('category_id', $categoryId);
        }

        $results = $query->take($limit)->get();

        return $results->map(fn($article) => [
            'id' => $article->id,
            'title' => $article->title,
            'content_snippet' => mb_substr(strip_tags($article->content), 0, 200),
            'view_count' => $article->view_count,
        ])->toArray();
    }

    /**
     * 相似文章推荐
     */
    public function similarArticles(int $articleId, int $limit = 5): array
    {
        $article = KnowledgeArticle::findOrFail($articleId);

        return KnowledgeArticle::search($article->title . ' ' . $article->keywords)
            ->where('id', '!=', $articleId)
            ->take($limit)
            ->get()
            ->toArray();
    }
}
```

### 6.18.5 帮助中心 API

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api\Support;

use App\Domains\Support\Models\HelpFaq;
use App\Domains\Support\Models\KnowledgeArticle;
use App\Domains\Support\Models\KnowledgeCategory;
use App\Domains\Support\Services\KnowledgeSearchService;
use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class HelpCenterController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(private KnowledgeSearchService $searchService) {}

    public function categories()
    {
        $tree = KnowledgeCategory::where('status', 1)
            ->orderBy('sort_order')
            ->get()
            ->toTree();

        return response()->json($tree);
    }

    public function articles(Request $request)
    {
        $articles = KnowledgeArticle::where('status', 1)
            ->when($request->category_id, fn($q) => $q->where('category_id', $request->category_id))
            ->orderByDesc('sort_order')
            ->paginate($request->input('per_page', 20));

        return response()->json($articles);
    }

    public function articleDetail(int $id)
    {
        $article = KnowledgeArticle::findOrFail($id);
        $article->increment('view_count');

        return response()->json([
            'article' => $article,
            'similar' => $this->searchService->similarArticles($id),
        ]);
    }

    public function search(Request $request)
    {
        $request->validate(['keyword' => ['required', 'string', 'min:2']]);

        return response()->json(
            $this->searchService->search($request->keyword, $request->category_id)
        );
    }

    public function hotQuestions()
    {
        $questions = \Cache::remember('help:hot_questions', 3600, function () {
            return KnowledgeArticle::where('status', 1)
                ->orderByDesc('view_count')
                ->take(20)
                ->get(['id', 'title', 'view_count']);
        });

        return response()->json($questions);
    }

    public function likeArticle(int $id)
    {
        KnowledgeArticle::where('id', $id)->increment('like_count');
        return response()->json(['message' => '点赞成功']);
    }
}
```

```php
return new class extends Migration

            $table->timestamp('answered_at')->nullable()->comment('回答时间');
            $table->timestamps();

            $table->index('status');
            $table->index('asked_at');
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('unknown_questions');
    }
};
```

## 6.19 数据备份与恢复

### 6.19.1 设计概述

数据备份策略覆盖 **数据库全量/增量备份**、**文件存储同步**、**恢复演练** 三大维度。数据库备份通过 Laravel Schedule 调用 `mysqldump` 生成 SQL 文件，文件备份通过 Storage 同步至 MinIO 多副本。恢复演练通过 Artisan Command 定期执行，验证备份有效性。

### 6.19.2 数据库备份（Schedule + mysqldump）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;
use Symfony\Component\Process\Process;

class DatabaseBackupCommand extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'backup:database
                            {--type=full : full|incremental}
                            {--tables= : 指定表，逗号分隔}';
    protected $description = '执行数据库备份';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $type = $this->option('type');
        $date = now()->format('Ymd_His');
        $filename = "backup/{$type}/yian_{$type}_{$date}.sql.gz";

        $host = config('database.connections.mysql.host');
        $database = config('database.connections.mysql.database');
        $username = config('database.connections.mysql.username');
        $password = config('database.connections.mysql.password');

        $command = match ($type) {
            'full' => sprintf(
                'mysqldump -h%s -u%s -p%s %s --single-transaction --quick --lock-tables=false | gzip',
                $host, $username, $password, $database
            ),
            'incremental' => $this->buildIncrementalCommand($host, $database, $username, $password),
            default => throw new \InvalidArgumentException('未知备份类型'),
        };

        $process = Process::fromShellCommandline($command);
        $process->setTimeout(3600);
        $process->run();

        if (!$process->isSuccessful()) {
            $this->error('备份失败: ' . $process->getErrorOutput());
            return self::FAILURE;
        }

        // 写入存储
        Storage::disk('backup')->put($filename, $process->getOutput());

        // 清理30天前的备份
        $this->cleanupOldBackups("backup/{$type}");

        $this->info("备份完成: {$filename}");
        return self::SUCCESS;
    }

    private function buildIncrementalCommand(string $host, string $db, string $user, string $pass): string
    {
        $lastBackupTime = $this->getLastBackupTime();
        $tables = $this->option('tables') ?? 'orders,order_items,payments,refunds';

        return sprintf(
            'mysqldump -h%s -u%s -p%s %s %s --where "updated_at > \\"%s\\"" --single-transaction | gzip',
            $host, $user, $pass, $db, str_replace(',', ' ', $tables), $lastBackupTime
        );
    }

    private function getLastBackupTime(): string
    {
        $files = Storage::disk('backup')->files('backup/incremental');
        if (empty($files)) {
            return now()->subDay()->toDateTimeString();
        }
        return now()->parse(basename(last($files), '.sql.gz'))->toDateTimeString();
    }

    private function cleanupOldBackups(string $path): void
    {
        $files = Storage::disk('backup')->files($path);
        foreach ($files as $file) {
            if (Storage::disk('backup')->lastModified($file) < now()->subDays(30)->timestamp) {
                Storage::disk('backup')->delete($file);
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```php
// routes/console.php
Schedule::command('backup:database --type=full')->dailyAt('02:00');
Schedule::command('backup:database --type=incremental --tables=orders,order_items,payments')->everySixHours();
```

### 6.19.3 文件备份（Storage → MinIO）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;

class FileBackupCommand extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'backup:files
                            {--bucket= : 指定桶}';
    protected $description = '同步文件到 MinIO 备份桶';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $sourceDisk = Storage::disk('s3');
        $backupDisk = Storage::disk('minio-backup');

        $files = $sourceDisk->allFiles('uploads');
        $count = 0;

        foreach ($files as $file) {
            if ($backupDisk->exists($file)) {
                continue; // 增量同步
            }

            $content = $sourceDisk->get($file);
            $backupDisk->put($file, $content);
            $count++;
        }

        $this->info("文件同步完成: {$count} 个文件");
        return self::SUCCESS;
    }
}
```

### 6.19.4 恢复演练

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;
use Symfony\Component\Process\Process;

class BackupDrillCommand extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'backup:drill
                            {--date= : 指定恢复日期(YYYYMMDD)}';
    protected $description = '执行季度备份恢复演练';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $date = $this->option('date') ?? now()->subDays(7)->format('Ymd');
        $pattern = "backup/full/yian_full_{$date}*.sql.gz";

        $files = Storage::disk('backup')->files('backup/full');
        $target = collect($files)->first(fn($f) => str_contains($f, $date));

        if (!$target) {
            $this->error("未找到 {$date} 的备份文件");
            return self::FAILURE;
        }

        // 1. 恢复到临时数据库
        $tempDb = 'yian_drill_' . time();
        DB::statement("CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS {$tempDb}");

        $command = sprintf(
            'gunzip < %s | mysql -h%s -u%s -p%s %s',
            Storage::disk('backup')->path($target),
            config('database.connections.mysql.host'),
            config('database.connections.mysql.username'),
            config('database.connections.mysql.password'),
            $tempDb
        );

        $process = Process::fromShellCommandline($command);
        $process->setTimeout(3600);
        $process->run();

        if (!$process->isSuccessful()) {
            $this->error('恢复失败: ' . $process->getErrorOutput());
            DB::statement("DROP DATABASE IF EXISTS {$tempDb}");
            return self::FAILURE;
        }

        // 2. 数据完整性校验
        $tables = DB::select("SELECT COUNT(*) as cnt FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_schema = ?", [$tempDb]);
        $rowCounts = DB::select("SELECT SUM(table_rows) as total FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_schema = ?", [$tempDb]);

        // 3. 业务功能抽样验证
        $validOrders = DB::select("SELECT COUNT(*) as cnt FROM {$tempDb}.orders WHERE status = 69");

        // 4. 清理临时库
        DB::statement("DROP DATABASE IF EXISTS {$tempDb}");

        // 5. 生成报告
        $report = [
            'drill_id' => 'DRILL-' . now()->format('Ymd'),
            'backup_date' => $date,
            'recovery_time_minutes' => $process->getDuration() / 60,
            'tables_count' => $tables[0]->cnt ?? 0,
            'total_rows' => $rowCounts[0]->total ?? 0,
            'valid_orders' => $validOrders[0]->cnt ?? 0,
            'success' => true,
            'created_at' => now(),
        ];

        DB::table('backup_drill_reports')->insert($report);

        $this->info('恢复演练完成，报告已生成');
        return self::SUCCESS;
    }
}
```

```php
// routes/console.php
Schedule::command('backup:files')->dailyAt('03:00');
Schedule::command('backup:drill')->quarterly();
```

### 6.19.5 备份策略矩阵

| 数据类型 | 备份频率 | 保留周期 | 存储位置 | 验证方式 |
|----------|----------|----------|----------|----------|
| MySQL 全量 | 每日 02:00 | 30天 | MinIO 备份桶 | MD5 校验 |
| MySQL 增量 | 每6小时 | 30天 | MinIO 备份桶 | 记录数校验 |
| 文件存储 | 每日 03:00 | 永久 | MinIO 跨区域副本 | 文件 MD5 |
| 恢复演练 | 每季度 | 永久 | 报告表 | 表数/行数/抽样 |

## 6.20 审计日志与合规

### 6.20.1 设计概述

审计日志系统覆盖 **操作日志**、**数据变更追踪**、**异常行为告警**、**日志归档** 四大职责。通过 Eloquent Observer 全局监听 `created/updated/deleted` 事件，自动记录操作人与变更快照。数据变更追踪采用 JSON 差异对比，异常行为通过 Rule 引擎触发 Notification 告警。日志归档通过 Schedule 定时迁移至冷存储。

### 6.20.2 操作日志（Eloquent Observer）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Observers;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Request;

class GlobalAuditObserver
{
    public function created(Model $model): void
    {
        $this->log('CREATE', $model);
    }

    public function updated(Model $model): void
    {
        $this->log('UPDATE', $model, $model->getOriginal(), $model->getChanges());
    }

    public function deleted(Model $model): void
    {
        $this->log('DELETE', $model);
    }

    private function log(string $action, Model $model, array $old = [], array $new = []): void
    {
        // 跳过审计日志表自身和系统表
        if (in_array($model->getTable(), ['audit_logs', 'login_logs', 'data_change_logs', 'tracking_events'])) {
            return;
        }

        $user = auth('customer')->user() ?? auth('admin')->user();

        \DB::table('audit_logs')->insert([
            'operator_id' => $user?->id,
            'operator_type' => $user ? get_class($user) : 'system',
            'operation_type' => $action,
            'target_table' => $model->getTable(),
            'target_id' => $model->getKey(),
            'old_value' => $old ? $this->maskSensitive(json_encode($old)) : null,
            'new_value' => $new ? $this->maskSensitive(json_encode($new)) : null,
            'ip_address' => Request::ip(),
            'user_agent' => substr(Request::userAgent() ?? '', 0, 500),
            'created_at' => now(),
        ]);
    }

    private function maskSensitive(string $json): string
    {
        $fields = ['password', 'pay_password', 'mobile_phone', 'id_card', 'bank_account'];
        foreach ($fields as $field) {
            $json = preg_replace(
                '/"' . $field . '":"[^"]*"/',
                '"' . $field . '":"***"',
                $json
            );
        }
        return $json;
    }
}
```

**在 AppServiceProvider 中注册全局 Observer**：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Providers;

use App\Observers\GlobalAuditObserver;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Support\ServiceProvider;

class AppServiceProvider extends ServiceProvider
{
    public function boot(): void
    {
        Model::observe(GlobalAuditObserver::class);
    }
}
```

### 6.20.3 数据变更追踪（JSON 差异对比）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Audit\Services;

class DataDiffService
{
    /**
     * 计算两个数组的深层差异
     */
    public function diff(array $old, array $new): array
    {
        $changes = [];
        $allKeys = array_unique(array_merge(array_keys($old), array_keys($new)));

        foreach ($allKeys as $key) {
            $oldVal = $old[$key] ?? null;
            $newVal = $new[$key] ?? null;

            if ($oldVal !== $newVal) {
                $changes[$key] = [
                    'old' => $oldVal,
                    'new' => $newVal,
                ];
            }
        }

        return $changes;
    }

    public function format(array $diff): string
    {
        $lines = [];
        foreach ($diff as $key => $change) {
            $lines[] = "{$key}: " . json_encode($change['old']) . ' → ' . json_encode($change['new']);
        }
        return implode("\n", $lines);
    }
}
```

### 6.20.4 异常行为告警（Rule 引擎 + Notification）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Domains\Audit\Services;

use App\Domains\Customer\Models\Customer;
use App\Notifications\AnomalyAlertNotification;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Notification;

class AnomalyDetectionService
{
    private array $rules = [
        'login_fail_burst' => [
            'description' => '登录失败突增',
            'threshold' => 10,
            'window' => 300, // 5分钟
        ],
        'large_order_unusual' => [
            'description' => '异常大额订单',
            'threshold' => 50000,
        ],
        'refund_rate_spike' => [
            'description' => '退款率突增',
            'threshold' => 0.3, // 30%
            'window' => 86400, // 1天
        ],
    ];

    public function scan(): void
    {
        $this->detectLoginFailBurst();
        $this->detectLargeOrderUnusual();
        $this->detectRefundRateSpike();
    }

    private function detectLoginFailBurst(): void
    {
        $results = DB::select("
            SELECT customer_id, COUNT(*) as fail_count
            FROM login_logs
            WHERE login_status = 0
              AND created_at >= DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 5 MINUTE)
            GROUP BY customer_id
            HAVING fail_count >= ?
        ", [$this->rules['login_fail_burst']['threshold']]);

        foreach ($results as $row) {
            $this->alert('login_fail_burst', [
                'customer_id' => $row->customer_id,
                'fail_count' => $row->fail_count,
            ]);
        }
    }

    private function detectLargeOrderUnusual(): void
    {
        $orders = DB::select("
            SELECT id, customer_id, order_sn, total_price
            FROM orders
            WHERE total_price >= ?
              AND created_at >= DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 1 HOUR)
              AND status NOT IN (0, 255)
        ", [$this->rules['large_order_unusual']['threshold']]);

        foreach ($orders as $order) {
            $this->alert('large_order_unusual', (array) $order);
        }
    }

    private function detectRefundRateSpike(): void
    {
        $results = DB::select("
            SELECT customer_id,
                   COUNT(*) as total_orders,
                   SUM(CASE WHEN status = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as cancelled_orders
            FROM orders
            WHERE created_at >= DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 1 DAY)
            GROUP BY customer_id
            HAVING cancelled_orders / total_orders >= ?
        ", [$this->rules['refund_rate_spike']['threshold']]);

        foreach ($results as $row) {
            $this->alert('refund_rate_spike', (array) $row);
        }
    }

    private function alert(string $ruleKey, array $context): void
    {
        $rule = $this->rules[$ruleKey];

        DB::table('anomaly_alerts')->insert([
            'rule_key' => $ruleKey,
            'rule_name' => $rule['description'],
            'context' => json_encode($context),
            'level' => match ($ruleKey) {
                'login_fail_burst' => 2, // 中危
                'large_order_unusual' => 1, // 低危
                'refund_rate_spike' => 3, // 高危
                default => 1,
            },
            'created_at' => now(),
        ]);

        // 通知运营人员
        $admins = \App\Domains\Admin\Models\AdminUser::where('receive_alerts', 1)->get();
        Notification::send($admins, new AnomalyAlertNotification($ruleKey, $rule['description'], $context));
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use App\Domains\Audit\Services\AnomalyDetectionService;
use Illuminate\Console\Command;

class AnomalyScanCommand extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'anomaly:scan';
    protected $description = '扫描异常行为并告警';

    public function handle(AnomalyDetectionService $service): int
    {
        $service->scan();
        $this->info('异常扫描完成');
        return self::SUCCESS;
    }
}
```

```php
// routes/console.php

```

### 6.20.5 日志归档（Schedule 定时冷存储）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;

class LogArchiveCommand extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'logs:archive '
        . '{--table=audit_logs : 归档表名} '
        . '{--days=90 : 归档多久以前的数据}';
    protected $description = '归档审计日志到冷存储';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $table = $this->option('table');
        $days = (int) $this->option('days');
        $cutoff = now()->subDays($days);

        // 1. 导出为 Parquet / JSONL
        $filename = "archive/{$table}/{$table}_{$cutoff->format('Ymd')}.jsonl";
        $batchSize = 1000;
        $offset = 0;

        $stream = fopen('php://temp', 'r+');

        do {
            $rows = DB::table($table)
                ->where('created_at', '<', $cutoff)
                ->orderBy('id')
                ->offset($offset)
                ->limit($batchSize)
                ->get();

            foreach ($rows as $row) {
                fwrite($stream, json_encode($row) . "\n");
            }

            $offset += $batchSize;
        } while ($rows->count() === $batchSize);

        rewind($stream);
        $content = stream_get_contents($stream);
        fclose($stream);

        // 2. 上传冷存储
        Storage::disk('minio-cold')->put($filename, $content);

        // 3. 删除热库已归档数据
        $deleted = DB::table($table)->where('created_at', '<', $cutoff)->delete();

        // 4. 记录归档日志
        DB::table('archive_logs')->insert([
            'table_name' => $table,
            'archived_count' => $deleted,
            'archive_path' => $filename,
            'archived_at' => now(),
        ]);

        $this->info("归档完成: {$table} {$deleted} 条记录 → {$filename}");
        return self::SUCCESS;
    }
}
```

```php
// routes/console.php
Schedule::command('logs:archive --table=audit_logs --days=90')->monthlyOn(1, '04:00');
Schedule::command('logs:archive --table=login_logs --days=90')->monthlyOn(1, '04:30');
Schedule::command('logs:archive --table=data_change_logs --days=90')->monthlyOn(1, '05:00');
```

### 6.20.6 审计日志体系矩阵

| 日志类型 | 表名 | 记录内容 | 保留策略 | 归档目标 |
|----------|------|----------|----------|----------|
| 操作审计 | audit_logs | 操作人/目标表/旧值/新值/IP/UA | 90天热存储 | MinIO 冷存储(JSONL) |
| 登录日志 | login_logs | 登录时间/账号/IP/设备/结果 | 90天热存储 | MinIO 冷存储 |
| 数据变更 | data_change_logs | 表/字段/差异/操作人 | 90天热存储 | MinIO 冷存储 |
| 异常告警 | anomaly_alerts | 规则/上下文/级别 | 1年 | 数据库 |
| 归档索引 | archive_logs | 归档元数据与校验 | 永久 | 数据库 |

### 6.20.7 敏感数据脱敏

```php
<?php

namespace App\Support;

class SensitiveDataMasker
{
    public static function phone(string $phone): string
    {
        if (strlen($phone) !== 11) return $phone;
        return substr($phone, 0, 3) . '****' . substr($phone, 7);
    }

    public static function idCard(string $idCard): string
    {
        if (strlen($idCard) < 8) return $idCard;
        return substr($idCard, 0, 3) . str_repeat('*', strlen($idCard) - 7) . substr($idCard, -4);
    }

    public static function address(string $address): string
    {
        $districtIdx = max(mb_strpos($address, '区'), mb_strpos($address, '县'));
        if ($districtIdx > 0) {
            return mb_substr($address, 0, $districtIdx + 1) . '****';
        }
        return mb_substr($address, 0, 6) . '****';
    }

    public static function token(string $token): string
    {
        if (strlen($token) <= 20) return $token;
        return substr($token, 0, 10) . '...' . substr($token, -5);
    }
}
```
