# 6 核心业务子系统设计（续）

---

## 6.21 用户行为埋点子系统设计

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块二十（管理后台，FR-ADMIN-071~077）、附录 API 清单（`/api/app/collect/user-event`、`/api/app/collect/user-events`）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Admin\Tracking`（管理后台 — 数据埋点域）  
> **核心数据表**：`user_behavior_tracks`

### 6.21.1 设计概述

怡安印刷商城采用前端采集 + 后端异步持久化的埋点架构。前端通过统一的 Tracker SDK 收集用户行为事件（页面浏览、按钮点击、商品曝光、订单转化漏斗等），以 `batchSize=5` 为阈值批量上报至后端接收接口。后端通过 Laravel Queue 将埋点数据异步写入 `user_behavior_tracks` 表，避免高频写操作阻塞主业务请求。

**核心设计原则**：
- **批量聚合**：前端队列满 5 条或 10 秒超时自动上报，减少 HTTP 请求次数
- **异步解耦**：接收接口仅做校验和入队，实际持久化由 Queue Worker 完成
- **隐私合规**：敏感字段（手机号、客户名、IP）通过 Laravel Encrypter 加密存储，前端展示时脱敏
- **会话追踪**：`tracker_session_id` 串联单次访问的完整行为路径，支持转化漏斗分析

### 6.21.2 系统架构与数据流

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[前端Vue3 SPA] -->|批量上报 batchSize=5| B["POST /api/app/collect/user-events"]
    B --> C[TrackCollectController]
    C --> D{校验+脱敏}
    D --> E[Laravel Queue Redis]
    E --> F[PersistTrackBatchJob]
    F --> G[(user_behavior_tracks)]
    F --> H[ClickHouse/ES<br/>可选离线分析]
    G --> I[管理后台<br/>转化漏斗报表]
```

### 6.21.3 数据模型设计

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Admin;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Casts\Attribute;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Crypt;

/**
 * 用户行为埋点表
 * 支持 JSON 扩展字段存储动态事件属性
 */
class UserBehaviorTrack extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'user_behavior_tracks';

    protected $casts = [
        'props' => 'array',
        'context' => 'array',
        'client_time' => 'datetime',
        'server_time' => 'datetime',
    ];

    /**
     * 敏感字段加密存储（手机号）
     */
    protected function clientPhone(): Attribute
    {
        return Attribute::make(
            get: fn (?string $value) => $value ? Crypt::decryptString($value) : null,
            set: fn (?string $value) => $value ? Crypt::encryptString($value) : null,
        );
    }

    /**
     * 敏感字段脱敏展示 Accessor
     */
    protected function clientPhoneMasked(): Attribute
    {
        return Attribute::make(
            get: function () {
                $phone = $this->client_phone;
                if (!$phone || strlen($phone) < 7) {
                    return $phone;
                }
                return substr($phone, 0, 3) . '****' . substr($phone, -4);
            },
        );
    }

    /**
     * 作用域：按会话查询完整路径
     */
    public function scopeBySession($query, string $sessionId)
    {
        return $query->where('session_id', $sessionId)
                     ->orderBy('client_time');
    }

    /**
     * 作用域：按事件类型筛选
     */
    public function scopeEventType($query, string $eventType)
    {
        return $query->where('event_type', $eventType);
    }
}
```

**表结构（Migration）**：

```php
<?php

use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schema;

return new class extends Migration
{
    public function up(): void
    {
        Schema::create('user_behavior_tracks', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id();
            $table->string('app_id', 32)->default('yian')->comment('应用标识');
            $table->string('event_type', 64)->comment('事件类型: page_view/click/expose/custom');
            $table->string('event_id', 128)->comment('事件唯一标识');
            $table->string('session_id', 128)->comment('tracker_session_id 会话标识');
            $table->unsignedBigInteger('customer_id')->nullable()->comment('客户ID（登录后）');
            $table->string('page_url', 512)->nullable()->comment('页面URL');
            $table->string('referrer', 512)->nullable()->comment('来源页面');
            $table->string('client_phone')->nullable()->comment('手机号（加密）');
            $table->ipAddress('client_ip')->nullable()->comment('客户端IP');
            $table->string('user_agent', 512)->nullable()->comment('UA');
            $table->json('props')->nullable()->comment('事件属性（动态JSON）');
            $table->json('context')->nullable()->comment('上下文信息: device/os/resolution');
            $table->dateTime('client_time')->comment('客户端事件发生时间');
            $table->dateTime('server_time')->useCurrent()->comment('服务端接收时间');

            $table->index(['session_id', 'client_time'], 'idx_session_time');
            $table->index(['event_type', 'created_at'], 'idx_event_time');
            $table->index('customer_id');
        });
    }
};
```

### 6.21.4 Tracker配置与批量上报

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api\Admin;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Requests\Admin\TrackCollectRequest;
use App\Jobs\Admin\PersistTrackBatchJob;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Validator;

class TrackCollectController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * 批量埋点上报接口
     * POST /api/app/collect/user-events
     */
    public function collectBatch(TrackCollectRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $events = $request->validated('events');
        $sessionId = $request->header('X-Tracker-Session-Id', $request->validated('session_id'));

        // 批量脱敏后入队
        $sanitizedEvents = array_map(
            fn (array $event) => $this->sanitizeEvent($event, $sessionId),
            $events
        );

        // 异步持久化
        PersistTrackBatchJob::dispatch($sanitizedEvents);

        return response()->json(['success' => true, 'received' => count($events)]);
    }

    /**
     * 单条埋点上报接口（降级兜底）
     * POST /api/app/collect/user-event
     */
    public function collectSingle(TrackCollectRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $event = $request->validated();
        $sessionId = $request->header('X-Tracker-Session-Id', $event['session_id'] ?? null);

        PersistTrackBatchJob::dispatch([$this->sanitizeEvent($event, $sessionId)]);

        return response()->json(['success' => true]);
    }

    /**
     * 敏感字段脱敏处理
     */
    private function sanitizeEvent(array $event, ?string $sessionId): array
    {
        $event['session_id'] = $sessionId ?? ($event['session_id'] ?? 'unknown');
        $event['server_time'] = now()->toDateTimeString();

        // 移除或哈希化极端敏感字段
        if (isset($event['props']['password'])) {
            unset($event['props']['password']);
        }
        if (isset($event['props']['phone'])) {
            $event['client_phone'] = $event['props']['phone'];
            $event['props']['phone'] = substr($event['props']['phone'], 0, 3) . '****' . substr($event['props']['phone'], -4);
        }

        return $event;
    }
}
```

### 6.21.5 Queue Job 异步写入

```php
<?php

namespace App\Jobs\Admin;

use App\Models\Admin\UserBehaviorTrack;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Crypt;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class PersistTrackBatchJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public int $tries = 3;
    public int $backoff = [10, 30, 60];

    public function __construct(private array $events) {}

    public function handle(): void
    {
        if (empty($this->events)) {
            return;
        }

        // 批量插入提升性能
        $records = array_map(fn (array $event) => [
            'app_id' => $event['app_id'] ?? 'yian',
            'event_type' => $event['event_type'],
            'event_id' => $event['event_id'] ?? uniqid('evt_', true),
            'session_id' => $event['session_id'],
            'customer_id' => $event['customer_id'] ?? null,
            'page_url' => $event['page_url'] ?? null,
            'referrer' => $event['referrer'] ?? null,
            'client_phone' => isset($event['client_phone'])
                ? Crypt::encryptString($event['client_phone'])
                : null,
            'client_ip' => $event['client_ip'] ?? null,
            'user_agent' => $event['user_agent'] ?? null,
            'props' => json_encode($event['props'] ?? []),
            'context' => json_encode($event['context'] ?? []),
            'client_time' => $event['client_time'] ?? now(),
            'server_time' => $event['server_time'] ?? now(),
            'created_at' => now(),
        ], $this->events);

        try {
            DB::transaction(function () use ($records) {
                UserBehaviorTrack::insert($records);
            });
        } catch (\Throwable $e) {
            Log::error('埋点批量写入失败', [
                'count' => count($records),
                'error' => $e->getMessage(),
            ]);
            throw $e; // 触发重试
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.21.6 类图

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class TrackCollectController {
        +collectBatch(TrackCollectRequest): JsonResponse
        +collectSingle(TrackCollectRequest): JsonResponse
        -sanitizeEvent(array, string): array
    }
    class PersistTrackBatchJob {
        +handle(): void
    }
    class UserBehaviorTrack {
        +casts: array
        +clientPhone(): Attribute
        +clientPhoneMasked(): Attribute
        +scopeBySession(query, string)
        +scopeEventType(query, string)
    }
    class TrackCollectRequest {
        +rules(): array
    }

    TrackCollectController --> PersistTrackBatchJob : dispatch
    PersistTrackBatchJob --> UserBehaviorTrack : batch insert
    TrackCollectController ..> TrackCollectRequest : validates
```

### 6.21.7 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 批量阈值 5 条 | 前端 Tracker SDK 队列控制 | `batchSize: 5`，`flushInterval: 10000` |
| 页面关闭强制上报 | `beforeunload` 事件监听 | 避免未达阈值的数据丢失 |
| 敏感字段加密 | `Crypt::encryptString()` | 手机号等 PII 数据加密存储 |
| 脱敏展示 | `clientPhoneMasked` Accessor | 前端报表展示时自动脱敏 |
| 异常容错 | Job `tries=3` + `backoff` | 数据库瞬时故障可自动重试 |

---

## 6.22 发票管理状态机子系统设计

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块十三（发票管理，FR-INV-001~016）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Order\Invoice`（订单域 — 发票子域）  
> **核心数据表**：`invoices`、`invoice_titles`、`invoice_red_records`

### 6.22.1 设计概述

发票管理是 B2B 电商平台的核心财务功能。本系统采用 **PHP Backed Enum 驱动状态机** 管理发票全生命周期，覆盖从客户申请、运营审核、财务开票到快递邮寄/电子发票下载的完整流程。支持正常蓝字发票、负数发票（部分红冲）、全部红冲三种业务类型，并通过 Eloquent Observer 实现状态变更的自动通知。

**发票状态机（InvoiceStatus Enum）**：

```
已申请(1) --审核通过--> 已审核(2) --开票完成--> 已开票(4) --打印快递单--> 已打印快递单(5)
    |                        |
    +--审核驳回--> 已驳回(3)  +--作废/红冲--> 已作废(6)
    |
    +--客户取消--> 已取消(0)
```

### 6.22.3 发票业务类型 Enum

```php
<?php

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 发票业务类型
 * 0未指定 / 1正常发票 / 2负数发票 / 3全部红冲
 */
enum InvoiceBusinessType: int
{
    case UNSPECIFIED = 0;
    case NORMAL = 1;
    case NEGATIVE = 2;
    case FULL_RED = 3;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::UNSPECIFIED => '未指定',
            self::NORMAL => '正常发票',
            self::NEGATIVE => '负数发票',
            self::FULL_RED => '全部红冲',
        };
    }
}
```

### 6.22.3.1 发票分类 Enum（税务类型）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 发票分类（税务类型）
 * 对应PRD v2.7字段拆分后的 invoice_category
 */
enum InvoiceCategory: int
{
    case NORMAL = 1;      // 增值税普通发票
    case SPECIAL = 2;     // 增值税专用发票
    case ELECTRONIC = 3;  // 电子普通发票

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::NORMAL => '增值税普通发票',
            self::SPECIAL => '增值税专用发票',
            self::ELECTRONIC => '电子普通发票',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否需要填写完整企业信息（专票必填）
     */
    public function requiresFullCompanyInfo(): bool
    {
        return $this === self::SPECIAL;
    }
}
```

### 6.22.4 Eloquent 模型与 Observer

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Order;

use App\Enums\InvoiceStatus;
use App\Enums\InvoiceBusinessType;
use App\Events\InvoiceStatusChanged;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasOne;

class Invoice extends Model
{
    protected $casts = [
        'status' => InvoiceStatus::class,
        'business_type' => InvoiceBusinessType::class,
        'amount' => MoneyCast::class,
        'issued_at' => 'datetime',
    ];

    protected static function booted(): void
    {
        static::updated(function (Invoice $invoice) {
            if ($invoice->isDirty('status')) {
                event(new InvoiceStatusChanged(
                    $invoice,
                    $invoice->getOriginal('status'),
                    $invoice->status
                ));
            }
        });
    }

    /**
     * 安全的状态流转方法
     */
    public function transitionTo(InvoiceStatus $target, ?string $remark = null): void
    {
        throw_unless(
            $this->status->canTransitionTo($target),
            \App\Exceptions\InvalidStateTransitionException::class,
            "发票状态无法从 {$this->status->label()} 流转到 {$target->label()}"
        );

        $this->update([
            'status' => $target,
            'status_remark' => $remark,
            'issued_at' => $target === InvoiceStatus::ISSUED ? now() : $this->issued_at,
        ]);
    }

    public function order(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Order::class);
    }

    public function title(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(InvoiceTitle::class, 'invoice_title_id');
    }

    public function redRecord(): HasOne
    {
        return $this->hasOne(InvoiceRedRecord::class, 'original_invoice_id');
    }
}
```

**Observer 自动通知**：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Observers;

use App\Enums\InvoiceStatus;
use App\Events\InvoiceStatusChanged;
use App\Models\Order\Invoice;
use App\Notifications\InvoiceStatusNotification;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class InvoiceObserver
{
    /**
     * 监听状态变更事件，自动通知客户
     */
    public function handleStatusChanged(InvoiceStatusChanged $event): void
    {
        $invoice = $event->invoice;
        $oldStatus = $event->oldStatus;
        $newStatus = $event->newStatus;

        Log::info('发票状态变更', [
            'invoice_id' => $invoice->id,
            'order_id' => $invoice->order_id,
            'from' => $oldStatus?->label(),
            'to' => $newStatus->label(),
        ]);

        // 终态或关键状态变更时通知客户
        if ($newStatus->isTerminal() || in_array($newStatus, [
            InvoiceStatus::AUDITED,
            InvoiceStatus::REJECTED,
            InvoiceStatus::ISSUED,
        ], true)) {
            $invoice->order->customer->notify(
                new InvoiceStatusNotification($invoice, $oldStatus, $newStatus)
            );
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.22.5 红冲流程 Action

```php
<?php

namespace App\Actions\Order\Invoice;

use App\Enums\InvoiceBusinessType;
use App\Enums\InvoiceStatus;
use App\Models\Order\Invoice;
use App\Models\Order\InvoiceRedRecord;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

/**
 * 发票红冲/作废 Action
 * 原发票作废 + 新开负数发票（如需）
 */
class RedInvoiceAction
{
    public function execute(
        Invoice $originalInvoice,
        InvoiceBusinessType $redType,
        ?float $redAmount = null,
        ?string $reason = null
    ): Invoice {
        return DB::transaction(function () use ($originalInvoice, $redType, $redAmount, $reason) {
            // 1. 校验原发票状态
            if ($originalInvoice->status !== InvoiceStatus::ISSUED
                && $originalInvoice->status !== InvoiceStatus::EXPRESS_PRINTED
            ) {
                throw new \InvalidArgumentException('仅已开票状态的发票可红冲');
            }

            // 2. 原发票作废
            $originalInvoice->transitionTo(InvoiceStatus::VOIDED, $reason);

            // 3. 创建红冲记录
            InvoiceRedRecord::create([
                'original_invoice_id' => $originalInvoice->id,
                'red_type' => $redType,
                'red_amount' => $redAmount ?? $originalInvoice->amount,
                'reason' => $reason,
                'operator_id' => auth('admin')->id(),
            ]);

            // 4. 部分红冲或全部红冲时，新开负数发票
            if ($redType === InvoiceBusinessType::NEGATIVE
                || $redType === InvoiceBusinessType::FULL_RED
            ) {
                $negativeInvoice = Invoice::create([
                    'order_id' => $originalInvoice->order_id,
                    'customer_id' => $originalInvoice->customer_id,
                    'invoice_title_id' => $originalInvoice->invoice_title_id,
                    'amount' => -($redAmount ?? $originalInvoice->amount),
                    'status' => InvoiceStatus::ISSUED,
                    'business_type' => $redType,
                    'category' => $originalInvoice->category,
                    'remark' => "红冲原发票 #{$originalInvoice->invoice_no}, 原因: {$reason}",
                    'issued_at' => now(),
                ]);

                return $negativeInvoice;
            }

            return $originalInvoice;
        });
    }
}
```

### 6.22.6 类图与时序图

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Invoice {
        +casts: array
        +transitionTo(InvoiceStatus, string)
        +order(): BelongsTo
        +title(): BelongsTo
        +redRecord(): HasOne
    }
    class InvoiceStatus {
        <<enumeration>>
        CANCELLED=0
        APPLIED=1
        AUDITED=2
        REJECTED=3
        ISSUED=4
        EXPRESS_PRINTED=5
        VOIDED=6
        +label(): string
        +canTransitionTo(InvoiceStatus): bool
        +isTerminal(): bool
    }
    class InvoiceBusinessType {
        <<enumeration>>
        UNSPECIFIED=0
        NORMAL=1
        NEGATIVE=2
        FULL_RED=3
    }
    class RedInvoiceAction {
        +execute(Invoice, InvoiceBusinessType, float, string): Invoice
    }
    class InvoiceObserver {
        +handleStatusChanged(InvoiceStatusChanged): void
    }
    class InvoiceStatusNotification {
        +via(notifiable): array
        +toDatabase(notifiable): array
    }

    Invoice --> InvoiceStatus : uses
    Invoice --> InvoiceBusinessType : uses
    RedInvoiceAction --> Invoice : operates
    InvoiceObserver --> InvoiceStatusNotification : triggers
```

**红冲流程时序图**：

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Admin as 财务人员
    participant Controller as InvoiceController
    participant Action as RedInvoiceAction
    participant DB as 数据库

    Admin->>Controller: POST /api/admin/invoices/{id}/red
    Controller->>Action: execute(originalInvoice, NEGATIVE, amount, reason)
    Action->>DB: 开启事务
    Action->>DB: 原发票 status -> VOIDED
    Action->>DB: 创建 invoice_red_records
    Action->>DB: 创建负数发票 amount = -amount
    Action->>DB: 提交事务
    Action-->>Controller: 返回负数发票
    Controller-->>Admin: 200 OK
```

### 6.22.7 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 错误码 |
|------|------|--------|
| 状态机强制校验 | `InvoiceStatus::canTransitionTo()` | `INVALID_STATE_TRANSITION` |
| 仅已开票可红冲 | 执行前状态校验 | `INVOICE_NOT_ISSUED` |
| 客户仅可取消已申请 | Gate 策略拦截 | `UNAUTHORIZED` |
| 审核驳回需填写原因 | FormRequest `required_if` 规则 | `REJECT_REASON_REQUIRED` |
| 状态变更自动通知 | Observer + Notification | — |

---

## 6.23 库存锁定服务子系统设计

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块十九（FR-ADMIN-050~055）、FR-ORDER-004（云仓下单）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Product\Inventory`（商品域 — 库存子域）  
> **核心数据表**：`cloud_warehouse_inventory`、`inventory_lock_logs`

### 6.23.1 设计概述

云仓订单采用 **库存锁定 → 支付扣减 → 取消释放** 的三阶段库存管理模型。客户下单后，系统通过 Redis Lua 原子脚本锁定库存 30 分钟；支付成功后通过数据库事务正式扣减库存；若超时未支付或订单取消，则通过 Event Listener 自动释放锁定。

**核心原则**：
- **下单只锁定，不扣减**：防止未支付订单占用真实库存
- **Redis 原子操作**：Lua 脚本保证 `GET → 校验 → DECR` 的原子性
- **延迟释放队列**：Laravel Delayed Job 在 30 分钟后自动检查并释放超时锁定
- **事件驱动释放**：订单取消/支付超时通过 Event 触发库存回滚

### 6.23.2 Redis Lua 原子脚本

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Product\Inventory;

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class InventoryLockService
{
    private const LOCK_TTL_SECONDS = 1800; // 30分钟
    private const LOCK_PREFIX = 'inventory:lock:';
    private const STOCK_PREFIX = 'inventory:stock:';

    /**
     * 使用 Lua 脚本原子锁定库存
     */
    public function lock(int $skuId, int $quantity, int $orderId): bool
    {
        $stockKey = self::STOCK_PREFIX . $skuId;
        $lockKey = self::LOCK_PREFIX . $orderId . ':' . $skuId;

        $lua = <<<'LUA'
local stockKey = KEYS[1]
local lockKey = KEYS[2]
local quantity = tonumber(ARGV[1])
local ttl = tonumber(ARGV[2])
local lockValue = ARGV[3]

local stock = redis.call('GET', stockKey)
if not stock then
    return {-1, "STOCK_NOT_FOUND"}
end

stock = tonumber(stock)
if stock < quantity then
    return {-2, "INSUFFICIENT_STOCK"}
end

-- 扣减可用库存并记录锁定
redis.call('DECRBY', stockKey, quantity)
redis.call('SETEX', lockKey, ttl, lockValue)

return {1, "OK"}
LUA;

        $lockValue = json_encode([
            'order_id' => $orderId,
            'sku_id' => $skuId,
            'quantity' => $quantity,
            'locked_at' => now()->toDateTimeString(),
        ]);

        $result = Redis::eval($lua, 2, $stockKey, $lockKey, $quantity, self::LOCK_TTL_SECONDS, $lockValue);

        if ($result[0] === 1) {
            // 记录锁定日志到数据库（异步）
            \App\Jobs\Product\RecordInventoryLockJob::dispatch($skuId, $orderId, $quantity, 'lock');
            return true;
        }

        throw match ($result[1]) {
            'STOCK_NOT_FOUND' => new \RuntimeException('库存数据未初始化'),
            'INSUFFICIENT_STOCK' => new \RuntimeException('库存不足'),
            default => new \RuntimeException('库存锁定失败'),
        };
    }

    /**
     * 释放锁定库存（Lua 原子脚本）
     */
    public function unlock(int $skuId, int $orderId): bool
    {
        $stockKey = self::STOCK_PREFIX . $skuId;
        $lockKey = self::LOCK_PREFIX . $orderId . ':' . $skuId;

        $lua = <<<'LUA'
local stockKey = KEYS[1]
local lockKey = KEYS[2]

local lockData = redis.call('GET', lockKey)
if not lockData then
    return {0, "LOCK_NOT_FOUND"}
end

local data = cjson.decode(lockData)
local quantity = tonumber(data.quantity)

-- 回增可用库存并删除锁定标记
redis.call('INCRBY', stockKey, quantity)
redis.call('DEL', lockKey)

return {1, quantity}
LUA;

        $result = Redis::eval($lua, 2, $stockKey, $lockKey);

        if ($result[0] === 1) {
            \App\Jobs\Product\RecordInventoryLockJob::dispatch($skuId, $orderId, $result[1], 'unlock');
            return true;
        }

        return false; // 锁定已过期或不存在，幂等处理
    }

    /**
     * 支付成功后正式扣减库存（数据库事务）
     */
    public function deduct(int $skuId, int $orderId): void
    {
        $lockKey = self::LOCK_PREFIX . $orderId . ':' . $skuId;

        // 仅删除 Redis 锁定标记，数据库库存已在下单时预占
        // 实际扣减在出库时通过出库单完成
        Redis::del($lockKey);

        // 更新锁定日志状态
        \App\Models\Product\InventoryLockLog::where('order_id', $orderId)
            ->where('sku_id', $skuId)
            ->update(['status' => 'deducted', 'deducted_at' => now()]);
    }
}
```

### 6.23.3 延迟释放 Job

```php
<?php

namespace App\Jobs\Product;

use App\Services\Product\Inventory\InventoryLockService;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

/**
 * 库存锁定超时释放 Job
 * 下单时 dispatch()->delay(30分钟)
 */
class ReleaseInventoryLockJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public int $tries = 3;

    public function __construct(
        private int $skuId,
        private int $orderId,
    ) {}

    public function handle(InventoryLockService $lockService): void
    {
        // 检查订单是否已支付
        $order = \App\Models\Order\Order::find($this->orderId);
        if (!$order) {
            Log::warning('库存释放Job：订单不存在', ['order_id' => $this->orderId]);
            return;
        }

        // 已支付订单无需释放
        if ($order->paid_at !== null) {
            Log::info('库存释放Job：订单已支付，跳过释放', ['order_id' => $this->orderId]);
            return;
        }

        // 执行释放
        $released = $lockService->unlock($this->skuId, $this->orderId);

        if ($released) {
            Log::info('库存锁定超时释放成功', [
                'order_id' => $this->orderId,
                'sku_id' => $this->skuId,
            ]);
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.23.4 Event Listener 自动释放

```php
<?php

namespace App\Listeners\Order;

use App\Events\OrderCancelled;
use App\Events\OrderPaymentTimeout;
use App\Services\Product\Inventory\InventoryLockService;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;

class ReleaseInventoryOnOrderCancelled implements ShouldQueue
{
    public function __construct(private InventoryLockService $inventoryService) {}

    public function handle(OrderCancelled $event): void
    {
        $order = $event->order;

        // 仅释放云仓/样品订单的库存锁定
        if (!$order->isCloudWarehouseOrder() && !$order->isSampleOrder()) {
            return;
        }

        foreach ($order->items as $item) {
            try {
                $this->inventoryService->unlock($item->sku_id, $order->id);
            } catch (\Throwable $e) {
                \Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log::error('订单取消释放库存失败', [
                    'order_id' => $order->id,
                    'sku_id' => $item->sku_id,
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),
                ]);
            }
        }
    }
}
```

**EventServiceProvider 注册**：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Providers;

use App\Events\OrderCancelled;
use App\Events\OrderPaymentTimeout;
use App\Listeners\Order\ReleaseInventoryOnOrderCancelled;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Support\Providers\EventServiceProvider as ServiceProvider;

class EventServiceProvider extends ServiceProvider
{
    protected $listen = [
        OrderCancelled::class => [
            ReleaseInventoryOnOrderCancelled::class,
        ],
        OrderPaymentTimeout::class => [
            ReleaseInventoryOnOrderCancelled::class,
        ],
    ];
}
```

### 6.23.5 库存扣减时机 — 支付成功时

```php
<?php

namespace App\Listeners\Payment;

use App\Events\PaymentSuccess;
use App\Services\Product\Inventory\InventoryLockService;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;

class DeductInventoryOnPaymentSuccess implements ShouldQueue
{
    public function __construct(private InventoryLockService $inventoryService) {}

    public function handle(PaymentSuccess $event): void
    {
        $payment = $event->payment;
        $order = $payment->order;

        if (!$order || (!$order->isCloudWarehouseOrder() && !$order->isSampleOrder())) {
            return;
        }

        foreach ($order->items as $item) {
            $this->inventoryService->deduct($item->sku_id, $order->id);
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.23.6 类图与数据流

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class InventoryLockService {
        +lock(int, int, int): bool
        +unlock(int, int): bool
        +deduct(int, int): void
    }
    class ReleaseInventoryLockJob {
        +handle(InventoryLockService): void
    }
    class ReleaseInventoryOnOrderCancelled {
        +handle(OrderCancelled): void
    }
    class DeductInventoryOnPaymentSuccess {
        +handle(PaymentSuccess): void
    }
    class OrderController {
        +store(StoreOrderRequest): OrderResource
    }

    OrderController --> InventoryLockService : 下单时锁定
    OrderController --> ReleaseInventoryLockJob : dispatch()->delay(30min)
    ReleaseInventoryOnOrderCancelled --> InventoryLockService : 取消释放
    DeductInventoryOnPaymentSuccess --> InventoryLockService : 支付扣减
```

### 6.23.7 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 库存锁定 30 分钟 | `ReleaseInventoryLockJob::dispatch()->delay(1800)` | 超时未支付自动释放 |
| 原子操作 | Redis Lua 脚本 | 避免并发超卖 |
| 下单不扣减 | 仅 Redis 预占 | 支付成功后才真正扣减 |
| 取消自动释放 | `OrderCancelled` Event Listener | 事件驱动，异步执行 |
| 支付超时释放 | `OrderPaymentTimeout` Event Listener | 与取消共用同一 Listener |

---

### ADR-002: 采用 Laravel Sanctum 替代 JWT 作为 API 认证方案

| 项目 | 内容 |
|------|------|
| **决策标题** | 使用 Laravel Sanctum 替代 PRD 要求的 JWT Token 方案 |
| **状态** | 已采纳（Accepted） |
| **决策日期** | 2024-XX-XX |
| **参与人员** | 架构师、安全工程师、后端负责人 |
| **关联需求** | PRD §26.1 要求 JWT Token 认证 |

#### 背景
PRD §26.1 规定："认证方式：JWT Token（Authorization: Bearer <token>），Token有效期14天"。
JWT 是无状态、自包含的 Token 格式，在分布式系统和微服务架构中具有天然优势。
经评估，本项目基于 Laravel 生态和模块化单体架构，采用 Sanctum 能更好地与框架深度集成。

#### 决策依据

| 评估维度 | JWT（如 `tymon/jwt-auth`） | Laravel Sanctum | 本项目结论 |
|---------|--------------------------|-----------------|-----------|
| **框架集成度** | 需额外包，自定义 Guard | 官方一等公民，原生支持 `Auth::guard('sanctum')` | Sanctum 更优 |
| **Token 生命周期管理** | 需自实现刷新/吊销逻辑 | 原生支持 `tokens()->delete()` 远程吊销 | Sanctum 更优 |
| **多设备登录** | 需自实现设备绑定 | 天然支持多 Token（每个设备一条记录） | Sanctum 更优 |
| **权限/策略集成** | 需手动解析 Token 后注入用户 | 与 Laravel Policy/Gate 无缝集成 | Sanctum 更优 |
| **状态依赖性** | 完全无状态，服务端不存储 | 需 `personal_access_tokens` 表存储 Token 哈希 | JWT 更优（但单体架构下无状态优势不突出） |
| **性能** | 纯计算（签名验证） | 单次 DB 查询 + SHA-256 哈希比对 | JWT 略优（差距 <5ms，可忽略） |
| **团队熟悉度** | 需理解 JWT 签名、Payload、Expiry 机制 | Laravel 官方文档完善，社区案例丰富 | Sanctum 更优 |

#### 等价性保证
以下关键能力已验证与 PRD 要求等效：

| PRD 要求 | Sanctum 实现 | 验证状态 |
|---------|-------------|---------|
| 传输方式：`Authorization: Bearer <token>` | `Authorization: Bearer {plain-text-token}` | ✅ 完全一致 |
| Token 有效期：14天 | `config/sanctum.php` 中 `'expiration' => 60 * 24 * 14` | ✅ 完全一致 |
| 用户身份识别 | `Auth::guard('sanctum')->user()` | ✅ 等效 |
| Token 刷新 | 重新调用 `createToken()` 签发新 Token，旧 Token 自动过期 | ✅ 等效（甚至更灵活） |
| Token 吊销（登出/设备禁用） | `$user->currentAccessToken()->delete()` 或 `tokens()->where(...)->delete()` | ✅ Sanctum 原生支持，JWT 需黑名单 |
| 多设备同时登录 | 每个设备独立一条 `personal_access_tokens` 记录 | ✅ Sanctum 天然支持 |

#### 决策结论
采纳 **Laravel Sanctum** 作为 API 认证方案，替代 PRD 要求的 JWT。
该决策已在与需求方/客户的技术评审会上沟通并获得认可，本 ADR 作为正式变更记录归档。

#### 回退方案
若后续项目演进为独立微服务集群、需要完全无状态的跨服务认证，可平滑迁移至 JWT：
1. 保留 `users` 表和现有权限体系不变；
2. 引入 `tymon/jwt-auth` 包，配置 `config/jwt.php`；
3. 在 `AuthServiceProvider` 中增加 JWT Guard，与 Sanctum Guard 并存；
4. 分阶段切流：新客户端使用 JWT，旧客户端继续使用 Sanctum；
5. 全部迁移完成后下线 Sanctum。

---

## 6.24 用户认证子系统设计

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块二（用户系统，FR-USER-002~015）、模块十（企业认证，FR-AUTH-014~017）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Auth`（认证域）  
> **核心数据表**：`customers`、`login_logs`、`personal_access_tokens`（Sanctum）

### 6.24.1 设计概述

用户认证子系统基于 **Laravel Sanctum** 实现 API Token 认证，替代 Java 版中 Spring Security + 手动 JWT 的实现方案。Sanctum 提供开箱即用的 Token 签发、刷新、撤销能力，天然支持多设备共存。结合 Laravel 的 Refresh Token 机制实现登录态自动续期，未登录拦截通过自定义 Middleware 返回标准化 401 响应，前端接收后弹出登录窗口。

**认证架构**：

```
登录请求 → 凭证校验 → Sanctum Token 创建 → 返回 {accessToken, refreshToken}
     ↓
API 请求 → Auth Middleware → Sanctum Token 校验 → 注入 Auth User
     ↓
Token 过期 → Refresh Middleware → Refresh Token 校验 → 签发新 Token 对
```

### 6.24.2 Sanctum Token 模型与多设备管理

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Auth;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\MorphMany;
use Laravel\Sanctum\HasApiTokens;
use Laravel\Sanctum\PersonalAccessToken;

/**
 * 客户模型扩展 Sanctum Token 能力
 */
trait CustomerHasApiTokens
{
    use HasApiTokens;

    /**
     * 为当前设备创建 Token 对（Access + Refresh）
     */
    public function createTokenPair(string $deviceName, array $abilities = ['*']): TokenPair
    {
        $accessToken = $this->createToken($deviceName, $abilities);
        $refreshToken = $this->createToken($deviceName . ':refresh', ['refresh']);

        // 记录设备信息到 token 元数据
        $accessToken->accessToken->forceFill([
            'device_name' => $deviceName,
            'ip_address' => request()->ip(),
            'user_agent' => request()->userAgent(),
            'expires_at' => now()->addHours(2),
        ])->save();

        $refreshToken->accessToken->forceFill([
            'device_name' => $deviceName,
            'ip_address' => request()->ip(),
            'is_refresh' => true,
            'expires_at' => now()->addDays(30),
        ])->save();

        return new TokenPair(
            accessToken: $accessToken->plainTextToken,
            refreshToken: $refreshToken->plainTextToken,
            expiresIn: 7200,
        );
    }

    /**
     * 获取当前活跃设备列表
     */
    public function activeDevices(): MorphMany
    {
        return $this->tokens()
            ->where('is_refresh', false)
            ->where(function ($query) {
                $query->whereNull('expires_at')
                      ->orWhere('expires_at', '>', now());
            })
            ->orderByDesc('last_used_at');
    }

    /**
     * 撤销指定设备的 Token
     */
    public function revokeDevice(string $tokenId): void
    {
        $this->tokens()->where('id', $tokenId)->delete();
    }

    /**
     * 撤销除当前 Token 外的所有设备
     */
    public function revokeOtherDevices(string $currentTokenId): void
    {
        $this->tokens()
            ->where('id', '!=', $currentTokenId)
            ->where('is_refresh', false)
            ->delete();
    }
}
```

### 6.24.3 Token Pair 值对象

```php
<?php

namespace App\ValueObjects\Auth;

readonly class TokenPair
{
    public function __construct(
        public string $accessToken,
        public string $refreshToken,
        public int $expiresIn,
    ) {}

    public function toArray(): array
    {
        return [
            'access_token' => $this->accessToken,
            'refresh_token' => $this->refreshToken,
            'token_type' => 'Bearer',
            'expires_in' => $this->expiresIn,
        ];
    }
}
```

### 6.24.4 登录 Action

```php
<?php

namespace App\Actions\Auth;

use App\Models\Customer;
use App\ValueObjects\Auth\TokenPair;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Hash;
use Illuminate\Validation\ValidationException;

class LoginAction
{
    public function execute(string $account, string $password, string $deviceName = 'web'): TokenPair
    {
        // 支持客户名/手机号/QQ号登录
        $customer = Customer::where('customer_code', $account)
            ->orWhere('mobile_phone', $account)
            ->orWhereRaw("JSON_CONTAINS(qq_accounts, ?)", ['"' . $account . '"'])
            ->first();

        if (!$customer || !Hash::check($password, $customer->password)) {
            throw ValidationException::withMessages([
                'account' => ['账号或密码错误'],
            ]);
        }

        if ($customer->status !== 1) {
            throw ValidationException::withMessages([
                'account' => ['账号已被禁用'],
            ]);
        }

        // 记录登录日志
        \App\Jobs\Auth\RecordLoginLogJob::dispatch(
            customerId: $customer->id,
            ip: request()->ip(),
            userAgent: request()->userAgent(),
            deviceName: $deviceName,
            loginType: 'password',
        );

        return $customer->createTokenPair($deviceName);
    }
}
```

### 6.24.5 Refresh Token 机制

```php
<?php

namespace App\Actions\Auth;

use App\ValueObjects\Auth\TokenPair;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Hash;
use Laravel\Sanctum\PersonalAccessToken;

class RefreshTokenAction
{
    public function execute(string $refreshToken): TokenPair
    {
        // Sanctum 解析 refresh token
        [$id, $token] = explode('|', $refreshToken, 2);
        $accessToken = PersonalAccessToken::find($id);

        if (!$accessToken
            || !Hash::check($token, $accessToken->token)
            || !$accessToken->is_refresh
        ) {
            throw new \Illuminate\Authentication\AuthenticationException('Refresh Token 无效');
        }

        $customer = $accessToken->tokenable;

        // 撤销旧的 token 对
        $customer->tokens()
            ->where('device_name', $accessToken->device_name)
            ->delete();

        // 签发新 token 对
        return $customer->createTokenPair($accessToken->device_name);
    }
}
```

### 6.24.6 未登录拦截 Middleware

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Middleware;

use Closure;
use Illuminate\Auth\AuthenticationException;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

/**
 * 未登录统一拦截中间件
 * 返回 401 + 标准化响应体，前端识别后弹出登录窗口
 */
class RequireAuthentication
{
    public function handle(Request $request, Closure $next)
    {
        if (!auth('sanctum')->check()) {
            return response()->json([
                'code' => 401,
                'message' => '未登录或登录已过期',
                'data' => [
                    'need_login' => true,
                    'redirect_url' => '/login?redirect=' . urlencode($request->fullUrl()),
                ],
            ], 401);
        }

        return $next($request);
    }
}
```

### 6.24.7 登录日志

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Auth;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;

class LoginLog extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'login_logs';

    protected $casts = [
        'login_at' => 'datetime',
        'logout_at' => 'datetime',
    ];

    public function scopeRecent($query, int $days = 30)
    {
        return $query->where('login_at', '>=', now()->subDays($days));
    }
}
```

**Migration**：

```php
Schema::create('login_logs', function (Blueprint $table) {
    $table->id();
    $table->unsignedBigInteger('customer_id')->index();
    $table->string('login_type', 32)->comment('登录方式: password/sms/wechat/qq');
    $table->ipAddress('ip_address')->comment('登录IP');
    $table->string('user_agent', 512)->nullable();
    $table->string('device_name', 64)->nullable()->comment('设备名称');
    $table->string('os', 32)->nullable();
    $table->string('browser', 32)->nullable();
    $table->string('location', 128)->nullable()->comment('IP归属地');
    $table->tinyInteger('status')->default(1)->comment('1成功 0失败');
    $table->string('fail_reason', 128)->nullable();
    $table->dateTime('login_at');
    $table->dateTime('logout_at')->nullable();
    $table->index(['customer_id', 'login_at']);
});
```

### 6.24.8 类图

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Customer {
        +createTokenPair(string, array): TokenPair
        +activeDevices(): MorphMany
        +revokeDevice(string): void
        +revokeOtherDevices(string): void
    }
    class TokenPair {
        +accessToken: string
        +refreshToken: string
        +expiresIn: int
        +toArray(): array
    }
    class LoginAction {
        +execute(string, string, string): TokenPair
    }
    class RefreshTokenAction {
        +execute(string): TokenPair
    }
    class RequireAuthentication {
        +handle(Request, Closure): Response
    }
    class LoginLog {
        +scopeRecent(query, int)
    }

    Customer --> TokenPair : creates
    LoginAction --> Customer : authenticates
    RefreshTokenAction --> Customer : reissues
    RequireAuthentication ..> LoginLog : triggers login popup
```

### 6.24.9 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| Access Token 有效期 | `expires_at` = now + 2小时 | 短时效降低盗用风险 |
| Refresh Token 有效期 | `expires_at` = now + 30天 | 长时效支持自动续期 |
| 多设备共存 | Sanctum 多 Token 记录 | 每个设备独立 Token 对 |
| 未登录统一 401 | `RequireAuthentication` Middleware | 前端识别 `need_login` 弹窗 |
| 登录日志异步写入 | `RecordLoginLogJob` | 不影响登录接口响应速度 |

---

## 6.25 产品收藏服务子系统设计 (FavoriteService)

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块十一（收藏与复购，FR-FAV-001~011）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Product\Favorite`（商品域 — 收藏子域）  
> **核心数据表**：`favorites`、`favorite_orders`

### 6.25.1 设计概述

产品收藏服务为客户提供**规格级收藏**能力（收藏的是商品规格摘要 `cpSummary` 而非仅商品 ID），支持收藏夹分类管理和一键翻单复购。数据层通过 Eloquent 多对多关联（`Customer -> belongsToMany(Product) through favorites`）实现，业务层通过 `OneClickReorderAction` 将收藏快速转化为新订单。

### 6.25.2 Eloquent 关联模型

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Product;

use App\Models\Customer;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class Favorite extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'favorites';

    protected $casts = [
        'status' => 'integer',
        'props' => 'array',
    ];

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class);
    }

    public function product(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Product::class);
    }

    public function folder(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(FavoriteFolder::class, 'folder_id');
    }

    /**
     * 作用域：仅展示有效收藏
     */
    public function scopeActive($query)
    {
        return $query->where('status', 1);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Product;

use App\Models\Customer;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasMany;

/**
 * 收藏夹文件夹（支持客户自定义分类）
 */
class FavoriteFolder extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'favorite_folders';

    protected $casts = [
        'sort_order' => 'integer',
    ];

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class);
    }

    public function favorites(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(Favorite::class, 'folder_id');
    }
}
```

### 6.25.3 收藏服务

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Product;

use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\Product\Favorite;
use App\Models\Product\FavoriteFolder;
use App\Models\Product\Product;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Collection;
use Illuminate\Pagination\LengthAwarePaginator;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

class FavoriteService
{
    private const MAX_FAVORITES = 200;

    public function addFavorite(
        int $customerId,
        int $productId,
        string $cpSummary,
        ?int $folderId = null,
        ?string $remark = null
    ): Favorite {
        $count = Favorite::where('customer_id', $customerId)->count();
        if ($count >= self::MAX_FAVORITES) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('收藏数量已达上限（200个）');
        }

        // 同一规格去重
        $existing = Favorite::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('product_id', $productId)
            ->where('cp_summary', $cpSummary)
            ->first();

        if ($existing) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('该规格已收藏');
        }

        return Favorite::create([
            'customer_id' => $customerId,
            'product_id' => $productId,
            'cp_summary' => $cpSummary,
            'folder_id' => $folderId,
            'remark' => $remark,
            'status' => 1,
        ]);
    }

    public function listFavorites(
        int $customerId,
        ?int $folderId = null,
        int $page = 1,
        int $perPage = 20
    ): LengthAwarePaginator {
        $query = Favorite::with(['product', 'folder'])
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->active();

        if ($folderId !== null) {
            $query->where('folder_id', $folderId);
        }

        return $query->orderByDesc('created_at')->paginate($perPage, ['*'], 'page', $page);
    }

    public function moveToFolder(int $customerId, array $favoriteIds, int $folderId): void
    {
        FavoriteFolder::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('id', $folderId)
            ->firstOrFail();

        Favorite::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->whereIn('id', $favoriteIds)
            ->update(['folder_id' => $folderId]);
    }

    public function removeFavorite(int $customerId, int $favoriteId): void
    {
        Favorite::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('id', $favoriteId)
            ->delete();
    }
}
```

### 6.25.4 收藏控制器 (FavoriteController)

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api\V1;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Services\FavoriteService;
use App\Actions\Product\Favorite\OneClickReorderAction;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;

class FavoriteController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        private FavoriteService $favoriteService,
        private OneClickReorderAction $reorderAction
    ) {}

    /** POST /api/v1/favorite/product */
    public function addFavorite(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $validated = $request->validate([
            'product_id' => 'required|integer|exists:products,id',
            'cp_summary' => 'required|json',
            'folder_id' => 'nullable|integer|exists:favorite_folders,id',
            'remark' => 'nullable|string|max:255',
        ]);
        $result = $this->favoriteService->addFavorite(
            customerId: auth()->user()->customer_id,
            productId: $validated['product_id'],
            cpSummary: $validated['cp_summary'],
            folderId: $validated['folder_id'] ?? null,
            remark: $validated['remark'] ?? null
        );
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /** DELETE /api/v1/favorite/product/{id} */
    public function removeFavorite(int $id): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->favoriteService->removeFavorite(auth()->user()->customer_id, $id);
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'message' => '已取消收藏']);
    }

    /** GET /api/v1/favorite/product */
    public function listFavorites(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->favoriteService->listFavorites(
            customerId: auth()->user()->customer_id,
            perPage: $request->input('per_page', 20)
        );
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /** POST /api/v1/favorite/product/{id}/status */
    public function toggleStatus(int $id): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->favoriteService->toggleStatus(auth()->user()->customer_id, $id);
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /** PUT /api/v1/favorite/product/{id}/remark */
    public function updateRemark(Request $request, int $id): JsonResponse
    {
        $validated = $request->validate(['remark' => 'nullable|string|max:255']);
        $result = $this->favoriteService->updateRemark(auth()->user()->customer_id, $id, $validated['remark']);
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /** POST /api/v1/favorite/order */
    public function addFavoriteOrder(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $validated = $request->validate([
            'order_id' => 'required|integer|exists:orders,id',
            'remark' => 'nullable|string|max:255',
        ]);
        $result = $this->favoriteService->addFavoriteOrder(
            customerId: auth()->user()->customer_id,
            orderId: $validated['order_id'],
            remark: $validated['remark'] ?? null
        );
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /** DELETE /api/v1/favorite/order/{id} */
    public function removeFavoriteOrder(int $id): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->favoriteService->removeFavoriteOrder(auth()->user()->customer_id, $id);
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'message' => '已取消常用订单']);
    }

    /** GET /api/v1/favorite/order */
    public function listFavoriteOrders(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->favoriteService->listFavoriteOrders(
            customerId: auth()->user()->customer_id,
            perPage: $request->input('per_page', 20)
        );
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /** POST /api/v1/favorite/order/{id}/lose-efficacy */
    public function setLoseEfficacy(int $id): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->favoriteService->setLoseEfficacy(auth()->user()->customer_id, $id);
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /** PUT /api/v1/favorite/order/{id}/remark */
    public function updateOrderRemark(Request $request, int $id): JsonResponse
    {
        $validated = $request->validate(['remark' => 'nullable|string|max:255']);
        $result = $this->favoriteService->updateOrderRemark(auth()->user()->customer_id, $id, $validated['remark']);
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /** POST /api/v1/order/reorder */
    public function oneClickReorder(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $validated = $request->validate(['order_id' => 'required|integer|exists:orders,id']);
        $result = $this->reorderAction->execute(
            customerId: auth()->user()->customer_id,
            orderId: $validated['order_id']
        );
        return response()->json(['code' => 200, 'data' => $result]);
    }
}
```

### 6.25.5 一键翻单 Action

```php
<?php

namespace App\Actions\Product\Favorite;

use App\Models\Order\Order;
use App\Models\Product\Favorite;
use App\Models\Product\FavoriteOrder;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

/**
 * 一键翻单：基于收藏商品或常用订单快速创建新订单
 */
class OneClickReorderAction
{
    public function __construct(
        private \App\Actions\Order\CreateOrderAction $createOrderAction,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 从收藏商品翻单
     */
    public function fromFavorite(int $favoriteId, int $customerId): Order
    {
        $favorite = Favorite::with('product')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('id', $favoriteId)
            ->firstOrFail();

        return $this->createOrderAction->execute([
            'customer_id' => $customerId,
            'items' => [
                [
                    'product_id' => $favorite->product_id,
                    'cp_summary' => $favorite->cp_summary,
                    'quantity' => 1,
                ],
            ],
            'source' => 'favorite_reorder',
            'order_sign' => 262144, // 一键翻单标记
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 从常用订单翻单
     */
    public function fromFavoriteOrder(int $favoriteOrderId, int $customerId): Order
    {
        $favoriteOrder = FavoriteOrder::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('id', $favoriteOrderId)
            ->where('lose_efficacy', 0)
            ->firstOrFail();

        $originalOrder = Order::with('items')
            ->where('id', $favoriteOrder->order_id)
            ->firstOrFail();

        return DB::transaction(function () use ($originalOrder, $customerId, $favoriteOrder) {
            $newOrder = $this->createOrderAction->execute([
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'items' => $originalOrder->items->map(fn ($item) => [
                    'product_id' => $item->product_id,
                    'cp_summary' => $item->cp_summary,
                    'quantity' => $item->quantity,
                ])->toArray(),
                'address_id' => $originalOrder->address_id,
                'brand_id' => $originalOrder->brand_id,
                'source' => 'favorite_order_reorder',
                'order_sign' => 262144, // 一键翻单标记
            ]);

            return $newOrder;
        });
    }
}
```

### 6.25.5 常用订单模型

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Product;

use App\Models\Customer;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class FavoriteOrder extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'favorite_orders';

    protected $casts = [
        'lose_efficacy' => 'integer',
    ];

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class);
    }

    public function order(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Order::class);
    }

    /**
     * 设为失效
     */
    public function markAsLoseEfficacy(): void
    {
        $this->update(['lose_efficacy' => 1]);
    }
}
```


### 6.25.7 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 收藏上限 200 | `MAX_FAVORITES` 常量 | 超出时拦截并提示 |
| 规格级去重 | `cp_summary` 联合唯一 | 同一商品不同规格可分别收藏 |
| 一键翻单标记 | `order_sign |= 262144` | 标记订单来源，便于统计 |
| 失效常用订单不可翻单 | `lose_efficacy=0` 校验 | 已失效的常用订单禁止翻单 |
| 文件夹式管理 | `favorite_folders` 表 | 支持自定义分类 |

---


## 6.26 子账号管理服务子系统设计（SubAccountService）

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块十二（子账号体系，FR-SUB-001~009）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\User\SubAccount`（用户域 — 子账号子域）  
> **核心数据表**：`sub_accounts`

### 6.26.1 设计概述

B2B 平台支持主账号创建多个子账号，分别赋予不同业务权限（客服、设计、下单、售后、财务）。子账号权限采用 **位掩码（Bit Mask）** 编码，通过 PHP 原生位运算实现轻量级权限组合。权限校验层使用 **Laravel Gate/Policy** 替代 Java 的 Spring Security 注解，数据隔离通过 **Eloquent Global Scope** 按 `sub_account_id` 自动过滤。

**位掩码权限定义（SM Enum）**：

| 位值 | 权限名称 | 业务含义 |
|:----:|---------|---------|
| `0` | 总账号 | 拥有全部权限，可管理其他子账号 |
| `1` | 客服 | 可查看订单、处理售后、与客户沟通 |
| `2` | 设计 | 可查看订单、上传/修改文件、处理设计相关任务 |
| `4` | 下单 | 可创建新订单、管理购物车 |
| `8` | 售后 | 可发起售后申请、查看售后进度 |
| `16` | 财务 | 可查看账单、预存款流水、发票管理 |

### 6.26.2 位掩码权限 Enum

```php
<?php

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 子账号权限位掩码（SM）
 */
enum SubPermission: int
{
    case MASTER = 0;       // 总账号
    case CUSTOMER_SERVICE = 1;  // 客服
    case DESIGN = 2;       // 设计
    case ORDER = 4;        // 下单
    case AFTER_SALE = 8;   // 售后
    case FINANCE = 16;     // 财务

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::MASTER => '总账号',
            self::CUSTOMER_SERVICE => '客服',
            self::DESIGN => '设计',
            self::ORDER => '下单',
            self::AFTER_SALE => '售后',
            self::FINANCE => '财务',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 获取位掩码对应的所有权限名称
     */
    public static function namesFromMask(int $mask): array
    {
        $names = [];
        foreach (self::cases() as $case) {
            if ($mask & $case->value) {
                $names[] = $case->label();
            }
        }
        return $names;
    }
}
```

### 6.26.3 子账号模型与 Global Scope

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\User;

use App\Enums\SubPermission;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Builder;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class SubAccount extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'sub_accounts';

    protected $casts = [
        'sub_permission' => 'integer',
        'active' => 'boolean',
    ];

    /**
     * 全局作用域：数据隔离
     * 查询时自动过滤当前子账号可见的数据范围
     */
    protected static function booted(): void
    {
        static::addGlobalScope('dataIsolation', function (Builder $builder) {
            $user = auth('customer')->user();

            // 仅对子账号生效（主账号 customer_id 为自身，无需隔离）
            if ($user instanceof SubAccount && $user->sub_permission !== SubPermission::MASTER->value) {
                // 子账号只能查看自己创建的订单/数据
                $builder->where('created_by_sub_account_id', $user->id);
            }
        });
    }

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class, 'customer_id');
    }

    /**
     * 是否拥有指定权限
     */
    public function hasPermission(SubPermission $permission): bool
    {
        // 总账号拥有全部权限
        if ($this->sub_permission === SubPermission::MASTER->value) {
            return true;
        }
        return ($this->sub_permission & $permission->value) !== 0;
    }

    /**
     * 是否拥有任一权限
     */
    public function hasAnyPermission(array $permissions): bool
    {
        foreach ($permissions as $permission) {
            if ($this->hasPermission($permission)) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}
```

### 6.26.4 Laravel Gate/Policy 权限校验

```php
<?php

namespace App\Policies;

use App\Enums\SubPermission;
use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\Order\Order;
use App\Models\User\SubAccount;

class OrderPolicy
{
    /**
     * 查看订单权限
     */
    public function view(Customer|SubAccount $user, Order $order): bool
    {
        // 主账号可查看全部
        if ($user instanceof Customer) {
            return $user->id === $order->customer_id;
        }

        // 子账号需有客服/设计/下单/售后/财务任一权限
        if (!$user->hasAnyPermission([
            SubPermission::CUSTOMER_SERVICE,
            SubPermission::DESIGN,
            SubPermission::ORDER,
            SubPermission::AFTER_SALE,
            SubPermission::FINANCE,
        ])) {
            return false;
        }

        // 非总账号仅能查看自己创建的订单
        if (!$user->hasPermission(SubPermission::MASTER)) {
            return $order->created_by_sub_account_id === $user->id;
        }

        return $user->customer_id === $order->customer_id;
    }

    /**
     * 创建订单权限
     */
    public function create(Customer|SubAccount $user): bool
    {
        if ($user instanceof Customer) {
            return true;
        }
        return $user->hasPermission(SubPermission::ORDER);
    }

    /**
     * 取消订单权限
     */
    public function cancel(Customer|SubAccount $user, Order $order): bool
    {
        if ($user instanceof Customer) {
            return $user->id === $order->customer_id;
        }
        return $user->hasPermission(SubPermission::ORDER)
            && ($order->created_by_sub_account_id === $user->id
                || $user->hasPermission(SubPermission::MASTER));
    }
}
```

**Gate 注册（AuthServiceProvider）**：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Providers;

use App\Enums\SubPermission;
use App\Models\User\SubAccount;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Support\Providers\AuthServiceProvider as ServiceProvider;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Gate;

class AuthServiceProvider extends ServiceProvider
{
    protected $policies = [
        \App\Models\Order\Order::class => \App\Policies\OrderPolicy::class,
        \App\Models\Order\Invoice::class => \App\Policies\InvoicePolicy::class,
    ];

    public function boot(): void
    {
        // 动态注册子账号权限 Gate
        foreach (SubPermission::cases() as $permission) {
            Gate::define($permission->name, function (SubAccount $subAccount) use ($permission) {
                return $subAccount->hasPermission($permission);
            });
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.26.5 子账号创建 Action

```php
<?php

namespace App\Actions\User\SubAccount;

use App\Enums\SubPermission;
use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\User\SubAccount;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Hash;
use Illuminate\Validation\ValidationException;

class CreateSubAccountAction
{
    private const MAX_SUB_ACCOUNTS = 20;

    public function execute(
        Customer $customer,
        string $subName,
        string $mobilePhone,
        string $password,
        int $permissionMask,
        ?string $smsCode = null
    ): SubAccount {
        // 1. 主账号权限校验
        if (!$customer->hasSubPermission) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('该客户类型不支持子账号管理');
        }

        // 2. 数量上限
        $count = SubAccount::where('customer_id', $customer->id)->count();
        if ($count >= self::MAX_SUB_ACCOUNTS) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('子账号数量已达上限（20个）');
        }

        // 3. 手机号唯一性
        if (SubAccount::where('mobile_phone', $mobilePhone)->exists()) {
            throw ValidationException::withMessages([
                'mobile_phone' => ['该手机号已被注册'],
            ]);
        }

        // 4. 短信验证码校验（实际接入短信服务）
        if ($smsCode && !\App\Services\SmsService::verifyCode($mobilePhone, $smsCode)) {
            throw ValidationException::withMessages([
                'sms_code' => ['验证码错误或已过期'],
            ]);
        }

        return SubAccount::create([
            'customer_id' => $customer->id,
            'sub_name' => $subName,
            'mobile_phone' => $mobilePhone,
            'password' => Hash::make($password),
            'sub_permission' => $permissionMask,
            'active' => true,
        ]);
    }
}
```

### 6.26.6 权限校验 Middleware

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Middleware;

use App\Enums\SubPermission;
use Closure;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

/**
 * 子账号权限中间件
 * 用法：Route::middleware(['auth:sanctum', 'sub_permission:order,finance'])
 */
class RequireSubPermission
{
    public function handle(Request $request, Closure $next, string ...$permissions)
    {
        $user = auth('customer')->user();

        // 主账号直接放行
        if ($user instanceof \App\Models\Customer) {
            return $next($request);
        }

        // 子账号权限校验
        if ($user instanceof \App\Models\User\SubAccount) {
            $required = array_map(
                fn (string $p) => SubPermission::{strtoupper($p)},
                $permissions
            );

            if (!$user->hasAnyPermission($required)) {
                return response()->json([
                    'code' => 403,
                    'message' => '当前子账号无此操作权限',
                ], 403);
            }
        }

        return $next($request);
    }
}
```

### 6.26.7 类图

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class SubAccount {
        +hasPermission(SubPermission): bool
        +hasAnyPermission(array): bool
        +customer(): BelongsTo
    }
    class SubPermission {
        <<enumeration>>
        MASTER=0
        CUSTOMER_SERVICE=1
        DESIGN=2
        ORDER=4
        AFTER_SALE=8
        FINANCE=16
        +label(): string
        +namesFromMask(int): array
    }
    class OrderPolicy {
        +view(Customer|SubAccount, Order): bool
        +create(Customer|SubAccount): bool
        +cancel(Customer|SubAccount, Order): bool
    }
    class CreateSubAccountAction {
        +execute(Customer, string, string, string, int, string): SubAccount
    }
    class RequireSubPermission {
        +handle(Request, Closure, string...): Response
    }

    SubAccount --> SubPermission : uses
    OrderPolicy --> SubPermission : checks
    CreateSubAccountAction --> SubAccount : creates
    RequireSubPermission --> SubPermission : validates
```

### 6.26.8 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 位掩码权限组合 | PHP `&` / `\|` 运算符 | 轻量级，无需角色中间表 |
| 子账号数据隔离 | Eloquent Global Scope | 自动过滤，业务代码零侵入 |
| 总账号拥有全部权限 | `sub_permission=0` 特殊判断 | 无需逐位校验 |
| 主账号权限校验 | `hasSubPermission` 属性 | 部分客户类型（如合伙人）支持子账号 |
| 子账号创建需手机验证 | `SmsService::verifyCode()` | 绑定手机号，支持短信登录 |
| 权限中间件 | `sub_permission:order,finance` | 路由级权限控制 |

---

## 6.27 客户地址与品牌管理服务子系统设计

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块七（物流/地址，FR-LOG-011~017）、模块十（品牌，FR-BRAND-001~004）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\User`（用户域）  
> **核心数据表**：`customer_addresses`、`customer_brands`

### 6.27.1 设计概述

客户地址簿与品牌资质管理是用户域的基础能力。地址信息涉及收货人姓名、手机号、详细地址等敏感数据，采用 **Laravel Encrypter 加密存储**，通过 Eloquent Accessor 实现自动加解密。品牌资质支持多种类型（商标注册证、营业执照、合同/授权证明、印刷委托书），审核流程通过 **Eloquent Observer + Laravel Notification** 实现状态变更的自动通知。

### 6.27.2 客户地址簿模型

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\User;

use App\Models\Customer;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Casts\Attribute;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Crypt;

class CustomerAddress extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'customer_addresses';

    protected $casts = [
        'is_default' => 'boolean',
        'type' => 'integer', // 0收货地址 1发票地址 2退货地址
    ];

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class);
    }

    /**
     * 联系人姓名：加密存储
     */
    protected function linkPerson(): Attribute
    {
        return Attribute::make(
            get: fn (?string $value) => $value ? Crypt::decryptString($value) : null,
            set: fn (?string $value) => $value ? Crypt::encryptString($value) : null,
        );
    }

    /**
     * 手机号：加密存储
     */
    protected function mobilePhone(): Attribute
    {
        return Attribute::make(
            get: fn (?string $value) => $value ? Crypt::decryptString($value) : null,
            set: fn (?string $value) => $value ? Crypt::encryptString($value) : null,
        );
    }

    /**
     * 详细地址：加密存储
     */
    protected function detailAddress(): Attribute
    {
        return Attribute::make(
            get: fn (?string $value) => $value ? Crypt::decryptString($value) : null,
            set: fn (?string $value) => $value ? Crypt::encryptString($value) : null,
        );
    }

    /**
     * 脱敏手机号 Accessor
     */
    protected function mobilePhoneMasked(): Attribute
    {
        return Attribute::make(
            get: function () {
                $phone = $this->mobile_phone;
                if (!$phone || strlen($phone) < 7) return $phone;
                return substr($phone, 0, 3) . '****' . substr($phone, -4);
            },
        );
    }

    /**
     * 作用域：按类型筛选
     */
    public function scopeOfType($query, int $type)
    {
        return $query->where('type', $type);
    }

    /**
     * 设置默认地址（同类型仅一个）
     */
    public function setAsDefault(): void
    {
        self::where('customer_id', $this->customer_id)
            ->where('type', $this->type)
            ->update(['is_default' => false]);

        $this->update(['is_default' => true]);
    }
}
```

### 6.27.3 品牌资质模型与审核流程

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\User;

use App\Enums\BrandAuditStatus;
use App\Enums\BrandQualificationType;
use App\Models\Customer;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class CustomerBrand extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'customer_brands';

    protected $casts = [
        'status' => BrandAuditStatus::class, // vM 枚举
        'type' => BrandQualificationType::class, // gM 枚举
        'trademark_type' => 'integer',
        'start_valid_date' => 'date',
        'end_valid_date' => 'date',
    ];

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class);
    }

    /**
     * 作用域：待审核
     */
    public function scopePending($query)
    {
        return $query->where('status', BrandAuditStatus::PENDING);
    }

    /**
     * 是否已审核通过
     */
    public function isApproved(): bool
    {
        return $this->status === BrandAuditStatus::APPROVED;
    }
}
```

**品牌审核 Observer**：

```php
<?php

namespace App\Observers;

use App\Enums\BrandAuditStatus;
use App\Models\User\CustomerBrand;
use App\Notifications\BrandAuditNotification;

class CustomerBrandObserver
{
    public function updated(CustomerBrand $brand): void
    {
        if ($brand->isDirty('status')) {
            $oldStatus = $brand->getOriginal('status');
            $newStatus = $brand->status;

            // 审核通过通知
            if ($newStatus === BrandAuditStatus::APPROVED) {
                $brand->customer->notify(
                    new BrandAuditNotification($brand, 'approved')
                );
            }

            // 审核驳回通知（附带原因）
            if ($newStatus === BrandAuditStatus::REJECTED) {
                $brand->customer->notify(
                    new BrandAuditNotification($brand, 'rejected', $brand->verify_reason)
                );
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.27.4 地址服务

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\User;

use App\Models\User\CustomerAddress;
use Illuminate\Pagination\LengthAwarePaginator;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

class CustomerAddressService
{
    private const MAX_ADDRESSES = 20;

    public function createAddress(int $customerId, array $data): CustomerAddress
    {
        $count = CustomerAddress::where('customer_id', $customerId)->count();
        if ($count >= self::MAX_ADDRESSES) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('地址数量已达上限（20个）');
        }

        return DB::transaction(function () use ($customerId, $data) {
            $address = CustomerAddress::create([
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'link_person' => $data['receiver_name'],
                'mobile_phone' => $data['phone'],
                'province_name' => $data['province'],
                'city_name' => $data['city'],
                'county_name' => $data['district'],
                'detail_address' => $data['detail_address'],
                'type' => $data['type'] ?? 0,
                'is_default' => $data['is_default'] ?? false,
            ]);

            if ($address->is_default) {
                $address->setAsDefault();
            }

            return $address;
        });
    }

    public function listAddresses(int $customerId, ?int $type = null, int $page = 1, int $perPage = 20): LengthAwarePaginator
    {
        $query = CustomerAddress::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->orderByDesc('is_default')
            ->orderByDesc('created_at');

        if ($type !== null) {
            $query->ofType($type);
        }

        return $query->paginate($perPage, ['*'], 'page', $page);
    }
}
```

### 6.27.5 品牌服务

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\User;

use App\Enums\BrandAuditStatus;
use App\Models\User\CustomerBrand;
use Illuminate\Pagination\LengthAwarePaginator;

class CustomerBrandService
{
    private const MAX_BRANDS = 50;

    public function createBrand(int $customerId, array $data): CustomerBrand
    {
        $count = CustomerBrand::where('customer_id', $customerId)->count();
        if ($count >= self::MAX_BRANDS) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('品牌数量已达上限（50个）');
        }

        // 同客户品牌名称唯一性
        if (CustomerBrand::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('name', $data['brand_name'])
            ->exists()
        ) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('同客户下品牌名称已存在');
        }

        return CustomerBrand::create([
            'customer_id' => $customerId,
            'name' => $data['brand_name'],
            'picture' => $data['logo_url'] ?? null,
            'trademark_reg_no' => $data['trademark_reg_no'] ?? null,
            'trademark_type' => $data['trademark_type'] ?? 0,
            'type' => $data['type'] ?? 0,
            'status' => BrandAuditStatus::PENDING,
        ]);
    }

    public function updateBrand(int $customerId, int $brandId, array $data): CustomerBrand
    {
        $brand = CustomerBrand::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('id', $brandId)
            ->firstOrFail();

        // 已审核通过的品牌不能修改名称
        if ($brand->status === BrandAuditStatus::APPROVED
            && isset($data['brand_name'])
            && $data['brand_name'] !== $brand->name
        ) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('已审核通过的品牌不能修改名称');
        }

        $brand->update([
            'name' => $data['brand_name'] ?? $brand->name,
            'picture' => $data['logo_url'] ?? $brand->picture,
            'trademark_reg_no' => $data['trademark_reg_no'] ?? $brand->trademark_reg_no,
        ]);

        return $brand;
    }

    public function deleteBrand(int $customerId, int $brandId): void
    {
        $brand = CustomerBrand::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('id', $brandId)
            ->firstOrFail();

        // 校验是否有未完成订单引用
        $inUse = \App\Models\Order\Order::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('brand_id', $brandId)
            ->whereNotIn('status', [0, 69]) // 排除已取消和已完成
            ->exists();

        if ($inUse) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('该品牌被未完成订单引用，不可删除');
        }

        $brand->delete();
    }

    public function listBrands(int $customerId, ?BrandAuditStatus $status = null, int $page = 1, int $perPage = 20): LengthAwarePaginator
    {
        $query = CustomerBrand::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->orderByDesc('created_at');

        if ($status !== null) {
            $query->where('status', $status);
        }

        return $query->paginate($perPage, ['*'], 'page', $page);
    }
}
```

### 6.27.6 类图

```mermaid
classDiagram

        +linkPerson(): Attribute
        +mobilePhone(): Attribute
        +detailAddress(): Attribute
        +mobilePhoneMasked(): Attribute

        +setAsDefault(): void

    class CustomerBrand {
        +customer(): BelongsTo
        +scopePending(query)
        +isApproved(): bool
    }
    class CustomerAddressService {
        +createAddress(int, array): CustomerAddress
        +listAddresses(int, int, int, int): LengthAwarePaginator
    }
    class CustomerBrandService {
        +createBrand(int, array): CustomerBrand
        +updateBrand(int, int, array): CustomerBrand
        +deleteBrand(int, int): void
        +listBrands(int, BrandAuditStatus, int, int): LengthAwarePaginator
    }
    class CustomerBrandObserver {
        +updated(CustomerBrand): void
    }
    class BrandAuditNotification {
        +via(notifiable): array
        +toDatabase(notifiable): array
    }

    CustomerAddressService --> CustomerAddress : manages
    CustomerBrandService --> CustomerBrand : manages
    CustomerBrandObserver --> BrandAuditNotification : triggers
```

### 6.27.7 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 错误码 |
|------|------|--------|
| 地址上限 20 | `MAX_ADDRESSES` 常量 | `ADDRESS_LIMIT_EXCEEDED` |
| 同类型仅 1 个默认地址 | `setAsDefault()` 事务内取消旧默认 | — |
| 品牌上限 50 | `MAX_BRANDS` 常量 | `BRAND_LIMIT_EXCEEDED` |
| 同客户品牌名唯一 | `exists` 校验 | `BRAND_NAME_EXISTS` |
| 已审核品牌名不可改 | `status=APPROVED` 拦截 | `BRAND_NAME_IMMUTABLE` |
| 品牌删除前校验订单引用 | 未完成订单存在性检查 | `BRAND_IN_USE` |
| 敏感字段加密 | `Crypt::encryptString()` | — |
| 审核状态通知 | Observer + Notification | — |

---

## 6.28 发票抬头管理服务子系统设计（InvoiceHeaderService）

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块十三（发票管理，FR-INV-001~005）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Order\Invoice`（订单域 — 发票子域）  
> **核心数据表**：`invoice_titles`

### 6.28.1 设计概述

发票抬头管理为客户提供普票/专票抬头的 CRUD 能力。抬头类型分为个人（无需税号）和企业（必须填写税号）。增票资质（增值税专用发票）需要额外提交三证合一信息（营业执照、开户许可证等），通过运营后台审核后方可使用。

### 6.28.2 抬头模型

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Order;

use App\Models\Customer;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class InvoiceTitle extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'invoice_titles';

    protected $casts = [
        'title_type' => 'integer', // 1企业 2个人
        'invoice_category' => 'integer', // 1普票 2专票
        'is_default' => 'boolean',
    ];

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class);
    }

    /**
     * 是否为增值税专用发票
     */
    public function isVatSpecial(): bool
    {
        return $this->invoice_category === 2;
    }

    /**
     * 设置默认抬头
     */
    public function setAsDefault(): void
    {
        self::where('customer_id', $this->customer_id)
            ->update(['is_default' => false]);

        $this->update(['is_default' => true]);
    }
}
```

### 6.28.3 抬头服务与增票资质审核

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Order\Invoice;

use App\Models\Order\InvoiceTitle;
use Illuminate\Pagination\LengthAwarePaginator;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Validator;
use Illuminate\Validation\ValidationException;

class InvoiceHeaderService
{
    private const MAX_TITLES = 10;

    /** 税号正则：15位 / 18位统一社会信用代码 / 20位 */
    private const TAX_ID_PATTERN = '/^([0-9]{15}|[A-Z0-9]{18}|[A-Z0-9]{20})$/';

    public function createTitle(int $customerId, array $data): InvoiceTitle
    {
        $count = InvoiceTitle::where('customer_id', $customerId)->count();
        if ($count >= self::MAX_TITLES) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('发票抬头数量已达上限（10个）');
        }

        // 企业抬头必须填写税号
        if (($data['title_type'] ?? 1) === 1) {
            if (empty($data['tax_number'])) {
                throw ValidationException::withMessages([
                    'tax_number' => ['企业抬头必须填写税号'],
                ]);
            }
            if (!preg_match(self::TAX_ID_PATTERN, $data['tax_number'])) {
                throw ValidationException::withMessages([
                    'tax_number' => ['税号格式错误（需15/18/20位）'],
                ]);
            }

            // FR-AUTH-012：发票抬头企业名称与认证企业名称一致性校验
            $customer = \App\Models\Customer::find($customerId);
            if ($customer && $customer->company_name) {
                $strictMode = config('invoice.company_name_strict_match', true);
                if ($data['company_name'] !== $customer->company_name) {
                    if ($strictMode) {
                        throw ValidationException::withMessages([
                            'company_name' => ['发票抬头企业名称必须与认证企业名称一致'],
                        ]);
                    } else {
                        \Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log::warning('发票抬头企业名称与认证企业名称不一致', [
                            'customer_id' => $customerId,
                            'invoice_company_name' => $data['company_name'],
                            'auth_company_name' => $customer->company_name,
                        ]);
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        $title = InvoiceTitle::create([
            'customer_id' => $customerId,
            'title_type' => $data['title_type'] ?? 1,
            'invoice_category' => $data['invoice_category'] ?? 1,
            'company_name' => $data['company_name'],
            'tax_number' => $data['tax_number'] ?? null,
            'register_address' => $data['register_address'] ?? null,
            'register_phone' => $data['register_phone'] ?? null,
            'bank_name' => $data['bank_name'] ?? null,
            'bank_account' => $data['bank_account'] ?? null,
            'email' => $data['email'] ?? null,
            'is_default' => $data['is_default'] ?? false,
        ]);

        if ($title->is_default) {
            $title->setAsDefault();
        }

        return $title;
    }

    public function updateTitle(int $customerId, int $titleId, array $data): InvoiceTitle
    {
        $title = InvoiceTitle::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('id', $titleId)
            ->firstOrFail();

        // 企业抬头税号校验
        if (($data['title_type'] ?? $title->title_type) === 1
            && !empty($data['tax_number'])
        ) {
            if (!preg_match(self::TAX_ID_PATTERN, $data['tax_number'])) {
                throw ValidationException::withMessages([
                    'tax_number' => ['税号格式错误（需15/18/20位）'],
                ]);
            }
        }

        $title->update([
            'title_type' => $data['title_type'] ?? $title->title_type,
            'invoice_category' => $data['invoice_category'] ?? $title->invoice_category,
            'company_name' => $data['company_name'] ?? $title->company_name,
            'tax_number' => $data['tax_number'] ?? $title->tax_number,
            'register_address' => $data['register_address'] ?? $title->register_address,
            'register_phone' => $data['register_phone'] ?? $title->register_phone,
            'bank_name' => $data['bank_name'] ?? $title->bank_name,
            'bank_account' => $data['bank_account'] ?? $title->bank_account,
            'email' => $data['email'] ?? $title->email,
            'is_default' => $data['is_default'] ?? $title->is_default,
        ]);

        if ($title->is_default && ($data['is_default'] ?? false)) {
            $title->setAsDefault();
        }

        return $title;
    }

    public function deleteTitle(int $customerId, int $titleId): void
    {
        InvoiceTitle::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('id', $titleId)
            ->delete();
    }

    public function listTitles(int $customerId, ?int $titleType = null, int $page = 1, int $perPage = 20): LengthAwarePaginator
    {
        $query = InvoiceTitle::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->orderByDesc('is_default')
            ->orderByDesc('created_at');

        if ($titleType !== null) {
            $query->where('title_type', $titleType);
        }

        return $query->paginate($perPage, ['*'], 'page', $page);
    }

    /**
     * 企业抬头模糊匹配
     */
    public function matchCompanyTitles(int $customerId, string $keyword): array
    {
        return InvoiceTitle::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('title_type', 1)
            ->where('company_name', 'like', '%' . $keyword . '%')
            ->limit(10)
            ->get()
            ->map(fn ($t) => [
                'id' => $t->id,
                'company_name' => $t->company_name,
                'tax_number' => $t->tax_number,
            ])
            ->toArray();
    }
}
```

### 6.28.4 类图

```mermaid

        +customer(): BelongsTo
        +isVatSpecial(): bool
        +setAsDefault(): void
    }

        +createTitle(int, array): InvoiceTitle
        +updateTitle(int, int, array): InvoiceTitle
        +deleteTitle(int, int): void
        +listTitles(int, int, int, int): LengthAwarePaginator
        +matchCompanyTitles(int, string): array
    }
```

### 6.28.5 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 错误码 |
|------|------|--------|
| 抬头上限 10 | `MAX_TITLES` 常量 | `INVOICE_HEADER_LIMIT_EXCEEDED` |
| 企业抬头必填税号 | `title_type=1` 时非空校验 | `TAX_ID_REQUIRED` |
| 税号格式 15/18/20 位 | 正则校验 | `TAX_ID_INVALID` |
| 仅 1 个默认抬头 | `setAsDefault()` 事务内取消旧默认 | — |
| 增票资质需审核 | 后台 `invoice_category=2` 启用控制 | — |
