## 6.29 客服会话管理子系统设计（CustomerSupportService）

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块十二（客服与帮助，FR-CS-001~010）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Admin\Support`（管理后台 — 客服子域）  
> **核心数据表**：`support_sessions`、`support_messages`

### 6.29.1 设计概述

客服会话管理系统支撑在线客服的全生命周期：会话创建、消息收发、历史查询、满意度评价、离线留言。会话数据持久化到 MySQL，实时消息通过 WebSocket（Laravel Reverb/Soketi）广播。客服分配由 `AgentAllocationService`（6.30节）完成，本服务专注会话状态管理和消息持久化。

### 6.29.2 会话与消息模型

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Admin\Support;

use App\Models\Customer;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasMany;

class SupportSession extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'support_sessions';

    protected $casts = [
        'status' => 'integer', // 1进行中 2已结束
        'source' => 'integer', // 1PC 2Mobile
        'start_time' => 'datetime',
        'end_time' => 'datetime',
        'satisfaction' => 'integer',
    ];

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class);
    }

    public function agent(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(AdminUser::class, 'agent_id');
    }

    public function messages(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(SupportMessage::class, 'session_id');
    }

    public function scopeActive($query)
    {
        return $query->where('status', 1);
    }

    public function markAsEnded(): void
    {
        $this->update([
            'status' => 2,
            'end_time' => now(),
        ]);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Admin\Support;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class SupportMessage extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'support_messages';

    protected $casts = [
        'sender_type' => 'integer', // 1客户 2客服 3系统
        'msg_type' => 'integer',    // 1文本 2图片 3文件 4系统通知
        'is_read' => 'boolean',
    ];

    public function session(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(SupportSession::class, 'session_id');
    }
}
```

### 6.29.3 客服会话服务

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Admin\Support;

use App\Models\Admin\Support\SupportMessage;
use App\Models\Admin\Support\SupportSession;
use App\Services\Admin\AgentAllocationService;
use Illuminate\Support\Str;

class CustomerSupportService
{
    public function __construct(
        private AgentAllocationService $agentAllocationService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 开始会话
     */
    public function startSession(int $customerId, ?int $orderId = null, string $source = 'PC'): array
    {
        // 检查是否有进行中的会话
        $existing = SupportSession::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->active()
            ->first();

        if ($existing) {
            return [
                'session_id' => $existing->session_id,
                'agent_id' => $existing->agent_id,
                'is_new' => false,
                'recent_messages' => $existing->messages()
                    ->orderByDesc('created_at')
                    ->limit(50)
                    ->get()
                    ->reverse()
                    ->values(),
            ];
        }

        // 创建新会话
        $sessionId = Str::random(32);
        $session = SupportSession::create([
            'session_id' => $sessionId,
            'customer_id' => $customerId,
            'order_id' => $orderId,
            'status' => 1,
            'source' => $source === 'PC' ? 1 : 2,
            'start_time' => now(),
        ]);

        // 自动分配客服
        $agentId = $this->agentAllocationService->allocate($customerId, $orderId);
        if ($agentId) {
            $session->update(['agent_id' => $agentId]);
            $this->sendSystemMessage($sessionId, '客服已接入，请问有什么可以帮您？');
        } else {
            $this->sendSystemMessage($sessionId, '当前客服繁忙，请稍等，正在为您排队...');
        }

        return [
            'session_id' => $sessionId,
            'agent_id' => $agentId,
            'is_new' => true,
            'recent_messages' => [],
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 发送消息
     */
    public function sendMessage(string $sessionId, int $senderId, int $senderType, array $data): SupportMessage
    {
        $session = SupportSession::where('session_id', $sessionId)->firstOrFail();

        // 权限校验
        if ($senderType === 1 && $session->customer_id !== $senderId) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('无权发送消息');
        }
        if ($senderType === 2 && $session->agent_id !== $senderId) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('无权发送消息');
        }

        $message = SupportMessage::create([
            'session_id' => $sessionId,
            'sender_type' => $senderType,
            'sender_id' => $senderId,
            'content' => $data['content'] ?? null,
            'msg_type' => $data['msg_type'] ?? 1,
            'file_url' => $data['file_url'] ?? null,
            'is_read' => false,
        ]);

        // 广播消息（WebSocket）
        broadcast(new \App\Events\SupportMessageSent($message))->toOthers();

        return $message;
    }

    /**
     * 结束会话
     */
    public function endSession(string $sessionId, int $operatorId, int $operatorType): void
    {
        $session = SupportSession::where('session_id', $sessionId)->firstOrFail();

        if ($operatorType === 1 && $session->customer_id !== $operatorId) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('无权结束会话');
        }

        $session->markAsEnded();
        $this->sendSystemMessage($sessionId, '会话已结束');
    }

    /**
     * 满意度评价
     */
    public function rateSession(string $sessionId, int $customerId, int $satisfaction, ?string $feedback = null): void
    {
        $session = SupportSession::where('session_id', $sessionId)
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->firstOrFail();

        if ($satisfaction < 1 || $satisfaction > 5) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('满意度评分范围1-5');
        }

        $session->update([
            'satisfaction' => $satisfaction,
            'feedback' => $feedback,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 获取会话历史
     */
    public function getSessionHistory(string $sessionId, int $userId, int $userType): array
    {
        $session = SupportSession::where('session_id', $sessionId)->firstOrFail();

        if ($userType === 1 && $session->customer_id !== $userId) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('无权查看');
        }

        return $session->messages()
            ->orderBy('created_at')
            ->get()
            ->toArray();
    }

    /**
     * 发送系统消息
     */
    private function sendSystemMessage(string $sessionId, string $content): void
    {
        SupportMessage::create([
            'session_id' => $sessionId,
            'sender_type' => 3, // 系统
            'content' => $content,
            'msg_type' => 4, // 系统通知
        ]);

        broadcast(new \App\Events\SupportMessageSent(
            SupportMessage::where('session_id', $sessionId)->latest()->first()
        ))->toOthers();
    }
}
```

### 6.29.4 类图

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class CustomerSupportService {
        +startSession(int, int, string): array
        +sendMessage(string, int, int, array): SupportMessage
        +endSession(string, int, int): void
        +rateSession(string, int, int, string): void
        +getSessionHistory(string, int, int): array
    }
    class SupportSession {
        +customer(): BelongsTo
        +agent(): BelongsTo
        +messages(): HasMany
        +scopeActive(query)
        +markAsEnded(): void
    }
    class SupportMessage {
        +session(): BelongsTo
    }
    class AgentAllocationService {
        +allocate(int, int): ?int
    }

    CustomerSupportService --> AgentAllocationService : allocates
    CustomerSupportService --> SupportSession : manages
    CustomerSupportService --> SupportMessage : persists
    SupportSession --> SupportMessage : has many
```

### 6.29.5 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 同客户单会话 | 进行中会话复用 | 避免重复创建会话 |
| 消息权限隔离 | sender_id 校验 | 客户/客服只能发送自己会话的消息 |
| 满意度 1-5 星 | `1 <= $satisfaction <= 5` | 超出范围拦截 |
| 系统消息自动广播 | `broadcast()->toOthers()` | 通过 WebSocket 实时推送 |
| 离线留言持久化 | `support_messages` 表 | 客服上线后可查看历史 |

---

## 6.30 客服分配服务子系统设计（AgentAllocationService）

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块十二（客服与帮助，FR-CS-006）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Admin\Support`（管理后台 — 客服子域）  
> **核心数据表**：`admin_users`、`support_sessions`

### 6.30.1 设计概述

客服分配服务负责将客户会话智能分配给在线客服。支持三种分配策略：**轮询（Round-Robin）**、**最少会话（Least Sessions）**、**技能匹配（Skill Match）**。客服状态通过 Redis 维护（在线/忙碌/离线），支持实时状态切换。

### 6.30.2 分配策略 Enum

```php
<?php

namespace App\Enums;

enum AgentAllocationStrategy: string
{
    case ROUND_ROBIN = 'round_robin';
    case LEAST_SESSIONS = 'least_sessions';
    case SKILL_MATCH = 'skill_match';

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::ROUND_ROBIN => '轮询',
            self::LEAST_SESSIONS => '最少会话',
            self::SKILL_MATCH => '技能匹配',
        };
    }
}
```

### 6.30.3 客服分配服务

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Admin;

use App\Enums\AgentAllocationStrategy;
use App\Models\Admin\AdminUser;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Redis;

class AgentAllocationService
{
    private const AGENT_STATUS_PREFIX = 'agent:status:';
    private const AGENT_SESSION_COUNT_PREFIX = 'agent:session_count:';
    private const ROUND_ROBIN_INDEX_KEY = 'agent:round_robin:index';

    public function __construct(
        private AgentAllocationStrategy $defaultStrategy = AgentAllocationStrategy::LEAST_SESSIONS,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 分配客服
     */
    public function allocate(int $customerId, ?int $orderId = null): ?int
    {
        $onlineAgents = $this->getOnlineAgents();
        if ($onlineAgents->isEmpty()) {
            return null;
        }

        return match ($this->defaultStrategy) {
            AgentAllocationStrategy::ROUND_ROBIN => $this->allocateByRoundRobin($onlineAgents),
            AgentAllocationStrategy::LEAST_SESSIONS => $this->allocateByLeastSessions($onlineAgents),
            AgentAllocationStrategy::SKILL_MATCH => $this->allocateBySkillMatch($onlineAgents, $orderId),
        };
    }

    /**
     * 轮询分配
     */
    private function allocateByRoundRobin($agents): int
    {
        $agentIds = $agents->pluck('id')->sort()->values();
        $index = (int) Redis::get(self::ROUND_ROBIN_INDEX_KEY) ?? 0;
        $selectedId = $agentIds[$index % $agentIds->count()];
        Redis::set(self::ROUND_ROBIN_INDEX_KEY, ($index + 1) % $agentIds->count());

        return $selectedId;
    }

    /**
     * 最少会话分配（默认策略）
     */
    private function allocateByLeastSessions($agents): int
    {
        $agentIds = $agents->pluck('id')->toArray();

        // 从 Redis 获取当前会话数
        $counts = array_map(
            fn (int $id) => (int) Redis::get(self::AGENT_SESSION_COUNT_PREFIX . $id) ?? 0,
            $agentIds
        );

        $pairs = array_combine($agentIds, $counts);
        asort($pairs);

        return array_key_first($pairs);
    }

    /**
     * 技能匹配分配（按订单品类匹配熟悉该品类的客服）
     */
    private function allocateBySkillMatch($agents, ?int $orderId): int
    {
        if (!$orderId) {
            return $this->allocateByLeastSessions($agents);
        }

        $order = \App\Models\Order\Order::find($orderId);
        $categoryId = $order?->cd_category_id;

        // 优先分配给有该品类技能的客服
        $skilled = $agents->filter(function ($agent) use ($categoryId) {
            $skills = json_decode($agent->skills ?? '[]', true);
            return in_array($categoryId, $skills, true);
        });

        if ($skilled->isNotEmpty()) {
            return $this->allocateByLeastSessions($skilled);
        }

        return $this->allocateByLeastSessions($agents);
    }

    /**
     * 获取在线客服列表
     */
    private function getOnlineAgents()
    {
        return AdminUser::where('role', 'customer_service')
            ->where('status', 1) // 在线
            ->where('is_busy', 0) // 非忙碌
            ->get();
    }

    /**
     * 更新客服状态
     */
    public function updateAgentStatus(int $agentId, int $status, bool $isBusy = false): void
    {
        Redis::set(self::AGENT_STATUS_PREFIX . $agentId, json_encode([
            'status' => $status, // 1在线 2离线
            'is_busy' => $isBusy,
            'updated_at' => now()->toDateTimeString(),
        ]));
    }

    /**
     * 增加/减少客服会话计数
     */
    public function incrementSessionCount(int $agentId, int $delta = 1): void
    {
        Redis::incrby(self::AGENT_SESSION_COUNT_PREFIX . $agentId, $delta);
    }
}
```

### 6.30.4 类图

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class AgentAllocationService {
        +allocate(int, int): ?int
        +updateAgentStatus(int, int, bool): void
        +incrementSessionCount(int, int): void
        -allocateByRoundRobin(Collection): int
        -allocateByLeastSessions(Collection): int
        -allocateBySkillMatch(Collection, int): int
    }
    class AgentAllocationStrategy {
        <<enumeration>>
        ROUND_ROBIN
        LEAST_SESSIONS
        SKILL_MATCH
    }

    AgentAllocationService --> AgentAllocationStrategy : uses
```

### 6.30.5 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 默认最少会话策略 | `LEAST_SESSIONS` | 负载均衡，避免个别客服过载 |
| 轮询索引持久化 | Redis `agent:round_robin:index` | 重启后状态不丢失 |
| 客服状态实时维护 | Redis Hash | 在线/忙碌/离线 |
| 技能匹配降级 | 无匹配时回退到最少会话 | 保证总有客服接待 |
| 会话计数原子更新 | `Redis::incrby` | 并发安全 |

---

## 6.31 WebSocket 配置与实时消息推送

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块十二（客服与帮助，FR-CS-001~010）、模块九（消息通知）  
> **所属领域**：`App\Domains\Common\Broadcast`（共享域 — 广播子域）  
> **技术选型**：Laravel Reverb（原生）或 Soketi（高性能替代）

### 6.31.1 设计概述

WebSocket 子系统承担实时消息推送职责，包括客服消息即时送达、订单状态变更推送、通知弹窗等。采用 **Laravel Broadcasting** 抽象层，底层可替换为 Reverb（Laravel 官方 WebSocket 服务器）或 Soketi（兼容 Pusher 协议的高性能替代方案）。

**频道设计**：
- **Presence Channel**：`support.{sessionId}` — 客服会话，支持"对方正在输入"状态
- **Private Channel**：`customer.{customerId}` — 客户专属频道，推送订单状态/通知
- **Private Channel**：`admin.notifications` — 后台运营通知

### 6.31.2 Broadcasting 事件定义

```php
<?php

namespace App\Events;

use App\Models\Admin\Support\SupportMessage;
use Illuminate\Broadcasting\Channel;
use Illuminate\Broadcasting\InteractsWithSockets;
use Illuminate\Broadcasting\PresenceChannel;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Broadcasting\ShouldBroadcast;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

class SupportMessageSent implements ShouldBroadcast
{
    use InteractsWithSockets, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(public SupportMessage $message) {}

    public function broadcastOn(): array
    {
        return [
            new PresenceChannel('support.' . $this->message->session_id),
        ];
    }

    public function broadcastAs(): string
    {
        return 'message.sent';
    }

    public function broadcastWith(): array
    {
        return [
            'id' => $this->message->id,
            'session_id' => $this->message->session_id,
            'sender_type' => $this->message->sender_type,
            'sender_name' => $this->message->sender_type === 1 ? '客户' : '客服',
            'content' => $this->message->content,
            'msg_type' => $this->message->msg_type,
            'file_url' => $this->message->file_url,
            'created_at' => $this->message->created_at->toDateTimeString(),
        ];
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Events;

use App\Models\Order\Order;
use Illuminate\Broadcasting\Channel;
use Illuminate\Broadcasting\InteractsWithSockets;
use Illuminate\Broadcasting\PrivateChannel;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Broadcasting\ShouldBroadcast;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

/**
 * 订单状态变更推送事件
 */
class OrderStatusUpdated implements ShouldBroadcast
{
    use InteractsWithSockets, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(public Order $order) {}

    public function broadcastOn(): array
    {
        return [
            new PrivateChannel('customer.' . $this->order->customer_id),
        ];
    }

    public function broadcastAs(): string
    {
        return 'order.status.updated';
    }

    public function broadcastWith(): array
    {
        return [
            'order_id' => $this->order->id,
            'order_sn' => $this->order->order_sn,
            'status' => $this->order->status->value,
            'status_name' => $this->order->status->label(),
            'out_status_name' => $this->order->out_status_name->value,
            'updated_at' => now()->toDateTimeString(),
        ];
    }
}
```

### 6.31.3 频道授权

```php
<?php

namespace App\Providers;

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Broadcast;
use Illuminate\Support\ServiceProvider;

class BroadcastServiceProvider extends ServiceProvider
{
    public function boot(): void
    {
        Broadcast::routes(['middleware' => ['auth:sanctum']]);

        // 客服会话频道：仅会话参与方可加入
        Broadcast::channel('support.{sessionId}', function ($user, string $sessionId) {
            $session = \App\Models\Admin\Support\SupportSession::where('session_id', $sessionId)->first();
            if (!$session) {
                return false;
            }

            // 客户或客服可加入
            return $user->id === $session->customer_id
                || $user->id === $session->agent_id;
        });

        // 客户私有频道：仅客户本人可订阅
        Broadcast::channel('customer.{customerId}', function ($user, int $customerId) {
            return $user->id === $customerId;
        });

        // 后台通知频道：仅运营人员可订阅
        Broadcast::channel('admin.notifications', function ($user) {
            return $user->role === 'admin' || $user->role === 'operator';
        });
    }
}
```

### 6.31.4 Reverb 配置

```php
<?php

// config/reverb.php
return [
    'default' => env('REVERB_SERVER', 'reverb'),

    'servers' => [
        'reverb' => [
            'host' => env('REVERB_SERVER_HOST', '0.0.0.0'),
            'port' => env('REVERB_SERVER_PORT', 8080),
            'hostname' => env('REVERB_HOST', 'localhost'),
            'options' => [
                'tls' => [],
            ],
            'max_request_size' => 10_000,
            'scaling' => [
                'enabled' => env('REVERB_SCALING_ENABLED', false),
                'channel' => env('REVERB_SCALING_CHANNEL', 'reverb'),
                'server' => [
                    'url' => env('REDIS_URL'),
                    'host' => env('REDIS_HOST', '127.0.0.1'),
                    'port' => env('REDIS_PORT', '6379'),
                    'username' => env('REDIS_USERNAME'),
                    'password' => env('REDIS_PASSWORD'),
                    'database' => env('REDIS_DB', '0'),
                ],
            ],
            'pulse_ingest_interval' => 15,
        ],
    ],

    'apps' => [
        'provider' => 'config',
        'apps' => [
            [
                'key' => env('REVERB_APP_KEY'),
                'secret' => env('REVERB_APP_SECRET'),
                'app_id' => env('REVERB_APP_ID'),
                'options' => [
                    'host' => env('REVERB_HOST'),
                    'port' => env('REVERB_PORT', 443),
                    'scheme' => env('REVERB_SCHEME', 'https'),
                    'useTLS' => env('REVERB_SCHEME', 'https') === 'https',
                ],
                'allowed_origins' => ['*'],
                'ping_interval' => env('REVERB_APP_PING_INTERVAL', 60),
                'activity_timeout' => env('REVERB_APP_ACTIVITY_TIMEOUT', 30),
                'max_message_size' => env('REVERB_APP_MAX_MESSAGE_SIZE', 10_000),
            ],
        ],
    ],
];
```

### 6.31.5 前端频道订阅示例

```javascript
// Vue3 中使用 Laravel Echo 订阅频道
import Echo from 'laravel-echo';
import Pusher from 'pusher-js';

window.Pusher = Pusher;

const echo = new Echo({
    broadcaster: 'reverb',
    key: import.meta.env.VITE_REVERB_APP_KEY,
    wsHost: import.meta.env.VITE_REVERB_HOST,
    wsPort: import.meta.env.VITE_REVERB_PORT ?? 80,
    wssPort: import.meta.env.VITE_REVERB_PORT ?? 443,
    forceTLS: (import.meta.env.VITE_REVERB_SCHEME ?? 'https') === 'https',
    enabledTransports: ['ws', 'wss'],
    auth: {
        headers: {
            Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('access_token')}`,
        },
    },
});

// 订阅客服会话 Presence Channel
echo.join(`support.${sessionId}`)
    .here((users) => {
        console.log('当前在线用户:', users);
    })
    .listen('.message.sent', (e) => {
        console.log('收到新消息:', e);
        messages.value.push(e);
    });

// 订阅订单状态 Private Channel
echo.private(`customer.${customerId}`)
    .listen('.order.status.updated', (e) => {
        console.log('订单状态更新:', e);
        // 触发前端弹窗或刷新订单列表
    });
```

```mermaid

    OrderStatusUpdated --> PrivateChannel : broadcasts

```

### 6.31.7 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| 客服消息实时推送 | Presence Channel `support.{sessionId}` | 双方实时收发 |
| 订单状态隔离推送 | Private Channel `customer.{customerId}` | 仅本人可见 |
| 频道权限校验 | `Broadcast::channel` 闭包 | 防止越权订阅 |
| 支持 Reverb/Soketi | Laravel Broadcasting 抽象层 | 可替换底层实现 |
| 心跳保活 | `ping_interval: 60` | 维持长连接 |

## 6.32-S ~ 6.35-S 已在前文详述子系统的 Service 层接口定义（简要补充）

> 以下子系统已在第 6 章上半部分（Part D / `ch04_core_business_part1.md`）详细设计，本节仅补充 PHP 接口定义与 Action 类签名，保持全文档接口一致性。

### 6.32-S 订单统计服务（OrderStatisticsService）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Order;

interface OrderStatisticsInterface
{
    /**
     * 客户订单状态分类统计（含待付定金细分、不可退款/已锁定汇总）
     * FR-ORDER-009 ~ FR-ORDER-010
     */
    public function getCustomerStatusCount(int $customerId): CustomerOrderStatusCountDTO;

    /**
     * 近6个月订单统计
     * FR-ORDER-045
     */
    public function getCustomerLastSixMonthStatistic(int $customerId): array;

    /**
     * 客户整体订单统计（总订单数、总金额、完成率）
     */
    public function getCustomerOverallStatistics(int $customerId): CustomerOrderStatisticsDTO;
}

/**
 * Action：刷新客户订单统计缓存
 */
class RefreshCustomerOrderStatisticsAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId): void;
}
```

### 6.33-S 热销榜与飙升榜服务（BestsellerRankService）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Product;

interface BestsellerRankInterface
{
    /**
     * 获取热销榜
     * 数据来源：Redis Sorted Set（每日定时刷新）
     */
    public function getBestsellerRank(?int $categoryId = null, int $limit = 10): array;

    /**
     * 获取飙升榜（增速排序）
     */
    public function getSoaringRank(?int $categoryId = null, int $limit = 10): array;
}

/**
 * Action：同步热销榜数据至 Redis
 * 由 Schedule 每日 02:00 触发
 */
class SyncBestsellerRankAction
{
    public function execute(): void;
}
```

### 6.34-S 样品订单服务（SampleOrderService）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Order;

interface SampleOrderInterface
{
    /**
     * 创建样品订单（简化流程，独立状态机）
     * FR-SAMPLE-008
     */
    public function createSampleOrder(int $customerId, array $items, ?int $couponId = null): Order;

    /**
     * 获取样品折扣率（基于 VIP 等级）
     * FR-SAMPLE-005
     */
    public function getSampleDiscountRate(int $vipLevel): float;
}

/**
 * Action：创建样品订单
 * 状态流：100待付款 → 101已付款 → 102待发货 → 103已发货 → 104已完成
 */
class CreateSampleOrderAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId, array $data): Order;
}
```

### 6.35-S 成长值服务（GrowthValueService）

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Vip;

interface GrowthValueInterface
{
    /**
     * 获取成长值明细
     * FR-POINT-014
     */
    public function getRecords(int $customerId, ?int $changeType = null, int $page = 1, int $perPage = 20): array;

    /**
     * 获取成长值汇总（当前等级、距离下一级差值、进度百分比）
     * FR-POINT-012
     */
    public function getSummary(int $customerId): GrowthValueSummaryDTO;

    /**
     * 发放成长值（订单完成/评价/签到等场景调用）
     */
    public function grant(int $customerId, int $changeValue, int $changeType, ?int $sourceId = null, ?string $sourceType = null, ?string $remark = null): void;
}

/**
 * Action：发放订单评价成长值
 */
class GrantCommentGrowthValueAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId, int $commentId, int $baseValue = 50): void;
}

/**
 * Action：发放订单消费成长值
 */
class GrantOrderGrowthValueAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId, float $orderAmount): void;
}
```

| `invoices` | 6.22 发票 | `status`, `business_type`, `amount` | Enum 驱动状态机 |
| `invoice_red_records` | 6.22 发票 | `original_invoice_id`, `red_type`, `reason` | 红冲记录 |
| `inventory_lock_logs` | 6.23 库存 | `sku_id`, `order_id`, `quantity`, `status` | 锁定审计 |
| `login_logs` | 6.24 认证 | `ip_address`, `device_name`, `login_at` | 异步写入 |
| `favorites` | 6.25 收藏 | `customer_id`, `product_id`, `cp_summary` | 规格级收藏 |
| `favorite_folders` | 6.25 收藏 | `customer_id`, `name`, `sort_order` | 收藏夹分类 |
| `favorite_orders` | 6.25 收藏 | `customer_id`, `order_id`, `lose_efficacy` | 常用订单 |
| `sub_accounts` | 6.26 子账号 | `sub_permission`, `active`, `customer_id` | 位掩码权限 |
| `customer_addresses` | 6.27 地址 | `link_person`, `mobile_phone`, `detail_address` | 加密存储 |
| `customer_brands` | 6.27 品牌 | `status(vM)`, `type(gM)`, `trademark_type` | 资质审核 |
| `invoice_titles` | 6.28 抬头 | `title_type`, `tax_number`, `is_default` | 税号正则校验 |
| `support_sessions` | 6.29 客服 | `session_id`, `agent_id`, `status`, `satisfaction` | 会话管理 |
| `support_messages` | 6.29 客服 | `sender_type`, `msg_type`, `is_read` | 消息持久化 |
| `admin_users` | 6.30 分配 | `role`, `status`, `skills`, `is_busy` | 客服状态 |

## 自检清单

- [x] 所有代码示例为 PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13 语法风格
- [x] 未出现 Java 特有概念（ServiceImpl / DAO / Mapper / CompletableFuture / 线程池 / XXL-JOB 等）
- [x] 发票状态机使用 PHP Backed Enum（`InvoiceStatus`）实现，含 `canTransitionTo()` 方法
- [x] 库存锁定使用 Redis Lua 原子操作（`DECRBY` / `INCRBY`）
- [x] 子账号权限使用位掩码 + Laravel Gate/Policy + Middleware
- [x] 敏感数据（手机号、姓名、地址）使用 Laravel Encrypter 加密存储
- [x] 认证使用 Laravel Sanctum，支持 Token 对（Access + Refresh）和多设备共存
- [x] 客服系统使用 Laravel Broadcasting + Presence/Private Channel
- [x] 数据模型关联使用 Eloquent 原生（belongsToMany / HasMany / BelongsTo / Global Scope）
- [x] 异步处理使用 Laravel Queue Job（埋点、登录日志、库存释放）
- [x] 状态变更通知使用 Eloquent Observer + Laravel Notification
- [x] 已在前文详述的服务（6.32~6.35）仅补充接口定义，未重复展开

---
